bya zhing / phyi nas bla ma dam pa rnams kyis rigs kyi bu rnams la dgag par bya'o/ /dge slong rnams la ni dbang bskur ba'i dus su yang sbyin par mi bya ste/ chos gos 'dzin
pa rnams la bla mas rang gi tshig gi thams cad rab tu bstan par bya'o/ /rnam pa gzhan du na bla ma dam tshig las nyams par 'gyur ro/ /zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /des na
sbyang rtogs sbar gsum dngos su nus kyang rab tu byung ba'i cha lugs 'dzin pas de lta bu dngos su byas na rang nyid la nyes par mi 'gyur yang / thub pa'i bstan pa la gnod
pa'i phyir dngos su mi mdzad pa yin no/ /de ltar na dbang dus su bza' ba'i dam tshig tu gsungs pa de dag nyams par 'gyur ba ma yin nam snyam na/ dus khyad par can gyi tshe
ni mkhyen rab dbang phyug gis ji skad bshad pa ltar rjes mthun pa'i tshul gyis nyams su blangs pas chog la/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig tu ni cho ga bzhin du bsgrub
pa'i bdud rtsi ril bu ji tsam 'byor pa bsten pas dag bya de legs par khegs pa yin te/ 'grel chen de nyid las/ rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa lnga'i ril bu yungs kar gyi
tshad tsam nyi ma so sor dam tshig bsten pa'i don du'o zhes gsungs pas so/ /gsum pa ni/ spyir rdo rje theg pa'i gzhung las bshad pa'i mchod pa'i yo byad dang / tshogs kyi
rdzas dang rdzogs rim bsgom pa'i tshe/ lus dub pa gso ba'i phyir du gsungs pa'i sha ni kha na ma tho

ba med pa'i sha kho na yin pas khyab ste/ bde mchog stod 'grel las/ da ni 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub bsgrub pa'i phyir pho nya mo'i kun tu spyod pa dang / 'khor lo 'dus pa la
bdud rtsi ril bu dang / g.yul du mtshon gyis bsad pa kha na ma tho ba dang bral ba'am/ nad kyis shi ba'am/ las ngan pas bsad pa yang ste/ go ku da ha na la sogs pa rnams
dang / nye bar spyod pa lnga la sogs pa rnams kyis pho nya mo rnams mchod pa'i cho ga phyi rol dang nang du gsungs te/ khyad par dus la zhes pa la sogs pas so zhes dang
/ yang dus 'khor 'grel chen las/ rgyu gang gis phyir mtshan ma dang kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pas srog gcod par gyur pa rgyud de'i phyir rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi mtshan
ma med pa dang / kha na ma tho ba med pa go ku la sogs pa bza' bar bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so/ /'dir yul gang na 'jig rten pa rnams kyis gang bza' ba ma yin pa dang /
gang btsong ba ma yin pa go ku la sogs pa rang gi las kyis shi ba dang / g.yul du las ngan pa'am/ rang gi skyon gyis chom rkun la sogs pas bsad pa de rnams rnal 'byor pas
bza' bar de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs so/ /rdzas kyi nyos pa ni ma yin zhing pha mes la sogs pa dang mchod sbyin la sogs pa'i bya ba la bsad pa yang ma yin te/ mtshan ma dang
bcas pa'i sha bza'o zhes pa ni de bzhin gshegs pas ma gsungs so/ /zhes dang / gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud las/ sha chen dam tshig mchog gi ni/ zhes sogs kyis 'grel chen sgron
gsal las/ sha chen zhes bya ba la

sogs pa gsungs te/ che ba ni mi ste/ de rnams kyi sha ni shi ba'i ro las byung bas na dam tshig mchog ste/ des gtor ma byin la/ rdo rje gsum mchog ces bya ba rang gi lus bsgrub
par byas na nam mkha' la gnas pa thob par 'gyur ro zhes sogs rgya cher bshad nas/ don bsdu ba na kha na ma thob ba med pa'i sha med na cho ga bya ba bstan par bya ba'i
phyir sha rnams thams cad ces bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/ de ltar bshad pa'i sha rnams ma rnyed na bsgoms pas sha rnams bskyed par bya'o/ /yang na bag phye la sogs pa
la mi ro la sogs pa byas la/ de'i rang gi gzugs las srog dang bral bar bsam nas/ de'i man ngag gis bsgrub par bya'o/ /rdo rje sbyor ba ste mi bshig pa'i kha zas kyi cho
ga bshad ma thag pa 'di byas na sgrub pa po la sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis rlobs par mdzad cing / mngon par 'dod pa'i don gyi dngos grub thob par 'gyur ro/ /zhes
bya ba la sogs pa rgyud dang gzhung 'grel tshad ldan rnams las shin tu mang bar gsungs so/ /des na sa bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa' padma dkar po dang / phyag na rdo rje
la sogs pas chos shin tu gsal bar bshad pa 'di dag rgyang ring du bor nas/ ltar snang ba'i lung dang rig pas phyin ci log gi grub pa'i mtha' 'dzugs pa ni/ 'dod sred can
gyi gdon gyis zin pa'am/ shes pa rang bzhin du mi gnas pa'am/ mngon sum la smyon pa kho na yin par gor ma chags so/ /de bzhin du dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mchod pa dang / rnal
'byor pa rnams kyis bsten byar gsungs pa'i chang yang rgyud sdom pa 'byung ba nas ji

ltar bshad pa ltar/ gtso bo'i cho ga tshul bzhin du byas pa'i bur chang ngam/ nas la sogs pa rgyud sde nas bshad pa dgos pa yin gyi/ ci yang rung ba'i chang gis tshogs rdzas
byed pa bshad pa med do/ /de ltar bshad pa'i sha dang chang rnams kyang dpa' bo'i ston mo la sogs pa'i tshe lha'i rnal 'byor brtan po dang ldan pas cung zad kha tshim pa
tsam bsten pa yin gyi/ ha cang rgyas pa dang ting nge 'dzin brtan po dang mi ldan pa'i las dang po pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa dag gis cho ga tsam shes pa'i gtan tshigs kyis ci
dgar 'jug pa dang / 'dzag bde don gnyer gyi blos phyag rgya bsten pa rnams bkag pa yin te/ dus 'khor las/ phyag rgya bsgom pa'i don du gsungs te nyin mtshan dus su chags
pa zad pa'i don ni min pa nyid gsung gi rdo rje mchod pa'i don te/ nges par sngags pa rnams la myos byed gsungs pa nyid ma yin/ zhes dang / de'i 'grel par/ da ni phyag
rgya zhes pa la sogs pas rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi phyag rgya dang / myang ba dang / kha zas dang / rgyu ba'i nges pa gsungs te/ 'dir bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag rgya gsungs pa
ni/ bsgom pa'i don du rnal 'byor gyi phyag rgya gsungs pa ste/ chags pa zad pa'i don ste/ rgyur nyin mtshan du bud med dang rol bar gsungs pa ni ma yin no/ /de bzhin du
chang btung ba ni cung zad kha tshim par byed pa ste/ bum pa la sogs pa bzhin du ma yin te/ myos byed ni rnal 'byor gyi dbang po rnams la thar pa ster bar byed par mi 'gyur
ro/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de bzhin du slob dpon chen po dznyA na kirtis/ gang

yang 'di skad du bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor ba'i chos kyi don mi shes par dam tshig dang sdom pa la sogs pa thos pa tsam la brten te/ dge ba la lhod pa 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi/
sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi kho bo rnal 'byor pa rnams la rjes su gnang ba yin no zhes sgra sangs mthon por sgrogs shing chags pa la sogs pa'i dbang du gyur pa'i sems
kyi rgyud kyis mi dge ba rnams kyang byed pa de rnams ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la skur pa btab cing bslus pas shin tu dam tshig nyams pa'i phyir mnar med pa nyid du
ltung bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /de bas na gnas skabs su bya ba'i khyad par 'di la bsnyad btags te bag med par spyod pa dag ni/ lhag spyod kyi ting nge 'dzin
bsgom pa'i rnam par thar pa dang kun tu mtshungs pa'o/ /smras pa/ yang dag mgon gyis ma gzigs pas/ /rnam dag dam pa'i tshul dor nas/ /ma dag 'tsho ba don gnyer ba/ /mtha'
dag tshogs kyi lan yod min/ /mjug gi chos ltar bcos nas chos min byed/ zhes sogs tshigs su bcad pa gcig la rgyas bshad mi 'dug kyang / de'i lan ni/ rgyal ba nyid kyis
legs par btab pa yin te/ 'phags pa dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bzung ba zhes bya ba'i mdo las/ kho bo cag gi rje thams cad mkhyen pa 'di lung bstan pa'i mjug tu/ gang dag
phyi dus dge slong rnams 'byung ba/ /rtsub dang gtum dang shin tu rtsub pa yi/ /dge slong gzhan gyis 'di la rtsod par 'gyur/ /chos 'di rgyal bas gsungs pa ma yin zhes/ /'jig
rten phyin ci log la kun dga' bltos/ /zhes dge

slong lta ba dang tshul khrims log par spyod pa rnams kyis lung rigs ltar snang gi sgo nas rtsod pa dag 'byung bar lung bstan pa'i thog tu babs pas 'di lta bu smra ba dag rje
thams cad mkhyen pa 'di la lhag par gus pa'i rgyur dpyod ldan rnams kyis nges par bya'o/ /'on kyang ding sang bstan pa'i snyigs ma ches lhag par gyur pas smin grol gyi
lam ston nus par khas 'che ba phal cher zhig yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi bslab par bya ba tsam la yang 'khu 'khrig za ba shas che bar snang bas tshig 'di rang gzhan kun
la gzu bor gnas pa'i blos brtags te smras pa yin na/ rtsod phreng 'di'i nang na 'di nyid kho na legs par byas pa yin no/ /smras pa/ chos tshul 'di la sbyangs sbyangs pa'i/
/bstan 'dzin gzhan la smod smod pa/ /de dag rnams kyis rang rang gi /smra bya'i gnas la nges nges kyi/ /bsgrub byed don du mna' bor bas/ /rang gzhung zin par khas 'che
ba'i/ /thos chung rnams kyis rang gis rang / /lha rnams dga' ba'i grangs su byas/ /gsar chung yid srub rigs kyi tshig /thun tshags bsdus pa'i smod pa'i mda'/ /phyogs 'dir
'phen brtson sred ldan de/ /'dod pa'i khyim du gnyid byos shig /ces smra'o/ /a ho badzra dznyA/ phyogs kun 'phrin las zer gyis 'gebs nus pa'i/ /'od gsal nyi zla'i snang
ba 'di med na/ /tshur rol mthong ba'i srin bu me khyer gyis/ /sa gsum snang byed dbang po bya nus sam/ /sngon dus rtog ge'i chang gis rab myos pa'i/ /phyir rgol glang po
smyon pa'i dor stabs kyis/ /gsung ngag mtsho skyes rtsa

ba dkrugs pa'i tshe/ /nyes spong lung rigs shes pa 'ga' yod dam/ /deng dus mkhas mang ngang pa'i ded dpon dang / /gzhan zer dbyangs su len pa'i bung ba yang / /chos 'di'i mkha'
la 'dab bzang ji bzhin du/ /'phur lding byed 'di mgon de'i drin min nam/ /gong ma'i bzhed gzhung ming gi mthar byed cing / /lam bzang bsgom la 'gyod tshang gzhung 'dzugs
pa'i/ /'byung po'i rigs la phebs par smra byed cing / /rang sde smod rnams gdon gyis ma btab bam/ rgyal po'i 'phrin dang g.yo sgyu'i sbyor ba yis/ /'bad pas bsgrub pa'i
dad pa'i rjes 'brang gis/ /sgra 'dzin dbang po gzhan smod ngur mo yis/ /rgyun du rtser la bsam sbyor gzhan med dam/ /chos brgyad 'khor dang khyim la 'khron pa yi/ /kun
dkris dbang gis dgag bsgrub zol sbyor mkhan/ /lus med 'dod pa'i bde ba bsgrub rnams la/ /nyung ngu'i tshig gis lan 'di rig par smras/ /gsung rab rgya mtsho'i don la ma
phyogs par/ /lan brgyar 'chad dang nyan pa'i grar zhugs kyang / /tshig tsam 'don pa'i ngal bas dus 'da' ba'i/ /blun po rnams kyis smad par ma gyur cig /'di sbyar dge bas
gsung ngag yid bzhin nor/ /sems 'jal rtog pa'i byi dor gyis sbyangs te/ /thos bsam bsgom pa'i rgyal mtshan rtser bzhag nas/ /blo gsal mang po'i mdun sar bsngags par shog
/'gro gsum mchod 'os thub bstan ganggA'i rgyun/ /nyes bshad 'phrog byed rkang pas ma bcos pa/ /bdag blo skal ldan shing rta la brten nas/ /srid mthar 'gro ba'i gdung ba sel
bar shog /tshe rab kun du dal

'byor gru bo che/ /'phags nor rin chen bdun ldan legs thob ste/ /'phrin las ba dan dkar po'i thabs mkhas kyis/ /rnam grol sku bzhi'i gling du bgrod par shog /ces gsung ngag
rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdam ngag gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba'i lam gyi sgo nas mtha' yas pa'i 'gro ba rnams 'chi ba med pa'i gnas su 'dren par byed pa'i
phyag len gyi rim pa'i cha shas phyogs re ba gang yin pa de dag la bshes gnyen gzhan gyis brgal zhing brtags pa'i lan rnam par nges pa tshangs pa'i rigs sngags zhes bya
ba 'di ni/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po yongs 'dzin ratna wardha yab sras kyi gsung ngag bdud rtsis skal ba bzang por byas pa shAkya'i dge slong dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
'phags pa'i yul na bi ro dhi zhes grags pa sa mo glang gi lo/ de bzhin gshegs pas bdud dang mu stegs pham par mdzad pa'i dus chen cho 'phrul gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs bsil
zer byed pa'i dkyil 'khor lang tsho rab tu rgyas pa'i nyin/ shrI e wa~M chos ldan yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas kyi gtsug lag khang chen po'i yang steng du legs
par sbyar ba'o/ /yi ge'i 'du byed mnga' ris yul ljongs kyi/ /thig ler rab skyes brtul zhugs mchog 'dzin cing / /mang thos nor 'chang nam mkha' brtan pa yi/ /sor mo'i
pad dkar bzhad pa'i ze'u 'bru 'o/ /'dis gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas pa'i rgyur gyur cig shu bhaM mastu sarba dza ga taM/ zhes pa
de rnams kyis brgal lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags nyid

bshad pa bstan zin nas/ gnyis pa de'i don bsdus bshad pa ni/ brgal lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi don bsdus don brgyad pa zhes bya ba las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ brgal zhing
brtags pa'i lan rnam par nges pa tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi don bsdus pa'i tshigs su bcad pa/ rje btsun dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /stobs ldan mda' lnga'i 'jug pas
ma bsgrin zhing / /dregs ldan lha brgya'i gtsug tu ngal gso mdzad/ /byams ldan bdud rtsi'i 'tsho ba la dges pa'i/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i bla chen phyag gi gnas/ /gangs can
ljongs 'dir kun mkhyen gnyis pa zhes/ /rab grags rgyal bas lung bstan 'khor lo'i mgon/ /mkhas kun dga' ba'i mdzad pa bzang po yis/ /ston pa'i rgyal sa 'dzin khyod bsngags
par 'os/ /gang de'i 'phrin las rnyog bral 'o ma'i mtsho/ /dpyod ldan mang po'i bsten byar rnam brtags pa/ /phyogs 'dzin mun pa'i khung bur nyal byed pa'i/ /blo chung
brang 'gro'i tshogs kyis spangs so lo/ /rmad byung brgyud pa'i bzhed gzhung dbang gi rgyal/ /sgros na dbugs kyi dug can gyis 'khyud na/ /'phrin las 'od zer 'phro bar mi nus
pas/ /lung rigs sngags 'di gzhan zer ring du bya/ /chags sdang dug mtsho bsrub pa las byung ba'i/ /tshig rtsub nag po brtsegs pa'i kha dog tsam/ /blo ngan mgrin pa'i rgyan
du re ba dag /khong khro'i mig me 'bar bar ma gyur cig /'di na sa skya'i chos lugs kyi/ /rjes su dad pas 'brangs ba 'ga'/ /phrag dog phyogs 'dzin lhur byas nas/ /rang
gzhan 'byed phyir 'di skad lo/ /sems bskyed brgyud pa med

pa dang / /rjes bzung grangs nges med pa dang / /sta gon 'grel pa med pa dang / /slob dpon grangs nges med pa dang / /dbang bskur yongs dag med pa dang / /lus dkyil 'byung
khung med pa dang / /rgyas gdab rigs mtshon med pa dang / /bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa rnams/ /chos ltar bcos na chos min byed/ /smin par 'dod kyang 'dis mi smin/ /grol bar
'dod kyang grol mi nus/ /nor pa'i chos rnams dgag par bya/ /  ces sogs rgyas bshad dang bcas nas/ /smra po nyid kyis legs byas ltar/ /mtshan ma ngan pa mtshon pa'i tshig
/du ma phreng du dngar bar byed/ blun po rnams kyis gang dran gyis/ /zab mo'i gnas la co 'dri ba/ /'di 'dra 'phel na bstan pa la/ /gnod phyir mkhas pa sun dbyung 'os/ /de
phyir kho bos rnam dpyod kyis/ /rgyas par logs su bkag zin mod/ /slar yang de don rtogs sla'i phyir/ /nyung zhing gsal bar 'dir 'chad do/ /de la rgol ba dang po ni/ spyir
dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed 'di lam 'bras brgyud pa la med/ khyad par du rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i sems bskyed kyi yi ge ngor chen pas sgo rum nas brnyed zer ba de'i
steng nas sems bskyed byed pa ni brgyud pa chad pa ni tshig de nyid kyi shes shing / yi ge de'i steng nas sus kyang byas pa med zhes lam 'bras pa phyi ma rnams kyi brgyud
pa grangs 'dren par byed do/ /zhes smra'o/ /de'i lan ni/ rje btsun mched kyi dbang chu dang / /mngon par rtogs pa ljon shing las/ /dbang bskur sngon du skyabs 'gro dang
/ /sems bskyed sdom pa 'bogs so zhes/ /gsungs pa de la lag len zhig /sa skya'i chos na yod dam med/ /yod na de yi brgyud pa gang / /med na khungs nas med pa 'am/ /gsar
du chad pa gang yin brtag /dang po ltar na sku mched kyis/

/de ltar bshad pa ming tsam las/ /nyams len rim par ma byung phyir/ /byang chub sems mchog ma bskyed la/ /gsang sngags bstan na phung ngo zhes/ /rdo rje 'chang gis bkag pa
de/ /rje btsun gong ma bsgrub mdzad dam/ /phyi ma ltar na dbang yod kyang / /sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed 'chad do zhes/ /chos dang mthun par smra nus sam/ /rang la khyab pa
bsgrub byas nas/ /phyogs chos gzhan la sbyor ram ci/ /gang ltar byas kyang byang chub sems/ /ma bskyed pa la dbang bskur ba'i/ /nyes pa khyed kyi thog tu babs/ /byed na de
yi brgyud pa ci/ /brgyud pa med pa'i sems bskyed cig /mi 'dod bzhin du khas len nam/ /thun mong min pa'i skyabs 'gro dang / /sems bskyed cho ga byed pa la/ /dbu ma'i lugs
kyi sems bskyed pa/ /lam 'bras pa la med do zhes/ /rnam par dpyod la 'brel ci zhig /kun dang thun mong min pa'i chos/ /tshad ldan brgyud pa gnyis ldan la/ /sems bskyed
brgyud pa med pa zhes/ /smod par byed pa'i smra ba'i lam/ /'dod lha'i bdag po'i phye bar zad/ /phyogs zhen dri la chags pa yis/ /gnas don pad tshal ma brnyed pa'i/ /'khos
med sbrang bu'i gshog rgyang gis/ /nyi zla sgrib par 'dod pa mtshar/ /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa ste don tshan dang po'o/ /rgol ba gnyis pa la ni/ slob
ma brgya phrag mang po la grangs nges med par rjes 'dzin gyi cho ga byed pa ni/ gsang ba spyi rgyud las/ mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ zhes sogs kyi lung dang 'gal/
dbang gi chu bo las/ dkyil 'khor gcig tu slob ma nyi shu rtsa lnga las lhag pa bzung bar mi bya zhes sogs gong ma'i gzhung dang 'gal/ rjes bzung

grangs nges med na sta gon dang 'gal la/ yod pa'i khas len dang 'gal te/ sta gon gyi grangs nges rjes bzung gi grangs nges la ltos/ dbang dus kyi grangs nges sta gon gyi grangs
nges la ltos par spyir rgyud las gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /zhes smra ba'o/ /de'i lan ni/ rjes bzung skabs kyi slob ma la/ /grangs nges med pa mi rung na/ /chos kyi rgyal
po 'phags pa yi/ /brtag gnyis TIkka gser sgam mar/ /grangs nges med la rjes 'dzin gyi/ /cho ga byed pa gsal bar bshad/ /de dag khyod kyis ma mthong bar/ /thag chod byed
pa rigs pa 'am/ /gzhan la smra ba'i zol sbyor gyis/ /'phags pa 'gegs la brtson par zad/ /'phags pa 'gegs pa'i sa skya pa/ /rnying pa'i rjes 'brang de ngo mtshar/ /spyi rgyud
nyid na grangs nges kyi/ /lung de sta gon skabs na yod/ /de phyir dbang chu'i dngos bstan ni/ /dbang bskur tshar gcig nyid la dgongs/ /gnyis dang gsum sogs 'ga' yod
na/ /rjes 'dzin 'phral nas bya mi dgos/ /dgos na 'phags pas bshad pa de/ /slob ma dbang bskur grangs med la/ /byed du rung ba'i lung nyid du/ /thal ba khyod kyis bzlog mi
nus/ /'phags pa dngos su 'gegs bzhin du/ /'phags pa bsgrub pa'i khengs pa can/ /khyod kyis gang dang gang smras pa/ /thams cad de dang de 'drar zad/ /stobs ldan rmongs pa'i
dregs pa yis/ /'phrog byed brnyas pa'i le lan gyis/ /sa gsum shor nas rang nyid kyang / /dam du bcing ba thob par 'gyur/ /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad
pa ste don tshan gnyis pa'o/ /rgol ba gsum pa ni/ slob ma smin byed kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor

gcig tu thog ma'i dbang bskur tshar gcig po de rigs mod/ de'i rjes su dkyil 'khor gcig nyid kyi steng nas nyin re bzhin sta gon snga ma'i dngos gzhi re dang dngos gzhi rting
ma'i sta gon re spel nas zhu mkhan ma rdzogs kyi bar du byed do/ /'di shin tu mi rigs pa'i rgyu mtshan smin byed rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang bskur tshar gcig
las lhag pa bskur du mi rung ste/ dkyil 'khor de la sta gon gcig las med pa'i phyir/ zhes sa skya pa'i srol 'dzin gzhan thams cad 'chad la/ khyed kyi de lta bu la gong
ma'i lung yod na ston cig /gal te sta gon gsum po sngar byas pa des chog go zhe na/ 'o na sgrub mchod sogs kyang sngar byas pa de nyid kyi gnas pas nyi ma gzhan byed ci
dgos/ gal te sta gon snga ma rnams bskyar nas byed dgos so zhe na/ dkyil 'khor bsgrubs zin nas de'i lha sta gon ji ltar byed ces smra'o/ /de'i lan ni/ sta gon gcig la dngos
gzhi 'ga'/ /sbrel nas byed pa sa skya pa'i/ /chos na med phyir 'brel med ces/ /smra ba de la blun pa ste/ /de ltar yin na rje rtse mos/ /mdzad pa'i Dombhi dkyil chog las/
/sgrub mchod nyi ma lngar byas nas/ /sta gon gcig la dngos gzhi gnyis/ /mdzad pa'i dngos gzhi dang po la/ /rab gnas dang ni gnyis pa la/ /slob ma dbang bskur byed do
zhes/ /gsal bar gsungs pa ma shes par/ /gong ma'i chos rnams 'gags par zad/ /rtse mo 'gag pa'i sa skya pa'i/ /rjes 'brang rnying pa gang nas byon/ /rje btsun chen po'i dus
tha ma'i/ /sta gon gcig la dngos gzhi drug /byed par bshad pa'i phyi ma lnga/ /'brel med yin phyir mi rung bar/ /rjes 'brang za shal khyed 'dod dam/ /rje btsun 'gag pa'i
sa skya pa/ /rnying pa de 'dra gad mo'i gnas/ /dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang bskur ba/ /gcig las nam yang mi rung na/ /ras bris

bzhengs pa don re chung / /sta gon bskyar nas rung zhes na/ /dkyil 'khor bsgrub nas sta gon ni/ /ji ltar byed ces khyed nyid kyis/ /gzhan la smras pa de brjod dam/ /slob dpon
lus kyi dkyil 'khor ni/ /gcig las med phyir lus dkyil du/ /dbang bskur slob dpon tshe gang la/ /gcig las byed du mi rung bar/ /gzhung bshad mkhas rlom khyed 'dod dam/
/de ltar na ni lam 'bras kyang / /tshar gcig nyid las mi rung bar/ /thal ba 'di la 'dod lan thob/ /mdor na 'di 'dra'i grub mtha' ni/ /mthong ba brgyud pa'i phyag len gyis/
/brgyan pa'i slob dpon ma bsten par/ /dkyil chog rnams kyi tshig rigs la/ /thug 'phrad byas pa'i gtam du snang / /mi mkhas rnams kyis rang nyid kyi/ /gtam ngan ngo sor
byed pa mang / /rgyal ngan 'ga' zhig pha bsad nas/ /rgyal rnga brdung ba ji bzhin no/ /zhes bya ba 'di ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa ste don tshan gsum pa'o/ /rgol ba
bzhi pa ni/ gzhan dag rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang bskur byed pa'i tshe grangs dang nges bzung med par sta gon dus gyi nyer lnga po thams cad la dus cig car du dbang bskur
ba ni sa skya pa'i lugs ma yin te/ slob dpon rin po che'i 'grel pa lugs kyi dbang chu dang man ngag lugs kyi dbang chu gnyis ka las nyer lnga po thams cad la slob dpon
gyi dbang cig car du bskur ba bkag pa'i phyir te/ ji skad du/ slob dpon snying rje chen po yis/ /slob ma dam pa snying rje can/ /sngags dang rgyud rnams 'dzin pa po/ /gcig
ni nan tan bskyed nas bzung / /zhes pa'i lung gi tshogs pa thams cad la dbang bskur bar mi bya ste/ slob ma'i gtso bor gyur pa dbang stegs la bzhag ste zhes dang / yang
dbang bskur nas bkra shis brjod zin pa'i 'og tu thams cad bkug

nas de kho na nyid bstan par bya'o zhes gsungs pa'i phyir/ rje btsun gong mas bkag pa de nyid nan gyis bsgrub par ma byed cig ces rgol lo/ /de'i lan ni/ rdo rje slob dpon dbang
bskur gyi/ /slob ma grangs nges bya dgos pa/ /gsang ba spyi rgyud la thug na/ /gsang ba spyi rgyud bya rgyud yin/ /bya rgyud rnams las slob dpon dang / /slob ma'i dbang
gi zlas phye ba'i/ /rdo rje slob dpon dbang bskur gyi/ /don dang tha snyad gnyis ka med/ /khyad gzhi med pa'i khyad chos mtshar/ /rje btsun gong mas de drangs pa/ /rung
mthun lung du drangs pa yin/ /dper na rtsa ltung bcu bzhi yi/ /lung sbyor mdo nas mdzad pa bzhin/ /rung mthun lung dang bshad pa'i khungs/ /nor ba shin tu bzhad gad che/
/spyi rgyud dgongs pa chos dbyings ltar/ /zab cing shin tu rtogs dka' ba/ /tshig tsam 'don pa lhur byed pa/ /khyed kyi re zhig rtogs mi nus/ /shes par 'dod na mkhas pa
bsten/ /nges bzung can gyi bskur tshul de/ /byed na dbang gong dngos gzhi yang / /de lta'i tshul gyis bskur dgos par/ /skabs 'dir gong ma bzhed gyur na/ /khyed la tshul
de yod min pas/ /ngal ba'i 'bras med glang chen khrus/ /gzhan du mchog dbang rnam pa gsum/ /slob ma'i dbang du khas longs shig /gzhan gzhung tshangs pa'i gzhal med khang
/ /byis blo'i gzong gis brkos pa las/ /rang lugs bye ma'i khang bu yi/ /tshul ngan dmangs nas zhig min nam/ /zhes bya ba 'di ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa ste don tshan
bzhi pa'o/ /rgol ba lnga pa ni/ gzhan dag rdo rje'i brtul zhugs dang rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la bskyed chog mi 'dod pa ni mi

'thad de/ rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i lam dus kyi dbang yi ge las thun mong gi dbang drug rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang dang bdun ka'i bdag dang dbang rdzas yongs su dag pa bzhis
byin gyis rlobs dgos te/ de yang rgyu dus dang mi 'dra ba ni dam tshig pa pho brang lnga'i gtso bor 'pho/ gzhan rnams rgyu dus dang 'dra'o zhes gsungs pa dang dngos su
'gal lo zhes smra'o/ /de'i lan ni/ brtul zhugs slob dpon dbang bskur gyi/ /dbang rdzas yongs dag bsdus pa yis/ /nam yang bskyed du mi rung ba'i/ /gong ma'i lung khungs ci
zhig yod/ /khyed dag yongs dag ci ltar byed/ /rje btsun gong mas ma bshad kyang / /cho ga gsum bskyed sogs sbyor na/ /mngon byang lnga las bskyed rung zhes/ /bshad na khyed
cag ci zhig smra/ /khyed kyis tshad mar khas blangs pa'i/ /rdo rje dril bu'i de nyid las/ /bshad pa'i lha yi bskyed tshul dang / /dbang chu nas bshad lha de dag /shar
nub ri bzhin ring du gyur/ /de gnyis 'gal spong ci ltar byed/ /khyed kyi bla mas mdzad pa yi/ /dkyil chog dpag bsam ljon shing las/ /bshad pa'i rdor dril bskyed chog dang
/ /rje btsun rtse mo'i dbang chu gnyis/ /snang mun bzhin du 'gal bar 'gyur/ /bka' srol gnyis la de mi rung / /gal te de ltar byar rung bar/ /bshad pa'i gong ma'i lung
yod na/ /kho bo khyed kyi rjes su 'brang / /de phyir ston pa'i dus la babs/ /tshul 'di bsgrub pa bzhi ldan gyi/ /lan du lung rigs dang bcas 'chad/ /thos nyung thos don mi
shes par/ /khungs min khungs su re ba yi/ /blo chung blo ngan nor 'chang ba/ /khyod min khyod 'dra shin tu mang / /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su

bcad pa ste don tshan lnga pa'o/ /rgol ba drug pa ni/ kha cig na re/ lus dkyil gyi pho brang lnga'i a~M la sogs pa'i yi ge rnams rin 'byung la sogs pa'i sa bon dubazhag nas
bskyed par byed pa mi 'thad de/ de ltar na bcos ma'i dkyil 'khor du thal ba'i phyir dang / ha~M dang hU~M lta bu sa bon mgo thur du bstan du mi rung ba'i phyir dang / zhes
bkag nas/ ngag 'don gyi tshe a~M rin chen 'byung ldan zhes sogs sbyar nas gzhung gi tshig mtha' dag med par byed do/ /'di mi 'thad de/ rje btsun rtse mos lus dkyil lung
dang sbyar ba'i le'u gnyis pa nas bhru~M la sogs pa ni pho brang lnga'i lha rnams kyi sa bon te zhes gsal bar gsungs pa dang / gzhung bshad mthong ngo cog gi grangs bgrangs
nas de rnams las 'byung khungs kyi tshig yod par bshad pa kho na 'byung ba dang / khyad par du dpe mdzod ma dang / sga theng ma gnyis su rtsa nang gi khams yab/ phyi
shun gyi rtsa las yum bskyed par bshad do/ /zhes zer ro/ /de'i lan ni/ lus dkyil lha rnams bskyed pa'i gzhi/ a~M las zhes sogs 'byung khungs kyi/ /tshig tu 'dod na gzhan
dag las/ /sangs rgyas las chos chos las ni/ /'phags pa'i tshogs zhes gang gsungs pa/ /'di 'dra'i rigs la 'byung khungs kyi/ /tshig ces mkhas pa rnams la grags/ /khyed kyang
de ltar 'dod na ni/ /a~M las byung zhing a~M yig las/ /logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung zhig /sprul 'khor dbus su 'dod dgos par/ /snga ma de yi rigs pas grub/ /de 'dra khyed
cag bzhed lags sam/ /tshig kyang bsgrig legs mi shes na/ /don bzang smos kyang ci dgos pa'i/ /blun po rnams kyi rang dga'i tshig /mkhas rnams bzhad gad bskyed pa yi/
/'brel med sna tshogs bris pa la/ /bstan bcos yin zhes bshad nyan byed/ /ces sogs 'di 'dra'i rigs la dgongs/ /rje btsun rtse

mo'i lung sbyor gyi/ /tshig des lus dkyil sa bon las/ /bskyed par grub na bhru~M a~M sogs/ /rtsa rgyud nas bshad yig lnga las/ /lus dkyil lha rnams bskyed par rigs/ /lus dkyil
sa bon bhru~M a~M sogs/ /yin zhes bsgrubs nas lha bskyed tshe/ /de dag min pa'i ha~M sogs las/ /bskyed par 'gal ba ltag sprod yin/ /gal te bhru~M a~M la sogs pa'i/ /sa
bon nyid las bskyed do zhes/ /'dod na gzhung bshad thams cad las/ /tsaNDa lI dang mthun pa yi/ /yig 'bru rnams las bskyed pa'i tshul/ /gsal bar bshad pa gzhung bshad la/
/mkhas par rlom pa khyed kyis bkag /sa chen 'gag pa'i sa skya pa'i/ /gzhung bshad mkhas rlom de re blun/ /gzhan du 'di kha byung mod kyang / /skabs 'dir lus la grub zin
zhig /lhar bsgom pa las 'dam kha med/ /yang na 'gal la ma 'khrul ba'i/ /tshad ma khas len byed dam ci/ /kho bo cag ni lung de'i don/ /rig pa'i dbang lnga'i rigs lnga po/
/pho brang gtso bor gnas gyur tshe/ /bhru~M a~M sogs las bskyed pa dang / /lus dkyil bsgom tshe ha~M sogs las/ /bskyed pa gnyis ka tshig nyung ngu'i/ /bstan par 'dod kyi
cig shos min/ /dang po'i las can gang zag gi /lus dkyil lha rnams sa bon las/ /gsar du bskyed pa ma yin par/ /gdod nas grub par go ba'i phyir/ /ngag 'don tshe na de mdzad
kyi/ /las zhes bya ba'i tshig de dag /nor pa yin pa su zhig smra/ /de yi phyir skabs ma longs par/ /tshig tsam rtsod pa'i ngal ba de/ /byis pa rnams kyi khyad nor yin/

/phyogs snga'i bsam pa ma nges par/ /phyogs 'dzin gtam gyi ca co yi/ /phyogs gzhan khegs par mngon rlom pa'i/ /phyogs re'i mig can 'ga' med dam/ /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi
tshigs su bcad pa ste don tshan drug pa'o/ /rgol ba bdun pa ni/ kha cig rgyas gdab kyi skabs su/ sambu T-i las/ rdo rje sems dpa' zhes byar bshad/ /bde ba dam pa ru ni
brjod/ /ces pa'i don/ 'khor lo drug pa 'dod pa po rnams kyi lugs la spyi gtsug gi 'khor lo rdo rje sems dpa' bsgom pa la 'bru mnan pas chog mod/ man ngag 'di pa'i lugs la
rgyas 'debs kyi lha bstan pa yin zhing / de dang mthun par slob dpon dgra las rnam rgyal gyi phyag rgya bzhi pa las/ kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ zhes bshad pas lus
dkyil gyi lha la rdo rje sems dpas rgyas 'debs pa rgyud dang rgya gar ba'i dgongs pa yin par gsal lo zhes zer zhing / ngag 'don gyi skabs su lus dkyil gyi lha thams cad la
rdo rje sems dpas dbur brgyan zhes zer ro/ /de la sambu Ti'i lung des rgyas 'debs bstan par gang las bshad/ gnad kyi gsal byed las/ gsang ba la ni sa yi khams/ zhes pa
nas brtsams te/ chos kyi skur ni rab tu grags/ /zhes pa'i bar gyi rang byung gi ye shes kyi mtshan nyid ston pa las/ rigs bdag gis rgyas gdab ston par dgos pa'i gnas tsam
yang med la/ rang blos sbyar ba'i rje btsun gong ma'i lugs su 'gyur ram/ slob dpon dgra las rnam rgyal gyi gzhung yang pho brang drug pa ston pa'i gzhung yin gyi/ rigs bdag
gis rgyas gdab ston pa'i gzhung ma yin te/ gzhung gi skabs la dpyad pas shes pa yin no/ /'o na rje btsun gong ma'i gzhung las ji ltar bshad ce na/ sras don ma las/ dbang
stegs ni lha thams cad la blangs na/ gtso bo lnga la sku rdo rje rnam snang la sogs pa lnga/ 'khor rnams la rang rang gi gtso bo'am/ yang na thams cad kyi dbu la gnas
lngar rdo rje rtse lnga pa re re bsam mo/ /zhes dang / 'phags pa rin po ches/ gtso bo lnga la rdo rje sems dpa' dang / 'khor rnams la rang

rang gi gtso bo/ skye mched kyi lha rnams la rang rang gi kha dog dang mthun pa'i rigs bdag khro bo bcu la srung 'khor gyi skabs nas 'byung ba bzhin rigs kyi bdag pos dbur
brgyan par bsam mo/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /'o na bshad pa gnyis po ma mthun pa'am/ 'phags pas gsungs pa de mi 'thad do zhe na/ mi mthun par snang ba 'di brgyud pa'i man
ngag med par yi ge la thug 'phrad byas pas smra ba ste/ 'dir rdor sems ni rigs lnga po rang rang gi rgyu rdo rje 'dzin pa yin pas rang rang gi rigs kyi rgyas gdab pa yang
yin la rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyas gdab pa yang yin pas don cig pa yang yin no zhes smra'o/ /de'i lan ni/ lus dkyil lha la rdor sems kyi/ /rigs bdag bshad pa de nor na/ /'phags
pas lus dkyil gtso bo la/ /rdor sems rigs bdag bshad pa de/ /rnam pa kun du dor dgos so/ /gal te 'phags pas bshad pa de/ /rdor sems rigs bdag rigs lnga yi/ /rgyu yi
rdor 'dzin yin pa'i phyir/ /de la 'gal ba med ces smra/ /de lta na ni lha kun gyi/ /rigs bdag rigs lnga'i rgyu rdor 'dzin/ /rdo rje sems dpa' yin pa'i phyir/ /gtso 'khor
kun la rdor sems kyis/ /rgyas 'debs byed pa grub pa'i phyir/ /skabs kyi rtsod pa sprin bzhin dengs/ /dgos med rtsod pa myos byed kyi/ /dregs pa kun gyi byed las yin/ /phyag
rgya bzhi pa'i dngos bstan de/ /pho brang drug par khyed 'dod na/ /pho brang lnga la rtsa 'dab dang / /'khor sogs bshad nas drug pa la/ /de dag mi 'byung ba de ci/ /spyi
gtsug 'khor lo zhes pa de/ /phyag rgya bzhi po gang du 'dus/ /phyag rgya bzhi ru ma 'dus pa'i/ /phyag rgya bzhi pa gad mo'i gnas/ /'khor lo bsgyur ba drug yod na/ /rgyal
chen 'khor

lo bsgyur ba lnga/ /zhes pa'i gzhung de nor ram ci/ /gzhung lugs mthong nas smra dgos kyi/ /phyogs su ma phyin 'ol spyod de/ /rang nyid srang la 'jal ba yin/ /zab mo'i lus
dkyil chos min par/ /smra ba'i log rtog 'jigs rung ba/ /byung tshe mthong thos skad med pa'i/ /sa skya'i rjes 'brang rnying pa la/ /smra bcad brtul zhugs su yin byin/ /mi
shes lung dang rigs pa yi/ /tshig phreng ngal ba lhur byas kyang / /blun po'i kha bshags ji bzhin du/ /rang gis rang nyid pham par byas/ /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi tshigs
su bcad pa ste don tshan bdun pa'o/ /rgol ba brgyad pa ni/ gzhan dag na re/ dbang bskur rab gnas kyi dus su sdom brtson rab byung rnams kyi tshogs 'khor mi byed de/
chos rje sa skya paNDi tas bkag pa'i phyir ro zhes 'dod do/ /de mi 'thad pa ni/ chos rje rang gi lung dang 'gal ba dang / rje btsun chen po'i lung dang 'gal bas so zhes sun
'byin pa'i tshe/ chos kyi rjes rab byung la dpa' bo'i ston mo dgos par bstan zhing / dpa' bo'i ston mo de tshogs 'khor gyi dbye bar mngon rtogs ljon shing du gsungs shing
/ chos rje rang gis kyang gsungs/ phyogs snga ma ni dus khyad par can gyi dus su dpa' bo'i ston mo yang mi byed pas bza' ba'i dam tshig las nyams/ chos rjes bshad pa
ni klu sgrub nas jo bo rje dang / kha che paN chen sogs kyi lugs yin pas sa skya pa'i rang lugs ma yin zhes dang / dus khyad par can gyi tshe rab byung gi tshogs 'khor ma
byas na rtsa ltung bcu gsum par 'gro ba de 'khrul spong gi dgongs pa yin no zhes smra'o/ /de'i lan ni/ mkhyen rab dbang phyug sa paN gyis/ /bshad pa'i rab byung ston mo
de/ /khyad par can gyi bza' ba yis/ /dgag bya de dag khegs nus sam/ /nus na nged cag sdom brtson rnams/ /chos rjes bshad pa de byed na/ /bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa

zhes/ /'brel med snyon de su la smra/ /tshul des dgag bya mi khegs na/ /klu sgrub nas ni chos rje sogs/ /tshad ldan sdom brtson mtha' yas pa/ /rtsa ltung can du khyed bsgrub
bam/ /mdor na tshogs 'khor ma byas pa/ /rkyang pas rtsa ltung 'byung ba de/ /gong ma'i gsung rab gang na bzhugs/ /khyed dag tshogs 'khor byed do zhes/ /kun la rlung ltar
sgrog byed na/ /rje btsun gong mas tshogs 'khor la/ /dpa' bo dpa' mo gnyis tshogs dang / /tshim pa drug sogs bshad pa yis/ /mtshan nyid tshang bar khyed byed dam/ /tshogs
'khor mtshan nyid ma tshang na/ /btags pa ba las 'da' ba med/ /de ltar 'dod na khyed nyid kyis/ /tshogs kyi 'khor lo ma byas phyir/ /rtsa ltung can du khas longs shig
/de phyir rang la skyon brjod pa/ /nges par smyon pa nyid du bas/ /gal te de dag kun byed na/ /phyag na rdo rje'i bstod 'grel las/ /chos gos 'dzin pa rnams la ni/ /bla mas
tshig gis bstan par bya/ /gzhan du bla ma dam tshig ni/ /nyams par 'gyur zhes gang gsungs pa'i/ /gzhan gyis ma khur sdig pa yi/ /khur de khyed cag 'khur ram ci/ /gzhan
yang dus 'khor rgyud 'grel sogs/ /tshad ldan rnams las rab byung gis/ /de ltar byed pa rgyas par bkag /chos rjes bshad pa'i ston mo de/ /dpa' bo'i ston mor khas blangs shing
/ /dpa' bo'i ston mo rje btsun gyis/ /tshogs 'khor dbye bar bshad ces pa/ /gnyis ka gcig char khas blangs nas/ /chos rjes bshad de sa skya pa'i/ /rang lugs min zhes smra
byed pa/

/'di yang 'gal ba ltag sprod yin/ /khu dbon gnyis ka bzhed pa de/ /sa skya'i chos su mi rung na/ /sa skya'i chos kyi mtshan gzhi ni/ /kun mkhyen gyis kyang brnyed mi nus/ /sa
paN 'gag pa'i sa skya pa/ /rnying pa de dag ches cher blun/ /de phyir phyi dro'i kha zas dang / /sha chang rol la rngam pa yi/ /zol gyis tshogs 'khor byed do zhes/ /'jig
rten pa rnams rmongs byed pa'i/ /'dod ldan de dag lhag spyod kyi/ /ting 'dzin bsgom pa ji bzhin no/ /yang dag mgon gyis ma bzung ba'i/ /rnam dag dam pa'i tshul dor nas/
/ma dag 'tsho ba don gnyer ba/ /mtha' dag tshogs kyang lan yod min/ /zhes bya ba ni bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa ste don tshan brgyad pa'o/ /ding sang bstan pa nyams
dma' bas/ /yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge bsnyen gyi/ /bsrung bya tsam la'ang cher lhod pa'i/ /rdo rje slob dpon gzugs brnyan gyis/ /smin grol nus par khas blangs nas/ /dad pa'i
rjes 'brangs bsdud pa mthong / /de phyir chos ltar bcos nas ni/ /chos min byed ces smra ba de/ /rang gzhan kun la gzu bo'i blos/ /smra ba yin na thal mo sbyor/ /gzhan
du rgyal bas lung bstan pa'i/ /tshad ldan mkhas pa smod byed pa'i/ /phyogs 'dzin mkhan de yid bsrub kyi/ /pho nya yin par gdon mi za/ /chos tshul 'di la sbyangs sbyangs pa'i/
/bstan 'dzin gzhan la smod smod pa/ /de dag rnams kyi rang rang gis/ /smra bya'i gnas la nges nges kyi/ /bsgrub byed don du mna' bor bas/ /rang gzhung zin par khas 'che
ba'i/ /thos chung rnams kyi rang gi rang / /lha rnams dga'

ba'i grangs su byas/ /gsar byung yid bsrub rigs kyi tshig /thun tshags bsdus pa'i smod pa'i mda'/ /phyogs 'dir 'phen brtson sred ldan dag /'dod pa'i khyim du gnyid byos shig
/a ho badzra dznyA/ phyogs kun 'phrin las gser gyi 'gebs nus pa'i/ /'od gsal nyi zla'i snang ba 'di med na/ /tshur rol mthong ba'i srin bu me khyer gyis/ /sa gsum snang
byed dbang po bya nus sam/ /sngon dus rtog ge'i chang gis rab myos pa'i/ /phyir rgol glang po smyon pa'i dor stabs kyis/ /gsung ngag mtsho skyes rtsa ba dkrugs pa'i tshe/
/nyes spong lung rigs shes pa 'ga' yod dam/ /deng dus mkhas mang ngang pa'i ded dpon dang / /gzhan zer dbyangs su len pa'i bung ba yang / /chos 'di mkha' la 'dab bzang
ji bzhin du/ /'phur lding byed 'di mgon de'i drin min nam/ /gong ma'i bzhed gzhung ming gi mthar byed cing / /lam bzang bsgom la 'gyod tshang gzhung 'dzugs pa'i/ /'byung
po'i rigs la phebs pa smra byed cing / /rang sde smod rnams gdon gyis ma btab bam/ /rgyal po'i 'phrin dang g.yo sgyu'i sbyor ba yi/ /'bad pas bsgrub pa'i dad pa'i rjes 'brang
gi /sgra 'dzin dbang po gzhan smod ngud mo yis/ /rgyun du rtser la bsam sbyor gzhan med dam/ /chos brgyad 'khor dang khyim la 'khron pa yi/ /kun dkris dbang gis dgag
bsgrub zol sbyor mkhan/ /lus med 'dod pa'i bde ba bsgrub rnams la/ /nyung ngu'i ngag gis lan 'di rigs par smras/ /gsung rab rgya mtsho'i don la ma phyogs par/ /lan brgyar
'chad dang nyan

pa'i grwar zhugs kyang / /tshig tsam 'don pa'i ngal bas dus 'da' ba'i/ /blun po rnams kyis smad par ma gyur cig /'di sbyar dge bas gsung ngag yid bzhin nor/ /sems 'jal rtog
pa'i byi dor gyis sbyangs te/ /thos bsam bsgom pa'i rgyal mtshan rtser bzhag nas/ /blo gsal mang po'i mdun sar bsngags par shog /'gro gsum mchod 'os thub bstan ganggA'i
rgyun/ /nyes bshad 'phrog byed rkang pas ma bcos pa/ /bdag blo skal ldan shing rta la brten nas/ /srid mthar 'gro ba'i gdung ba sel bar shog /tshe rabs kun du dal 'byor gru
bo che/ /'phags nor rin chen bdun ldan legs thob ste/ /'phrin las ba dan dkar po'i thabs mkhas kyis/ /rnam grol sku bzhi'i gling du bgrod par shog /ces gsung ngag lam
'bras kyi sgo nas 'gro ba rnams 'chi ba med pa'i gnas su 'dren par byed pa'i lam gyi srol rgyal po lta bu'i nang nas phyag len gyi rim pa'i cha shas phra mo dag la/ phyogs
re ba'i blo can gzhan gyis brgal zhing brtags pa'i lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags zhes bya ba sngar byas zin pa las/ slar yang de nyid kyi don bsdus pa'i tshigs su bcad pa
'di yang / khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po dang dbyer ma mchis pa 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po ratna wardha la sogs pa yongs 'dzin chos bzhin du spyod pa mang po'i thugs
rje'i spyan ras kyis 'tsho zhing / gsung gi bdud rtsis skal ba bzang por gyur pa shAkya'i dge slong dkon mchog lhun grub ces bgyi bas/ rnam 'gyur gyi lo cho 'phrul gyi zla
ba'i dkar phyogs rdzogs pa gsum pa'i nyin kho na bris rtsom gnyis ka rdzogs

par la shrI e wa~M chos ldan gyi yon tan rin po che sgrog pa'i tshal gyi yang thog tu grub par byas pa'o//rnam dpyod zhe 'thung rus pa las byung ba'i/ /rtog spyod rnam 'gyur
rtse brgya dang ldan pa'i/ /brgal lan 'di ni lha dbang rdo rje ste/ /log rtog brag ri rmang nas 'bebs byed yin/ /zhes bya bar rtogs par bya'o/ /'dis bstan pa spyi dang
bye brag tu gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas pa'i rgyur gyur cig shu bha~M/ zhes pa de rnams kyis rje btsun mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan dkon
mchog lhun grub kyi gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad pa bstan zin nas// ! //gsum pa snyan brgyud mkhas pa'i dbang po'i gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad pa ni/ rje btsun
sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i gsung ngag rin po che'i skabs brgyad la 'khrul pa spong ba rdo rje'i
'phrul 'khor gyi zegs ma zhes bya ba las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ bi dza nU/ kun khyab dga' chen rigs brgya'i bdag /mkhas btsun bzang po'i mchog gyur rje/ /rgyal bas lung bstan
e wa~M pa/ /ngor chen rdo rje 'chang dbang rgyal/ /gong ma'i gsung rab padmo'i tshal/ /khyed kyi 'phrin las nyi gzhon gyis/ /legs par phye ba'i dri bsung ni/ /nam mkha'i
pha mthar khyab pa la/ /rang sde nyung ngu'i phrag dog gis/ /myos pa'i me khyer srin bu dag /nga rgyal lus bskyod smre sngags kyis/ /dub rnams ngal bso'i bcud len sbyin/
/byang chub sems bskyed med pa dang / /rjes 'dzin mang po med pa dang / /sta

gon gcig las med pa dang / /lus dkyil bskyed gzhi med pa dang / /slob dpon gcig tu nges pa dang / /dbang chog lung khungs med pa dang / /rigs gtso'i rgyas 'debs med pa dang
/ /dpa' bo'i ston mo med pa rnams/ /rdo rje theg pa spyi dang ni/ /khyad par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan la gnad gcod bdud kyi tshig /yin phyir thos kyang rna ba dgag
/ces rtsa tshig gi phyogs snga'i thugs rigs dang mthun par brjod nas/ de nyid kyi rang 'grel gyi lan gyi snying po phyung ba mdor bsdus te sbyor ngag tu bkod pa 'di ltar
ro/ /smra ba dang po/ rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas maNDal tshom bu lnga pa la brten pa'i sems bskyed 'di byed mi rigs cing brgyud pa med pa'i bsgrub byed/
lam 'bras pa phyi ma 'ga' zhig gis yi ge 'di steng nas ma thob cing lag len la'ang mi byed pa'i phyir/ zhes par snang ba de ltar na rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo'i dbang
chu'i steng nas kyai rdo rje'i dbang bskur byed pa mi 'thad cing brgyud pa med par thal/ 'phags pa rin po che'i zhal slob dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/
zhang dkon mchog dpal ba la sogs pas yi ge 'di'i steng nas ma thob cing / lag len yang mi byed pa'i phyir/ khyab pa mtshungs/ 'dod mi nus/ ma grub na der thal/ de dag 'phags
pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil rnams kyi steng nas byed pa las 'os med pa'i phyir/ de gnyis la nang gses kyi khyad par phra mo tsam las med do snyam na/ gong
ma la'ang mtshungs te/ 'di dang dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed la nang gses kyi

khyad par phra mo tsam las med pa'i phyir/ yi ge 'di'i lung mkhan chen shes rdor bas ma thob pa sogs thal ror snang ste/ ngor pa yang 'di'i lung mi byed pa'i phyir/ des na
spyir rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa dang / khyad par rje btsun rin po ches brgyud pa'i sems bskyed thob la ma nyams pa dag gis 'di'i steng nas gzhan la sems bskyed phog
pa la skyon ci yang med cing / phyag len gyi khyad par ches khungs btsun zhing rnam par dag par 'gyur ba yin no/ /rje btsun mchog gis mdzad pa yi/ /brgyud pa gnyis ldan
sems bskyed kyi/ /yi ge tsam la'ang zhe sdang pa/ /grags pa'i zhabs kyis ci mdzad dam// ! //smra ba gnyis pa/ slob ma rjes 'dzin dus gcig la nyer lnga las mang ba dang /
zung du gyur pa la mi rung ba'i sgrub byed/ dngos gzhi'i grangs nges sta gon la ltos/ sta gon gyi grangs nges rjes 'dzin la ltos pa'i phyir zer ro/ /de ltar na rjes 'dzin
la grangs nges mi dgos par thal/ dngos gzhi'i grangs nges sta gon la ma ltos/ sta gon gyi grangs nges rjes 'dzin la ma ltos pa'i phyir/ khyab pa la dngos 'gal/ rtags dang
po grub ste/ spyi rgyud las/ sta gon gnas pa byas pa la/ /gal te rkyen gyis ma 'ongs na/ /bla ma blo ldan mkhas pa yis/ /der ni slob ma gzhan mi bzung / /zhes slob ma nyi

su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas tshe med na ni/ /de

yi gzugs brnyan byas nas ni/ /ji skad gsungs ba'i las rnams bya/ /zhes rjes 'dzin la yod pa'i slob ma sta gon dus shi na gzugs brnyan gyi byang bu la sta gon bya ba dang /
slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /gal te rkyen 'ga' zhig gis ni/ /der ni 'ong par ma gyur na/ /gzhan zhig de yi skyin por gzhug /ces phyogs gzhan du song nas ma sleb pa lta
bu la de'i tshab gzhan zhig la sta gon byed par bshad cing / de gnyis la rjes 'dzin dgos par ma bshad pa'i phyir/ des na gsang ba spyi rgyud kyi lung gi dngos bstan gyi
dgongs pa nyer lnga las mi mang ba la rjes 'dzin byed pa ni/ dbang tshar gcig bskur ba lta bu la dgongs pa yin no/ /rig pa'i gnad dang mi ldan par/ /mang po'i lung gi chal
chol gyis/ /srin bu'i kha chu ji bzhin du/ /rang nyid dam du ma bcings sam// ! //smra ba gsum pa/ nub dang po la sa lha/ bum pa sta gon byas pa'i nub de kho na la slob
ma sta gon byed kyi/ nub phyi ma phan chod kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor dang 'brel bar slob ma sta gon byar mi rung ste/ de'i dus kyi slob ma sta gon dang / sta gon snga
ma gsum la 'brel med pa'i phyir zer ro/ /de ltar na nub phyi ma rnams la dngos gzhi'i bsgrub mchod kyang byed mi rung bar 'gyur te/ de dus kyi dngos gzhi'i bsgrub mchod
la sta gon snga ma gsum dgos pa gang zhig de med par ma zad de dang 'brel tsam yang med pa'i phyir/ gzhan yang dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang lan gcig las bskur du mi rung
na ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor la'ang mtshungs pa'i phyir dang / mi mtshungs te rdul tshon

gyi khyad chos yin no snyam na/ de gnyis la de 'dra'i khyad par sus kyang ma bshad pa'i phyir dang / rje btsun rin po ches gzhan phan bdud rtsir/ nub drug gi bar du rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du sbrel nas dbang bskur ba bshad pa sogs gnod byed mtha' yas so/ /des na rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang tshar mang du bskur ba sa skya pa'i
lugs min/ bu ston pa'i slob brgyud dag gi srol yin zer ba/ rje btsun chen po ngor pa dang bzhed pa gcig pa 'dug pas sa skya pa'i khyu nas 'bud kyang / bu ston pa'i slob
brgyud du 'ong don med pas thugs dran brten pa zhu/ ngor pa 'gog pa'i zol sbyor gyis/ /dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbang phri zhing / /sa skya'i rje btsun chen po de/ /rgyang ring
dor la dgos pa ci// ! //smra ba bzhi po/ slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges med pa'i bsgrub byed/ dus gcig la nyer lnga la bskur ba'i phyir zer bar snang ba na/ de ltar
na slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges yod la/ dus gcig la nyer lnga las mang ba la mi bskur ba'i phyir/ khyab pa tshad grub rtags gsal dang po/ 'khrul 'khor gsum/ slob
dpon gyi dbang la dbang stegs kyi steng du gcig bsgrengs su bzhag nas bskur dgos snyam na/ ngor pa yang dbang stegs gcig gi steng du slob ma gnyis gsum la sogs pa dus gcig
tu 'jog par mi bzhed cing / dkyus ma la lag len bde ba'i dbang du byas nas so sor ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang stegs bskyed pa la bzhag nas slob dpon gyi dbang bskur bar mdzad
la/ rgyas par na spyi rgyud

las/ bla mas slob ma gcig pu ni/ /dkyil 'khor dag tu dbang bskur bya/ /mkhas pas gcig char slob ma gnyis/ /dbang bskur ba ni yongs mi bya/ /gnyis sam gsum mam bzhi yang rung
/ /bla mas dbang bskur bya ba ni/ /yo byad gsar pa gzhan rnams kyis/ /thams cad thams cad so sor bya/ /zhes dang / dbang bskur don du dkyil 'khor ni/ /bye ma dkar pos bri
bar bya/ /dkyil 'khor dag dang rjes mthun par/ /stegs bu gru bzhi byas nas su/ /de yi dbus su tshon sna lngas/ /padma yongs su rdzogs par bri/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i don
rje btsun gong ma'i yi ge las 'byung ba'i phyag len dbang stegs kyi dkyil 'khor mtshan nyid tshang ba'i steng du ji skad bshad pa'i yo byad yongs su rdzogs pa'i tshig
bsgrengs du/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len shin tu rgyas pa'ang byed pas/ khyed kyi padma 'dab brgyad kyi ri mo tsam gyi steng du bzhag nas slob dpon gyi
dbang bskur ba la de tsam gyi nga rgyal gyis nyams dag pa ngal ba lhur len par zad do/ /bung ba gzhon nu'i gshog brgyangs kyis/ /nga rgyal lding bskor 'di mthong tshe/
/yongs 'du'i 'dab bzang dbang po des/ /'dzam gling mun par ma byas mtshar// ! //smra ba lnga pa/ lus dkyil gyi lha rnams sa bon la bskyed pa'i bsgrub byed/ sras don ma gnyag
ma sogs gzhung bshad mang po las a~M las ha~M las zhes sogs dang / sga theng ma/ dpe mdzod ma gnyis su/ lte ba'i nang gi a~M gi byang sems las bcom ldan 'das rin chen
'byung ldan zhes dang / phyi'i rtsa a~M

las de'i yum sa rnam par dag pa spyan ma zhes gsungs pa sgrub byed do/ /de ltar na lus dkyil gyi lha rnams sa bon las bskyed la/ sras don ma sogs las bskyed par gsungs pa'i
phyir/ 'dod na mi bskyed par thal/ sga theng ma dang / dpe mdzod ma gnyis las mi bskyed par bshad pa'i phyir/ ma grub na der thal/ lte ba'i rtsa lam yi ge rnam pa can dang
/ de'i nang gi khams gnyis/ bskyed rim gyi skabs kyi lha'i bskyed chog gi sa bon yin par rgya bod su yang mi 'thad pa'i phyir/ des na slob dpon rin po ches lung sbyar
du gsungs pa yang / pho brang lnga'i gtso bo'i sa bon tsam bstan pa yin gyi/ khyed 'dod pa ltar yin na de dag brtag gnyis nas bshad pa'i yig 'bru lnga po de las skabs 'dir
bskyed dgos pa la de 'dra sus kyang ma bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /des na gnas de dag gi rtsa yi ge hU~M la sogs pa'i rnam par gnas pa rnams lha de dang der bskyed pa las de
bskyed ces brjod pa la dgongs nas a~M las hU~M las sogs gsungs/ ngo bo rtsa yi ge'i rnam par gnas pa de nyid ka lhar bskyed rgyu yin pas las dang po pa rnams kyis go bde
ba dang / blun po rnams la 'di lta bu'i log rtog skye ba dgag pa'i phyir/ a~M rin chen 'byung ldan sogs gsal bar gsungs/ don la khyad par med pa ni gnad kyi bshad pa yin
no/ /rang bzhin lhun grub bskyed gzhi ni/ /bor nas bcos ma'i bskyed chog gis/ /bsgrub las gong ma'i gsung rab la/ /nang 'gal yod par grub 'di mtshar// ! //smra ba drug pa/
lam dus kyi brtul zhugs

kyi dbang dang / rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la yan lag bzhi rdzogs kyi bskyed chog dgos pa'i bsgru byed du/ rje btsun gyi lam dus kyi dbang chog tu/ de la thun mong
gi dbang drug rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang dang bdun ka'i bdag dang dbang rdzas gnyis ka yongs su dag pa bzhis byin gyis brlabs dgos te/ de'ang dam tshig pa ni rgyu dus kyi
dbang dang mi 'dra ste/ pho brang lnga'i gtso bor 'pho/ rdo rje 'chang yang zhal gcig phyag gnyis par 'pho la lhag ma rnams ni rgyu dus kyi dbang dang khyad par med de
zhes pa'i lung 'dren par byed do/ /'o na brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la yan lag bzhi rdzogs kyi bskyed chog dgos par thal/ rje btsun gyi dgos par gsungs pa'i
phyir/ 'dod na mi dgos par thal/ rje btsun gyi mi dgos par gsungs pa'i phyir te/ gong du drangs ma thag pa'i lung de nyid las/ 'di skabs kyi lam dus kyi dbang dang rgyu
dus kyi dbang la lha dam tshig pa bskyed pa'i rgyas bsdus tsam ma gtogs gzhan khyad par med par gsal bar gsungs pa'i phyir dang / rgyu dus kyi dbang la de ltar mi dgos
par rje btsun rtse mo'i dbang chu dang / 'phags pa rin po che'i bdag 'jug gnyis las gsal bar bshad cing / der ma zad gong ma'i yi ge chos rje bla ma/ theg chen chos rje sogs
sus kyang khyed 'dod pa ltar gyi bskyed chog ye ma gsungs so/ /des na rje btsun gyis/ bdun ka'i bdag dang dbang rdzas la yan lag bzhi rdzogs kyi bskyed chog dgos par
gsungs pa la gtso che ba la dgongs nas gsungs pa yin gyi/ re re nas khyab mtha' 'dzin pa ni

ma yin no/ /de ltar ma yin na/ ming dbang la'ang nges par dbang rdzas dgos pa dang / ding sang lag len la rdo rje dril bu spyi bor bzung nas ming dbang bskur dus kyang dbang
rdzas de la bskyed chog sus kyang mi byed pa sogs la thugs zhib gnang ba zhu/ 'dab bzang dbang po yud kyis bgrod pa la/ /rtsing por bsam nas byi bas lo brgyar ni/ /zhib
mor phyin yang rang nyid ngal ba las/ /gzhan du lhag pa'i khyad chos ga la thob// ! //smra ba bdun pa/ lus dkyil gyi lha la rgyas gdab rigs mtshon med pa'i bsgrub byed du
rdo rje sems dpas rgyas btab zhes zer ba dang / pho brang lnga'i gtso bo lnga la sras don mar rnam snang la sogs pa rigs lnga so sos rgyas gdab pa dang / 'phags pa rin
po ches gtso bo lnga la rdo rje sems dpas rgyas 'debs par gsungs pa la de gnyis dgongs pa gcig pa'i sgrub byed du/ de skabs kyi rigs lnga dang rdo rje sems dpa' khyad par
med par byas nas/ rgyas btab de rang rigs kyi rgyas gdab gang yin la/ rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyas btab yang yin par 'dod do/ /de ltar na lus dkyil gyi lha rnams la rdo rje
sems dpas rgyas btab pa rigs mtshon med pa ma yin par thal/ rigs mtshon yod pa'i phyir/ der thal/ rang rigs kyi rgyas btab yod pa'i phyir/ der thal rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyas
btab yin pa'i phyir/ 'khrul 'khor gsum/ sambu Ti'i lung gis ma bstan pa'i sgrub byed gnad kyi gsal byed las ma bshad do/ /zhes pa'ang mi 'thad de/ der rgyud 'chad pa'i
dbang du byas pa'i

bshad pa yin la/ 'dir man ngag gi lung sbyar du 'dren pa la de ji lta ba dgos pa'i nges pa med pa'i phyir dang / phyag rgya bzhi pa'i lung gi pho brang drug pa kho na ston
rgyu yin na bstan bcos der pho brang lnga'i lha brgya lnga bcu rtsa bdun bstan pa'i rjes su/ kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ /rdo rje sems dpa' zla ba'i mdog /ces gsungs
pas lha de thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i gnas spyi bor rdo rje sems dpa' re re 'god par bshad la/ de ltar min na kun gyi zhes pa'i mang tshig gi 'bru ji ltar gnon soms shig
des na sras don mar lha thams cad la rdo rje rtse lnga pas rgyas 'debs par gsungs pa'ang 'di dang shin tu gnad mthun pa yin no/ /rang gi grub mtha'i gtso bo la/ sun 'byin
byed pa'i lung rigs mtshon/ thogs nas de nyid bsgrub par rlom/ /'di 'dra'i rigs pa sngar ma byung // ! //smra ba brgyad pa/ ngor lugs la bza' ba'i dam tshig med do zhes
rtsa bar dam bcas pa dang / 'grel par bdud rtsi ril bu la brten pa khyad par gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig tu mi rigs te/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig yin zhes dang / dpa'
bo'i ston mo tshogs kyi 'khor lo yin te/ khyad par gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig tshogs kyi 'khor lo yin pa'i phyir/ de ltar na yang mngon rtogs ljon shing las/ khyad par gyi
bza' ba'i dam tshig ni tshogs kyi 'khor lo ste/ de la gnyis las/ ming don dang / cho ga'o/ /dang po la lnga/ gang zag gi dbye ba dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbye ba dang / dus
kyi dbye ba dang / dgos pa'i dbye ba dang / mchod bya'i dbye ba'o/ /dang po la

gsum/ dpa' bo rnal 'byor ma tshogs pa la tshogs kyi 'khor lo zhes bya la/ dpa' bo 'ba' zhig tshogs na dpa' bo'i ston mo/ dpa' mo 'ba' zhig tshogs na dpa' mo'i ston mo/ zhes
sogs kyi lung 'dren pa dang / dpa' bo'i ston mo tshogs kyi 'khor lo ma yin na/ dpa' bo'i ston mo la sogs pa'i bdun po de rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig ni yin don med la/
de'i phyir bza' ba'i dam tshig gang yang ma yin par thal lo/ /zhes zer ba rnams rim bzhin mi rigs te/ ngor lugs la bza' ba'i dam tshig yod par thal/ bdud rtsi ril bu bsten
pa de bza' ba'i dam tshig yin pa'i phyir/ der thal/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig yin pa'i phyir/ 'khor gsum/ ri bong rwa tshogs kyi 'khor lo yin par thal/ khyad par gyi
bza' ba'i dam tshig tshogs kyi 'khor lo yin pa'i phyir/ 'khor gsum/ shes bya rtag pa yin par khas blangs pas/ shes bya yin na rtag pa yin pas khyab pa khas len mi dgos
pas dgongs par zhu/ gzhan yang dpa' bo'i ston mo med par thal/ de yod na bza' ba'i dam tshig yin dgos pa la/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig gi yin don med/ khyad par gyi
bza' ba'i dam tshig min te tshogs kyi 'khor lo ma yin pa'i phyir/ der thal/ de la rje btsun gyi tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ dpa' bo'i ston mo dpa' mo'i ston mo zhes de gsum mi 'dra
ba tha dad du bshad pa'i phyir/ ma yin/ de gsum ming gi rnam grangs kyi dbye ba yin no snyam na/ de ltar na dpa' mo'i ston mo yang / dpa' bo'i ston mor 'gyur zhing /
dpa' mo

yang dpa' bor 'gyur pa sogs brjod kyis mi lang bas/ 'di 'dra'i grub mtha' mi 'dzin par gsol ba 'debs so/ /smras pa/ byis pa sgron me thogs nas mun rum du/ lan brgyar 'bad kyang
phyogs kun gsal mi nus/ /mkhas pa nyi zla'i 'od kyis skad cig la/ /rab yangs 'dzin ma'i khyon kun lham mer gsal/ /da lta sa steng 'di na sa skya pa'i/ /gsang chen bstan
pa dri med 'dzin pa la/ /rje btsun ngor pa'i 'phrin las kho na las/ /gzhan du yod med gzur gnas kun gyis shes/ /de phyir tshul der smod na rang nyid ni/ /nyams par ma
zad rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /bstan la dad gus med par mi 'gyur ram/ /de bas da ni chags sdang phrag dog spongs/ /bdag ni byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan la/ /snying nas dad
mos 'on kyang rjes 'brang 'ga'i/ /blo mtsho'i gting zab brtag phyir nyams dgar ni/ /smras la dam pas bzod bzhes thugs rjes skyong / /de skad brjod pa'i dge tshogs chu klung
des/ /'gro 'di'i log rtog dri ma kun sbyangs te/ /'khrul med gong ma'i gsung gi nying khu yi/ /zung 'jug rdo rje'i bcud len grub gyur cig /mangga laM/ zhes pa de rnams
kyis snyan brgyud mkhas pa'i dbang po'i gsung rab las 'byung tshul bstan zin nas/ bzhi pa de dag gi lan 'debs rdzong lugs kyi mkhas pa dam tshig legs bshad las 'byung
tshul bshad pa la gnyis te/ chos rje bzang po bkra shis kyi gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad pa dang / dge chu ba buddha shrI'i legs bshad las 'byung tshul bshad pa'o/ /dang
po ni/ chos kyi rje mkhan chen bzang bkras pas mdzad

pa'i snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ na mo gu ru bhya/ snyan brgyud 'khrul sel zhes bya ba/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams dang dbyer ma mchis pa mthu stobs kyi dbang

gsum 'bras stsol rje la 'dud/ /chos kyi spyan ldan bla ma'i gsung / /chos ltar bcos pas dri mar byas/ /chos mthun rigs pas dag byed pa/ /chos 'dod rnams la bshad par bya/
/bla chen badzra dhwa dza yis/ /gong ma'i gsung mchog dgongs pa'i don/ /legs par bshad pa mang bkod kyang / /'dir ni chu rgyun bzhi pa ru/ /sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa
sogs/ /tshig brgyad 'grel par bcas pa la/ /sun 'byin rnam par spros pa'i lan/ /skabs don legs par bshad par bya/ /dang po'i don la 'di skad du/ brgyud pa gnyis kyi sems
bskyed kyi/ /cho ga rje pas mdzad pa ni/ /sgo rum brnyed las brgyud ces pa/ /tshad ldan smras pa med do lo/ /sgo rum brnyed dam min yang rung / /mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje
pas/ /bla ma bcu phrag lhag pa las/ /rje yi bka' 'bum kun gyi lung / /gsan pa gang na'ang de 'dra med/ /sdom rgyun yod pa'ang bsgrub bya yin/ /gzhan yang mtha' gzhan bkag
pas shes/ /des na de 'dra'i cho ga ni/ /gsar du gzhan gyis byas par nges/ /dbang gi sngon du ljon shing las/ /sems bskyed cho ga bshad na yang / /phyag len nub par

mkhas rnams bzhed/ /gzhan yang spros pa 'di skad lo/ /dbang bskur byed pa'i sngon rol du/ /sems bskyed 'dod dam mi 'dod dris/ /'dod na'ang khyed la de med de/ /lugs gnyis brgyud

de 'dra'i sems bskyed kyi/ /cho ga med par dbang bskur ba/ /khyed rang 'dod pa dran par gyis/ /sta gon 'jug pa'i gnas skabs su/ /sems bskyed gsungs phyir dgos 'di med/ /gsum
la skyabs 'gro la sogs pa'i/ /'khrul spong nyid las ji skad du/ /smon 'jug sems bskyed blang bar bya/ /de ni gud du blangs kyang rung / /ma blangs kyang ni sta gon gyi/

/rjes

/khyad par rdzogs rim brtan par gsungs/ /rgya gzhung dgongs pa drug pa bstan/ /sras don ma zhes gtso bo lnga/ /rigs lngas rgyas btab 'khor rnams la/ /rang rigs gtso bos
rgyas btab dang / /yang na kun gyi gnas lnga ru/ /rdo rje rtse lnga bsam par bya/ 'phags pas gtso bo rdor sems dang / /'khor rnams rang rang gtso bo dang / /skye mched
kha dog mthun pa'i rigs/ /khro bo srung 'khor skabs ltar gsungs/ /rang rang du ni rdor sems phyir/ /rigs lnga rdor sems don gcig yin/ /de ltar ci 'byin bkod pa la/ /rkun
rgyab brdzun ma 'di skad lo/ /rgyud 'chad

tshe na rdzogs rim dang / /man ngag skabs su lus dkyil bstan/ /rgyud don ma gnyer lus dkyil ston/ /phyag rgya bzhi par rgyas gdab ston/ /'di tsam zin so gsal po yin/ /gal te
rdzogs rim nyid bstan na/ /'khor lo drug pa gang gis ston/ /phyag rgya bzhi par 'khor lo lnga/ /rdzogs rjes kun gyi dbang sogs gsungs/ /drug pa bstan zhes 'os spyod yin/
/sras 'phags 'gal spong khyod bzhin 'dod/ /sras don ma yi phyi ma ni/ /dbu rgyan rang chas don yin zer/ /a seng ma las rdo rje yi/ /theg pa dgongs pa du ma zhes/ /gsungs
pa 'di nyid mthong na yang / /mkha' 'gros byin rlabs birWa sogs/ /grub thob rnams la brten dgos zhes/ /'di 'dra mang mthong rgyu don rnams/ /rang 'gar rtog ge'i rigs pas
'chad/ /birWa'i snyan brgyud zab mo rnams/ /rgyud dang rgya gzhung 'gal lo zhes/ /'brel med tshig 'di gzhan lugs bzhin/ /snyan brgyud yi ge med pa'i rtags/ /de yi zin so
mkhas pas khrel/ /'khor lo drug pa'ang lnga po bzhin/ /don gyis bstan zhing ma bstan na/ /khyod kyi rgyud don ji ltar rung / /khyad par rgyas btab zur du gsungs/ /'gal
yang snyan brgyud ga la gnod/ /'khor lo drug pa man ngag lugs/ /gdan sogs yi ger shin tu gsal/ /dbu rgyan rang chas zer ba de/ /snyan brgyud med pa'i babs bcol yin/ /gsung
ngag ma rdzogs rang rigs sogs/ /rgyas btab dgos pa snying po ste/ /zhib tu gsang gtam mi sgrog go /bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa dang / /zhes

par lan 'debs 'di skad du/ ljon shing las bshad tshogs 'khor gyi/ /dbye bas sa lugs khyab na ni/ /dpa' bo'i ston mo'ang der 'gyur ro/ /de ni 'khor gsum lan med yin/ /dbye ba
thams cad dngos yin na/ /rnal 'byor pho mo tshogs par 'gyur/ /rab byung tshogs 'khor ma byas na/ /rtsa ltung 'byung na klu sgrub sogs/ /rtsa ltung can du thal bar 'gyur/
/dbye ba thams cad dbye gzhi ru/ /nges par 'dod na bden gnyis kyi/ /dbye gzhi 'jig rten blo tsam dang / /shes byar don dam bden pa dang / /khyod kyis khas len dgos zhes
zer/ /'dod lan thebs pa'i thal 'gyur la/ /'khor gsum rigs pa shes pas khrel/ /pho mo tshogs pa rnam gnyis te/ /gang zag phal la grags pa dang / /rdor sems bsgom pa'i ting
'dzin gyi/ /lha dgu la sogs dkyil 'khor dang / /dpa' bo dpa' mo rnams kyang yod/ /de lta min na tshogs 'khor gyi/ /tshim pa lnga yang dka' bar gnas/ /rtsa khams dpa' bo
dpa' mo ru/ /gdod nas grub par khyod nyid 'dod/ /gzhan yang tshogs 'khor rtsod spong las/ /phyi nang mkha' 'gro zhes kyang gsungs/ /rtsa ltung 'byung dang mi 'byung ba/
/klu sgrub la sogs sdom las grol/ /de lta min na de bzhin 'byung / /'on kyang lugs gnyis so sor nges/ /bu ram phyi dror 'dod pa dang / /mi 'dod 'gal ba med pa bzhin/ /gcig
tu nges na ha cang thal/ /don dam shes byar khas len pas/ /dpe de da dung bsgrub bya yin/ /gzhan yang spros pa 'di skad zer/ /tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid rjes mthun pa/ /drug
pa dngos su

yod med yin/ /phyag rgya'i rnal 'byor la rten nas/ /rdzogs rim ye shes dngos su bskyed/ /lhan skyes tshim nus rnal 'byor pa/ /kho nas tshogs 'khor bya ba dang / /de med khyim
pa'ang de dngos med/ /rab byung bzang yang de 'dra bkag /Dombhi bas kyang pho mo gnyis/ /nges par dgos pa bshad ces zer/ /'o na sngon gyi lam 'bras pa/ /kyai rdor dbang
zhus thams cad la/ /lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes gang / /dngos su skye bar 'dod dam ci/ /lo rgyus kun las tshogs 'khor bshad/ /khyad par grub chen buddha shrI/ /tshogs 'khor
mdzad pa'i rnam thar ltos/ /rab byung tshogs 'khor mi rung na/ /dge slong dpa' bo rdo rje de/ /tshogs 'khor gshegs pa'ang mi bden nam/ /'di rnams bod nas byung rgyal
smras/ /tshim pa drug pa'i nyams len dang / /mchog dbang gsum po mtshungs pa'i phyir/ /tshogs 'khor bzhin du de la yang / /dngos rtags gnyis su 'byed dgos 'gyur/ /tshogs
'khor dbang bskur gnyis ka la/ /dngos rtags 'byed na rtog bzo yin/ /gzhan yang spros pa 'di ltar bris/ /'khrul spong las ni tshogs gral du/ /sdom pa 'og ma'i bcas pa dang
/ /'gal bar dogs na rtsa ltung bshad/ /tshogs 'khor ma byas ltung bshad min/ /dngos lan thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /dri lan du ni gsal ba ltar/ /bskyed rim brtan po yod pa
dang / /ma dad bzlog nus rnal 'byor pas/ /tshogs 'khor dngos su bya ba dang / /rab byung rnams la min par gsungs/ /rnal 'byor tshogs 'khor rung ba dang / /rab byung

tshogs 'khor mi byed par/ /dus 'khor bde mchog bshad ces zer/ /'di dag gnad kyi snying po'i lan/ /rje yi rtsa ltung 'khrul spong las/ /rab byung phyi dro mi bza' ba'ang / /bcu
gsum pa yi ltung bas 'jigs/ /cung zad 'thung zhing kha zas brten/ /snod min drung du rab byung la/ /de skad smra na rtsa ltung gsungs/ /tshogs 'khor dus su rab byung
gis/ /bslab pas bcings nas chang 'thung dang / /phyi dro'i kha zas brten pa yis/ /ltung ba byung dogs mi brten pa/ /rtsa bar gsungs shing nad pa yi/ /reg pa tsam las mi brten
yang / /nyes med ril bu brten pa ni/ /'di yi skabs ni min zhes gsungs/ /gal te gong du bshad pa ltar/ /bcas 'gal dogs pas rtsa ltung ste/ /bcas 'gal med na'ang bstan
pa bsam/ /tshogs 'khor med phyir mi 'gal na/ /'o na de 'dra'i dgos med pa'i/ /rab byung tshogs 'khor rung bar mthun/ /bstan la phan nam min yang rung / /dgos pa gtso bor
rje btsun bzhed/ /chang ni 'o mar bsgyur nus pa/ /tshogs 'khor chad du khyed nyid 'dod/ /'o ma'i ltung ba'i nyes pa gang / /de la ma dad ga la 'ong / /bstan la'ang gnod
par ji ltar 'gyur/ /nad la gnod pa'ang dka' ba yin/ /gzhan gyi rab byung tshogs 'khor dus/ /sha chang brten zhes snod smin bsgrags/ /rang gi tshogs 'khor ma byas par/ /khyed
la ltung ba gnyis su 'gyur/ /tshogs 'khor ma byas rtsa ltung ste/ /ma brten pa zhes rtsa ba dang / /'grel par dam rdzas mi brten zhes/ /ma mthong phyogs mthong gzhan
la smod/ /rang nyid ngo tsha gzhan gyis

khrel/ /'khrul spong don yang dang po yi/ /las can rnams kyi'ang rung ba ste/ /ljon shing nyid las dam tshig dang / /tshogs 'khor gnas dang gang zag gsum/ /chos rjes tshogs
'khor rtsod spong las/ /gnas dang mdun bskyed tshogs 'khor dus/ /bzod gsol skabs dang rnam pa bzhir/ /las ni dang po zhes bya ba/ /khu dbon gnyis kyi gsungs pa 'di/ /log
rtog brag ri 'joms pa'i thog /tshim pa drug pa'ang rnam gnyis te/ /phyag rgya bsten dang ting 'dzin gnyis/ /phyi ma Dombhi he ru kas/ /mar dang mar gyi nying khu yis/ /snying
kha ru ni byug par bya/ /ji skad gsungs pa de bzhin gsungs/ /des na zhib tu ma bltas par/ /rbad chod sngas na rang nyid 'bebs/ /rigs pa tshogs 'khor mchog dbang mtshungs/
/de phyir rgyu lam mtshan nyid pa/ /rab byung nyams len mi 'dod dam/ /gal te sha chang dngos su yin/ /mchog dbang ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor phyi/ /mtshungs min snyam
na dge slong la/ /sa brko me reg la sogs dang / /dbang dus gzhu sogs 'gog gam ci/ /dgos pa gtso phyir de mthong tshe/ /nyes med zhes ni rje btsun bzhed/ /mdor na tshogs 'khor
'chad skabs dang / /dang po'i las can rab byung dang / /med mi rung ba sha chang dang / /kun nas mtshungs pa'i rigs pa sogs/ /gtan tshigs bzang po 'di mthong phyin/
/gzhan lugs bsres nas snyan brgyud kyi/ /gdams pa 'gog pa'i babs bcol rnams/ /nyung na tshogs kyi bsod nams 'phel/ /des na khyed kyis bshad pa rnams/

/gzhan gyi sa lugs snyan brgyud la/ /skyon brjod snying la zhugs pa yi/ /yid ches med pa'i skyogs bshad mang / /lugs gtan 'gal yang snyan brgyud dang / /'gal med sa lugs snying
por bzung / /dus 'khor bde mchog gsal lo zhes/ /snyan brgyud 'gog pa'i zur za yin/ /tshogs 'khor bshad pa ma rtogs dang / /rjes 'dzin la sogs log rtog dang / /lus dkyil
the tshom bcas pa ste/ /ma rtogs log rtog the tshom gyis/ /'khrul pa snyan brgyud 'di yis sel/ /dbus gdong nyer lnga'i phyogs snga las/ /'phros don lan dang tshig skyon
sogs/ /zhib dpyod byas na mang yod kyang / /gnad rnams dril nas 'di tsam bris/ /gzhan yang gsang ba kun rgyan gyi/ /dgongs pa yin zhes rjes 'brang rnams/ /la la tshogs
'khor sha chang rol/ /phal cher tha mal sha chang brten/ /dbang bskur skabs su tshogs 'khor spong / /rang gzhan gnyis ka'i lugs dang 'gal/ /'ga' zhig bdud rtsi ril bu bsten/
/bcu gsum pa yi nyes med zer/ /'khrul spong nyid las skabs min gsungs/ /gzhan yang dbus pa'i thos bral 'ga'/ /sems bskyed brgyud pa yod par thal/ /zhes sogs tshig khri
smra ba thos/ /'o na shes rab snying po las/ /gzugs med sgra med la sogs dang / /dbu ma rtsa ba'i mchod brjod du/ /'gag pa med pa skye med pa/ /zhes sogs la yang mtshungs
pa'i phyir/ /blun po'i rigs pa rang la zlog /brgal lan med pa'i ci drag yin/ /de 'dra gnas lugs skabs yin na/ /snga ma'ang skabs don ci mi rtsi/ /bden lan byin pa kun

la phan/ /snying nas rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /snyan brgyud lhag ma'ang nub par dogs/ /legs par bshad pa'i dge ba 'dis/ /snyan brgyud zab mo rab rgyas shing / /'gro bas sangs
rgyas myur thob shog /'og zla'i yar tshes bco lnga'i nyin/ /nyin byed snyan brgyud 'khrul sel 'di/ /'di phyir phan bde 'byung ba'i gnas/ /gnas mchog mkhar byung yangs rtser
bkod/ /snyan brgyud 'khrul sel zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos 'di ni/ mkhas pa chen po lcags thang pa dang dpal sgyi chu ba yab sras rnams kyi zhabs pad bsten pas/ mdo sngags
kyi don la blo gros kyi snang ba cung zad gsal ba ngam ring chos sde chen po'i mkhan chen bzang po bkra shis zhes bya bas grub pa'i bsti gnas se mkhar byung gi yangs
rtser legs par bkod pa 'dis sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar zhing rgyas pa dang / lam gyi bar chad zhi nas sems can thams cad kyis rdo rje 'chang gi go 'phangs myur du thob
par gyur cig dge legs 'phel/ ces pa de rnams kyis chos rje bzang po bkra shis kyi gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad zin nas// ! //gnyis pa sgyi chu ba burdha shrI'i legs bshad
las 'byung tshul bshad pa ni/ des mdzad pas yang lan nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ oM bde legs su gyur cig rgyal ba kun gyi ye shes 'jam pa'i
dbyangs/ /gangs can 'dul phyir mi'i tshul bzung nas/ /ma nor lam ston rje btsun sa skya pa/ /skye dgu kun gyi gtsug na rgyal gyur cig /mdo rgyud man ngag bstan bcos kun
gyi don/ /ji bzhin rtogs

nas gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i/ /'khrul med smra ba'i dbang po mus srad pa/ /las skal bsags rgyab can gyi gtsug tu mchod/ /smin grol lam gyi cha thebs ma lus pa/ /sa skya'i bla
chen rnams kyi dgongs pa bzhin/ /snyan brgyud bzhi ldan rje btsun sgyi chu ba/ /bdag cag rnams kyi 'dren par gsol ba 'debs/ /'di ltar dri ma med pa'i lung gis phyug cing
mngon par rtogs pa'i yon tan gyis brgyan pa/ nyan thos dang theg pa chen po spyi la brtsams ste bstan pa gces spras su mdzad pas/ ngur mig 'dzin pa rnams kyi rtse mor
byon pa/ rang dang gzhan gyi grub mtha' rgya mtsho lta bu la dbang 'byor bas mkhas pa'i bya ba gsum la thogs pa med pa/ gdul bya mtha' dag smin grol la 'god pa'i mdzad pa
bzang pos sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i khur lci ba/ snyigs dus kyi rdo rje 'chang chen po kun dga' bzang po zhes yongs su grags pa de nyid kyis skyes bu brtson 'grus kyi stobs
bral zhing shes rab kyi mig long ba/ rnam g.yeng gi khur che zhing le lo'i 'dam du bying ba/ blo gros kyi rtsal med pas legs bshad don du mi gnyer ba/ dad pa'i rjes su
'brang zhing nyung ngu la dga' ba dag gi ngo bor/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras 'bu dang bcas pa'i gdam ngag rim par snyan du brgyud pa'i yig sna/ nges par med du mi rung
ba brgya phrag gcig dang sum cu rtsa brgyad las/ thos bsam gyis sgro 'dogs chod par byas nas dkri tshul gyi rim pa sum cu/ chos kyi tshom chen po lnga brgya dang lnga
bcu rtsa gnyis/ bsgom gegs bsal ba'i thabs brgya phrag gcig dang sum cu ste/ mdor na rdo rje 'chang

nas ding sang gi bar du tshig don gyi cha thams cad snyan brgyud yin pa rje btsun gong ma rnams dang rjes 'brang tshad ldan dag gis yi ger bkod pa/ tshig gi lhad med pa/ ngan
rtog gi dri ma bral ba/ rang bzo'i rtog rtags kyis zin bris spangs pa/ rtsa khra 'phros gsum du grags pa 'di nyid gzhung khrid rgyas pa nyid kyi steng du dril te/ de yang
snang ba gsum ni phar phyin rang rkang du mdzad la/ de'i rjes su brgyud pa gnyis kyi lugs su byas pa'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga'am/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho
ga chos rje pas mdzad pa gang rung gis byang chub sems dpa'i sdom ldan du mdzad nas bzod dbang bskur te sngags la 'jug par mdzad do/ /da ni phyogs phyi ma'i dgongs pa brjod
par bya ste/ de yang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la thog mtha' bar gsum du bka' drin che ba sad mi mi bdun dang / g.yo dmar gtsang gsum la sogs pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi
rigs su 'khrungs pa dang / sa lam gyi yon tan phal cher bgrod de nub phyogs u rgyan gyi yul nas gangs can gyi ljongs su skye ba bzhes pa/ rdo rje theg pa la mkhas pa'i
mchog tu gyur pa/ khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras khu dbon rnams kyi gsung rab tshig don ma lus pa thugs su chud nas 'gal med du rtogs zhing 'khrul med du smra ba'i
spobs pa can/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes yongs su grags pa de nyid kyis phyogs snga ma'i lugs srol de dag gong ma'i gsung dang
'gal zhing / rang bzo'i dri mas slad pas/ zab mo'i man ngag med pa'i

phyir thar 'dod dad brtson shes rab dang ldan pa'i gdul bya dag bslu bar gzigs nas/ de dag la thugs brtse ba dang / snyan brgyud zab mo mi nub par bya ba'i phyir rnam par bshad
pa'i chu rgyun la sogs pa bstan bcos chen po mang po dag brtsams so/ /de dag las 'dir ni/ sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang / /zhes pa nas/ de kun 'di rgyu dgag par
bya/ /zhes pa'i bar mi 'thad pa'i phyogs brgyad smos nas/ lung rigs man ngag gi sgo nas sun phyung ste chos dang mthun pa'i lan med par byas so/ /'on kyang / dkon mchog gsum
gyi gdung sob pa/ 'phrin las kyi mdzad pa lhun grub pa/ rje ngor pa nyid kyi gdan sar byon pa/ dgongs pa bsgrub pa la khur 'khur ba/ yongs kyi bshes gnyen chen po de
nyid kyis tshangs pa'i rigs sngags zhes bya ba'i lan byas so/ /de la phal cher ni mi 'byar ba'i lung dang / mi 'jug pa'i rigs par snang la/ 'ga' zhig ni nan gyis 'dod dgos
pa'i klan ka dang / shas cher chos dang mi mthun pa'i tshigs bcad dang dma' 'byin pa'i ngan smras su go zhing / kha cig ni zol sbyor gyi ngag dang / la la ni don gyi khas
blangs par yang snang bas/ yang dag par na lan dgos par mi 'dug mod/ de lta na yang rang nyid bla ma rnams kyi bka' drin dran zhing / yid ches pa btab par bya ba dang
/ blo gros kyi snang ba bskyed pa'i phyir chags sdang spangs te 'di bri ba la skyon med do/ /de la gnas skabs brgyad du brgal lan ngos bzung nas dngos lan kho na byas pas/
chos dang mthun zhing gzhan dag la chags sdang spang gi snang ba mi bskyed

pa yin no/ des na sems bskyed kyi skabs su/ rigs sngags mkhan po na re/ sems bskyed kyi yi ge de gsar du brnyed pa dang / de la lung gi brgyud pa med pa yin du chug kyang /
des sems bskyed kyi sdom rgyun med par dbang gi 'byor pa sus bsgrub par nus pa ma yin te/ spyir rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i dbang gi sngon du 'gro ba'i sems bskyed cig mi 'dod
na ni shin tu skal ba dman la/ 'dod na sangs rgyas nas rje rtse mo yan la yi ge de gtan med kyang / de'i brjod bya dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa'i rgyun yod
pa dang / rje btsun nas kho bo cag gi rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bar la yang bde kyai gnyis kyi dbang gi sngon du yi ge de dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa 'bog pa'i
phyag len gyi cho ga ma nor ba yod pas/ phyag len dang mthun pa'i yi ge su zhig gis byas kyang de'i steng nas cho ga byed du rung ba yin te/ dper na rtse mo'i dbang chu'i
lung ma thob kyang man ngag lugs kyi dbang phyin ci ma log par thob pa'i rdo rje slob dpon zhig gis dbang chog de'i steng nas dbang bskur byas chog pa dang / karma sha
taM lta bu'i steng nas sdom pa thob la ma nyams pa'i mkhan po zhig gis las chog go chod po gang yang rung ba zhig gi steng nas sdom pa phog pas chog pa zhig ste/ snyan
brgyud yi ger bris pa thams cad la 'dis mtshon no zhes zer ro/ /de ni ma brtags pa'i lan te/ su zhig gis byas par ma nges pa'i chog bsgrigs kyi yi ge de chos rje khu dbon
tsam gyi rjes su byung na ni de'i steng nas cho ga byas pa'i phyir gsung bgros dang bcas

pa'i nges pa yong ba rigs pa la med pa'i phyir dang / rjes phyi mo nas byung ba yin na rtsa ba med pa'i yan lag yang mi rigs pa'i phyir dang / bar skabs der phyag dpe 'di la
rten bya ba tsam yang ma byung bas mi 'thad pa'i phyir dang / snyan brgyud yin zhes pa yang gyi na tsam yin te/ rje nA ro pa'i lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga /birWa pa'i
lugs kyi snyan brgyud du smra ba bzhad gad kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir/ bde kyai gnyis kyi dbang gi sngon du yi ge de dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed byed ces pa yang / sngags
sdom gyi sngon du byang sdom dgos pa'i bstan pa spyi'i babs 'gros kyi smra ba la brten nas bsgrigs pa ste/ de ltar na byang sdom gyi sngon du so thar dgos pas/ skabs der
gsol bzhi'i cho ga la brten pa'i bsnyen rdzogs re yang mdzad pa zhu cig des na sambu Ti las/ skyabs su 'gro ba'i rim pa yis/ /shin tu legs par sbyangs nas ni/ /sngags dang
rgyud kyi rim pa yis/ /gsang ba'i de kho na nyid bsgrag /zhes gsungs pas dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa'i sngon du skyabs su 'gro zhing / sems bskyed pa tsam mdzad ces gsungs
mod phyag len gyi rim pa mi snang ngo / /'on kyang 'gal ba yod pa min te/ sta gon gyi skabs su 'byung bas so/ /des mi rung ba yang min te/ khrid kyi tshe ma rtogs khyed rang
yang phyag len tal ma la mi byed pa yin pas so/ /rjes 'dzin grangs nges kyi skabs su rigs sngags mkhan po na re/ spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin gyi rnam gzhag lam
'bras nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin bshad/ dang po ni spyi rgyud las/ sa'i cho ga bstan pa'i rjes

su/ las kun byed pa'i gsang sngags kyis/ /de nas slob ma yongs su bzung / /bu mo gzhon nu'i bkal ba'i skud/ /blangs nas bzhi bcu rtsa dgu bzlas/ /slob ma rnams ni blos bsam
nas/ /mnyam par gzhag pas mdud pa bor/ /de ltar slob ma yongs bzung na/ /las la bgegs ni med par 'gyur/ /zhes pa slob ma rjes 'dzin dngos bstan/ /ces dang / mkhas pas slob
ma gcig gam gsum/ /zhes pa nas/ sta gon gnas par brtsams par bya/ /zhes pa'i bar gyis slob ma'i grangs dang lus kyi spyod lam bstan/ ces pa dang / gnyis pa ni dbang chur
dbang bskur don du gnyer ba'i slob ma la/ sngags gsang sngags la zhugs pa dang / theg chen gyi sgor zhugs pa dang / zhes sogs lugs srol tha dad du brjod nas/ rgol ba khyod
kyi rjes bzung ni lag len de bshad ma thag pa gnyis po gang yin/ zhes skyon brjod nas kho bo cag gi rjes 'dzin gyi rnam gzhag rje btsun gong mas bshad pa de ltar 'dod
la/ zhes pa dang / de lta na yang dbang chu'i dngos bstan dang 'gal lo snyam pa'i tsher ma khong du sbed dgos pa ma yin te/ der grangs nges bshad pa de spyi khyab tu sbyar
mi dgos pas nyes pa de shin tu spangs pa'i phyir ro/ /ji ltar na lung dang rigs pa gnyis kyi sgo nas so/ lung ni rnam snang mngon byang las/ gcig gnyis bzhi las lhag
kyang rung / /spyad mi dgos par bzung bar bya/ /zhes dang / slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan pas sems can gyi khams ma lus pa bsgral ba'i dbang du byas te/ byang chub

kyi rgyur 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir slob ma tshad med pa bzung bar bya'o/ /zhes dang / de dbang bskur la grangs nges mi dgos pa'i dmigs gsal lo snyam na/ gcig shes kyang dbang
bskur la grangs nges dgos pa'i dmigs gsal lo/ /min te/ slob dpon rin po ches dbang chur/ rjes 'dzin gyi skabs su drangs pas so zhe na/ drangs ma thag pa'i lung phyi ma
de yang 'phags pa'i brtag gnyis kyi TIkka snying po gsal bar/ rjes 'dzin gyi skabs su drangs pas kun tu mtshungs so/ /zhes dang / rigs pa ni rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang
slob ma re re nas byed pa de'i tshe'ang maNDal 'bul ba dang gsol ba gdab pa sogs slob ma ji tsam yod pa thams cad kyi cig car du bya rung bar bshad pa'i rigs pas so/ /dbang
bskur la grangs nges yod kyang / rjes 'dzin gyi tshe de ma byas pa la nyes pa med par shes pa yin/ zhes dang / kho bo cag gi rang lugs ni/ 'phags pa rin po che'i rtsa
rgyud kyi TIkka dang / spyi rgyud dgongs pas grangs nges yod pa dang / rnam snang mngon byang gi dgongs pas grangs nges med pa gnyis char slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi skabs 'di
nyid du bshad pas/ gnyis ka ltar yang mi 'gal ba nyid du 'dod do zhes lan 'debs par mdzad do/ /legs par rna ba bklags te gsan pa zhu/ spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin
gyi rnam gzhag de khyod la med par thal/ ji skad du bshad pa'i lag len de dag khyod la med pa'i phyir/ rtags gsal dngos/ lam 'bras nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin gyi rnam gzhag
de khyod la med par thal/ ji skad du bshad pa'i grangs nges

kyi rnam gzhag de dag khyod la med pa'i phyir/ rjes 'dzin la grangs nges kyi rnam gzhag 'thad par thal/ 'phags pa'i rtsa rgyud kyi TIkka dang / spyi rgyud kyi dgongs pas grangs
nges yod pa de khyod 'dod pa'i phyir/ yang rjes 'dzin la grangs nges kyi rnam gzhag mi 'thad par thal/ rnam snang mngon byang gi dgongs pas grangs nges med pa de khyod
'dod pa'i phyir/ spyir rgyud sde las bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin la grangs nges kyi rnam gzhag mi 'thad par thal/ rgyud sde las bshad pa'i grangs nges yin na dbang bskur gyi
grangs nges yin pas khyab pa gang zhig dbang bskur gyi grangs nges yin na rjes 'dzin gyi grangs nges min dgos pa'i phyir dang / spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i grangs nges de
rjes 'dzin gyi grangs nges min pa'i phyir dang / dbang chu nas bshad pa'i grangs nges de rjes 'dzin gyi grangs nges min pa'i phyir dang / rnam snang mngon byang gi lung des
kyang rgyud sde gsum la grangs nges yod pa bkag pa'i phyir te/ des kyai rdor gyi rjes 'dzin la grangs nges yod pa bkag pa gang zhig bde mchog sogs la mtshungs pa'i phyir/
'phags pa rin po che'i rtsa rgyud kyi TIkka yod par ma grags shing / dkar chag snga rting rnams su yang ma byung bas/ gzhan zhig gi 'phags pa'i mtshan sbyar ba'am/ khyod
rang gis med bzhin du mthong ba kho na yin no/ /gzhan yang khyod kyis spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin 'chad pa'i skabs su/ skabs 'dir grangs nges yod pa'i dmigs bsal yang ma
byung bas mi 'thad la/ zhes dang grangs nges med pa'i shes byed du 'phags pa'i rtsa

rgyud kyi TIkkar rnam snang mngon byang gi lung drangs pa bkod pa dang / yang 'phags pa'i rtsa rgyud TIkka dang spyi rgyud dgongs pas grangs nges yod pa dang / rnam snang mngon
byang gi dgongs pas grangs nges med pa gnyis ka slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi skabs su 'dir bshad pas mi 'gal ba nyid du 'dod do/ /zhes gsungs na/ 'di lta bu'i 'gal ba'i khur
chen gyis dub par ma gyur tam/ rang nyid kyis smras pa'i rigs sngags kyis bcings par gsal lo/ /des na/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor la/ /slob ma grangs nges med par
gsungs/ /lhag ma dmigs bsal ma mdzad pa'i/ /slob ma la ni grangs nges yod/ /'di ni gsang ba spyi rgyud las/ /mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /lnga 'am yang na bdun dag
gam/ /nyi shu rtsa ni lnga yi bar/ /zung du ma gyur slob ma gzung / /de bas lhag pa'i slob ma ni/ /yongs su gzung ba mi shis so/ /de'i rgyu mtshan/ de bas lhag pa'i slob
ma la/ /cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ /mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nus/ /de yi mtshan mo ma tshar na/ /cho ga nyams pa rgyal bas gsungs/ /nyams na cir 'gyur zhe na/ dpal
ldan dam pa dang po las/ cho ga nyams pa'i byin rlabs kun/ /bgegs kyis yin par rgyal bas gsungs/ /yin pas ci to snyam na/ bgegs kyis bsod nams ma lus mdzad par byed/ /ces
dang / rje btsun gyi slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga dang / de smin par bya ba dbang bskur ba'i mngon rtogs so/ /dang po ni rgyud 'di las gsal po tsam ma gsungs kyang
/ slob mas gsol ba btab pa

ni/ sambu Ti las/ slob mas pus mo'i lha nga ni/ /sa la dad pas btsugs nas ni/ /thal mo sbyar nas bstod pa yis/ /ston pa la ni zhu bar bya/ /zhes dang / de ltar cho ga rgyud
gsum du mi gsal ba rnams/ ji ltar de nyid bsdus pa yis/ /dkyil 'khor cho ga de bzhin bya/ /zhes bshad pa de nyid bsdus pa dang / gsang ba spyi rgyud las rtogs par bya'o/
zhes dang / rje sa paN gyis/ gang du las ni yod gyur la/ /las kyi cho ga rnams med pa/ /de ni spyi yi rgyud dag las/ /gsungs pa'i cho ga mkhas pas bsten/ /ces sogs mtha'
yas pa gsungs la/ sngar khyed kyis drangs pa'i rnam snang mngon byang gi lung de ni spyod rgyud kyi lugs la grangs nges mi dgos pa'i khungs yin zhing / spyi rgyud kyi lung
ni rgyud sde gzhan gsum la grangs nges dgos pa'i lung yin na/ 'di 'dra ba'i lung sbyor ni sa skya pa'i rjes su 'jug bzhin du rgyud sde phan tshun dkrugs par zad do/ /gzhan
yang spyi rgyud las/ slob ma rjes su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas der med na ni/ /de yi gzugs brnyan byas nas ni/ /ji skad gsungs pa'i las rnams bya/ /zhes gsungs pa
nyid kyang slob ma brgya stong grangs med la dus gcig tu rjes 'dzin gyi cho ga byed pa bkag pa yin te/ dbang bskur gyi grangs kha tshang ba'i phyir/ rjes bzung tshe'i dus
