stong tsam ma yin par bgrang ba las 'das ba'i bar du 'phel nas rim pa rim par bar cung zad tsam yang chad pa med par brgyud de 'ongs pa'i gsung rab dag la/ rang gi blos
sbyar ba'i grub pa'i mtha' nyi tshe ba dag dang mi mthun pa rgyu mtshan du byas nas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor thal mos g.yogs pa ltar sun 'byin pa'i tshig gis 'gog par byed do/
/de la thal mo'i grib ma la gnas pa'i skye bo phra mo 'ga'

zhig kyang de dang mthun par sems par byed mod kyi/ de dag ni de ltar ma yin te/ de la bzhi/ gdan gyi rnam gzhag sa chen gyi bkar bsgrub pa dang / gzhal yas khang gi gsal byed
slob dpon rin po che'i bkar bsgrub pa dang / de kho na nyid gsum gyi man ngag dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis dkri ba'i gzhung shing rje btsun gyi bkar bsgrub pa
dang / khrid kyi dkar chag sa paN gyi bkar bsgrub pa'o/ /dang po ni/ rjes 'brang kha cig rang gis bzhag pa'i kyai rdo rje'i zhabs kyi bzhugs lugs dang gzhung 'di nyid 'gal
bar mthong ste/ ha shang gis dgongs pa nges 'grel gyi mdo bltas pa ltar/ rnam par dag pa ma yin par smra'o/ /de ni shin tu mi rigs te/ rje btsun gyi dngos slob dkar shAkya
grags kyi dag ldan las/ gzugs khams kyi tshangs pa phyed krung gis mnan pa ni/ gti mug la zung 'jug ngo bo nyid kyi rgya/ stong gsum gyi bdag po drag po dbang phyug
chen po g.yas brkyangs pas mnan pa ni/ 'dod chags gsal ba la zhe sdang stong pa'i rgya/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi bdud sdig can g.yon bskums pas mnan pa ni/ zhe sdang stong
pa la 'dod chags gsal ba'i rgya/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi dbang po yum gyi zhabs g.yon pas mnan pa ni/ nga rgyal dang 'dod chags 'bras bu la rgyu'i rgya'o/ /zhes gdan gyi
rnam dag ji lta ba bzhin du bzhag pas/ de nyid rnam dag yin par grub pa'i phyir dang / 'phags pa rin po ches kyang / zhabs mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs shing g.yon bskums
pa/ rgyab gnyis gar stabs kyis bzhugs

pa/ zhes gsungs pa'ang gzhung 'di'i don yin pas tshad mar mdzad par grub pa'i phyir dang / ding sang yan chad kyi dpal ldan sa skya pa rjes 'brang dang bcas pa'i kyai rdo rje
man ngag lugs kyi ras bris bzhengs sku sogs mthong ba kun la 'dir bshad pa'i bzhugs tshul kho na ltar snang bas de dag kun kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar byed pa 'grub pa'i
phyir dang / khyad par khyed rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i gur rigs bsdus kyi sgrub thabs su bzhugs tshul 'di kho na ltar bshad pa'i
phyir dang / grub chen buddha shrIs thugs dam ras bris la yang bzhugs tshul 'di bzhin du yod par grags pas bla ma de dag kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar byed pa gsal ba'i phyir
dang / gang zag de tsam gyi tshad mar byas pas tshad mar mi 'gyur na/ ha cang thal ba las kyang ches thal ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /yang 'di la rjes 'brang kha cig na re/
slob dpon rin po ches mtsho skyes 'grel par/ de dag kyang mnyam par brtsegs pa'i snying khar zhabs g.yas gnyis kyis mnan pa'o/ /rol mo'i tshul ni skyil krung phyed pa'o
zhes dang / mtsho skyes dbang chog tu/ bdud bzhi brtsegs pa'i gdan la zhabs g.yas gnyis brkyangs g.yon gnyis bskum pa'i gar stabs kyis bzhugs pa zhes gsungs pa'i bzhugs
tshul 'di dang mi mthun pa'i phyir rnam par ma go zhes smra ba grag go /de ni lugs so sor ma phyed pa'i babs bcol yin te/ lugs de dag mtsho skyes kyi dgongs 'grel yin pa'i
phyir dang / gnyis ka'i thun mong ba yang yod mod kyi/ bzhugs tshul mi

mthun par mngon rtogs rgyas pa'i lung gis grub pas/ 'phags bsgrub kyi skabs su 'chad pa ltar yin pa'i phyir ro/ /yang rjes 'brang kha cig na re/ mngon rtogs rgyas pa mtsho
skyes dang tshul mtshungs pas nged kyi bzhag pa'i bzhugs tshul 'di rigs pa yin no zhes smra ba grag go /de ltar na gdan gyi rnam dag las byung ba'i bzhugs tshul 'di lta bu
yang mi 'dod bzhin du khas len dgos te/ rin chen 'bar ba las/ nyi mar zhabs g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskums/ lhag ma gar gyi tshul gyis bzhengs/ /zhes gsungs shing / mngon
rtogs 'bring po Dombhi ba dang mtshungs pa'i phyir ro/ /de la gzhan dag na re/ zla zer las/ a bhyas skyil krung phyed pa dang / g.yon bskums g.yas brkyangs dang / rin chen
'bar bar g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskums/ lhag ma gar gyi tshul du bshad pa'i don yang mdun ma gnyis g.yas pa'i brla la g.yon bskums sor mo sbyar ba dang / lhag ma rgyab ma
gnyis mdun ma lta bu'i gar stabs so zhes 'bru bsnan du rung na/ slob dpon thams cad dgongs pa gcig par 'gyur pas shin tu legs kyi/ gzhan du na slob dpon 'di gnyis mi mkhas
par thal ba'i skyon yod de/ rgyud dang mi mthun pa'i phyir ro zhes 'byung bas bzhugs tshul mthun par sbyor bas skyon med do zhe na/ shin tu mi 'thad de/ mdun rgyab gnyis
bzhugs stabs mthun pa la dum bur byas nas mi mthun pa'i tshig gis bstan pa la dgos pa ci zhig yod/ gzhan dag 'gog pa'i tshig gi zol gyis mi mkhas par thal skyon 'phangs
nas rje btsun gong ma rjes 'brang dang

bcas pa 'gog pa la ngal ba du mas 'bad par zad pa'i phyir ro/ /yang kha cig na re/ 'di'i thad du dag ldan las/ dbang phyug dang de las che ba gsum dang bcas pa nyid kyi gdan
du mdzad/ zhes gsungs pa la/ 'dir dbang po dang / nye dbang gnyis drag po las chung bar bshad pas dag ldan dang 'gal ba'i phyir rnam par ma dag go zhe na/ de ni shin tu
mi 'thad de/ dag ldan nyid las/ bcom ldan 'das kyi gdan tshangs pa ni/ gzugs kyi khams kyi tshangs pa'o/ /dbang po ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi brgya byin/ nye dbang gzhan 'phrul
dbang byed kyi bdud sdig can no/ /drag po ni 'jigs byed do/ /zhes dbang po dang nye dbang drag po las chung bar bshad pa'i phyir/ gzhung de yang mi 'thad par thal ba'i
phyir dang / 'dod na/ dag ldan bkag nas sa skya par khas 'ches ba 'gal ba'i khur chen po khyer ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /'o na rje btsun gyi gsung de ji ltar 'chad ce na/
de ni lugs tha dad pa gnyis bkod pa yin pas/ bla ma'i man ngag gis phye ste bshad dgos pa yin no/ /gdan gyi rnam gzhag 'di bla ma 'ga' zhig gi rje btsun gyis mdzad par bzhed
la/ de lta na yang 'gal ba yod pa ma yin no/ gdan gyi rnam gzhag bkar bsgrubs pa bstan zin to// ! //gnyis pa gzhal yas khang gi gsal byed slob dpon rin po che'i bkar
bsgrubs pa ni/ rjes 'brang kha cig rang gis bzhag pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshad kyi rnam par gzhag pa dang gzhung 'di nyid 'gal bar mthong ste/ hwa shang gi dgongs 'grel ltar
'dir yang smra bar

byed do/ /de yang shin tu mi 'thad de/ chos rje bla ma dam pas rje btsun yab sras gsum bka' 'bum bsgrigs pa'i srol thog mar phye ba de'i nang du ma chug kyang / theg chen chos
rjes phyag dpe la 'di nyid kyi mjug tu/ 'di la phyi mo du ma snang na yang / bka' 'bum snga ma rnams su ma chug kyang / phyis sgo rum dpe khang nas kyang bla dpe rnying
pa byung ba mthong nas yid ches par byas nas bka' 'bum phyi ma rnams su bzhugs su gsol ba yin no/ /zhes gsungs pas tshad ma yin par nges pa'i phyir dang / khyed rang ltar
na yang bstan bcos 'di rje btsun chen po dang sa paN gyi slob ma zhang bya ru bas byas pa yin no zhes smra bar grag cing / gong ma'i yi ger mi gsal ba rjes 'brang gi
yi ge rnams su bshad pa la tshad mar byed do zhes kyang zer ba grag pas/ dkyil 'khor gyi tshad 'chad pa na yi ge 'di tshad mar byed dgos pa'i phyir dang / tshad mar mi byed
na gzhan gsum brtsegs su byed pa'i sa skya pa yab sras rjes 'brang sus kyang khungs cung zad tsam yang med pa'i phyir dang / zhang bya ru bas khrid kyi sngon 'gro mi byed
pa la tshad mar byed la/ skabs 'di la tshad mar byar mi rung ba'i don mthun gyi rgyu mtshan ci yang med pa'i phyir ro/ /yang kha cig yi ge 'dir brtsig pa thams cad rgya
dpangs mnyam par bshad pas pha gu sogs brtsegs/ gzhan yang yod pa'i phyir/ spyir rgya dpangs mnyam pa de la med pas tshad ma yin no zhes smra ba grag go /de yang ma yin
te/ pha gu sogs brtsegs de dag phyi rol du snang ba yin gyi/ nang du dpangs la mi 'phar ba gnad khong du ma chud

pa'i smra ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /gzhal yas khang gi gsal byed bkar bsgrub pa bshad zin to// //gsum pa de kho na nyid kyi man ngag dang / dang po rab 'bring gsum gyi dkri ba'i
gzhung shing rje btsun gyi bkar bsgrub pa la gnyis/ dbang po de kho na nyid gsum gyi man ngag bkar bsgrub pa ni/ rjes 'brang kha cig bzlas pa'i skabs su 'phags pa rin
po ches bzhag pa'i phar 'khor la sogs pa'i bzlas pa'i man ngag bkag pa las/ yi ge 'di nyid du phar 'khor shin tu gsal bar bshad pas rang gi smra ba 'di nyid ma brtan dogs
nas yi ge 'di la bskur pa btab pa yin no/ /de yang shin tu mi 'thad de/ rje btsun gyis/ smin byed ltung ba'i rnam gzhag sgrub thabs bzhi/ zhes sogs kyi gzhung 'di rnams
yig cha'i grangs ston pa'i gsung yin pa'i phyir/ rdo rje dril bu bgrang phreng dgang blugs dang / zhes pa 'dis kyang lag len gyi yi ge dag ston dgos pa'i phyir dang / lag
tu blang ba'i chos gzhan rnams la yi ge yod la/ 'di la med pa la rgyu mtshan ci yang med pa'i phyir dang / rgyud 'grel na yod pas der kha 'phangs pa yin na yi ge gzhan rnams
la'ang mtshungs pa'i phyir dang / de dag bshad pa tsam dang lag len du sgrig pa'i khyad par yod na 'di la yang mtshungs pa'i phyir dang / yi ge'i grangs ston pa ma yin
par/ las dang po pa sogs la dgos pa sgrigs nas ston pa tsam yin na/ bris sku dang glegs bam la sogs pa shin tu mang ba 'chad dgos pas nyung ba'i phyir dang / ye shes dang
dam tshig gi rdo rje dril bu go nor bas rnam

gzhag ma yin na/ gnad kyi gsal byed du/ yang na ye shes ni rnam pa lnga ste/ rdo rje 'dis rtse mo lnga pa'i rnam par dag pa'ang shes par 'gyur ro/ /zhes bla ma rnams gsungs
so/ /zhes dpyad pa'i 'grel pa de yang rnam dag ma yin par 'gyur ba'i phyir dang / gnad kyi gsal byed du/ lha'i rnam dag sbyar ba dang mi mthun pas ma yin na/ dbang chu chen
mor/ de la de bzhin gshegs pa lnga dang / yum lnga dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / lha mo la sogs pa rdo rje'i de kho na nyid ltar yongs su rdzogs par mos pa bskyed
la/ zhes gsungs pas dbang chu de yang rnam dag ma yin par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir rngog pa'i rjes 'brang dag gi yi ge'o zhes 'chad pa ni/ gzhan rang gi tshig la
yid ches bskyed par byed pa'i zol tsam mo/ /gnyis pa dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyi dkri ba'i gzhung shing bkar bsgrub pa ni/ rjes 'brang kha cig gi dang por lam 'bras kyi
sngon 'gro'i tshig bkag pas/ phyis su yi ge 'di nyid dang 'gal bar mthong ste/ rang gi grub pa'i mtha' la mi gnod par bya ba'i phyir/ rje btsun gyi gsung ma yin zhes dgag
pa brjod par byed mod/ de yang shin tu mi 'thad de/ rje btsun gyi dkar chag gi yi ge las/ 'o na glegs bam dang dkar chag 'di ci'i phyir bri zhe na/ gzhan don 'ba' zhig
gi phyir te/ 'ga' zhig ci zin zin gyi ngan rtog bris te khyer nas 'ong pa yang mthong / 'ga' zhig rje bla mas ma mdzad par mdzad do zer ba yang mthong / glegs bam 'di nyid
kyi nang du rang gi ngan rtog bcug pa'ang mthong nas brtse ba'i phyir dkar chag tu

btab pa 'di las/ glegs bam 'dir rang gi ngan rtog gis bslad pa gang yang gzhug par mi bya'o/ /gal te rang dran pa gso ba'i zin bris byed na yang logs su zhog cig ces gsungs
pas/ yi ge lhag yod med rnams legs par phye nas rnam par gzhag pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs/ mkhas grub kyi slob ma rgya mtsho dang 'dra ba shin tu mang ba rnams la bshad
cing tshims par mdzad/ de nas ding sang gi bar du gang zag dam pa gzhal gyi mi lang ba dang / yi ge rigs gzhal gyi mi lang bar rim par brgyud de thos bsam bsgom pa'i
brgyud pa bar ma chad pa chen po 'dir/ nyin mor byed pa'i dkyil 'khor shar ba ltar 'ong pa 'di la su zhig gis snyon 'dings par nus blo dang ldan pa dag gis mthong na rang
gi gnas lugs go bar byed pa yin pa'i phyir dang / sa paN gyi khrid kyi dkar chag tu tshad mar bzhag cing / bla ma dam pas kyang gzhung shing bzhi'i khrid yig tu tshad mar
bzhag pa'i phyir dang / de dag kyang yi ge tsam ma yin par nyams khrid du lag len bar ma chad par yod pa'i phyir dang / de tsam gyis kyang tshad mar mi 'gyur na/ go ba
nyid kyis chog pa'i phyir ro/ /der ma zad rjes 'brang de dag gis 'di 'dra ba yang byas par snang / rje btsun gyi dkar chag las gzhung shing bzhi'i khrid kyi yi ge yod par
bshad cing / sngar gyi yi ge rnying pa de bkag pas/ de'i hor stong bsab pa'i don du rang blos sbyar ba'i dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyi dkri ba'i gzhung shing gi yi ge byas
te/ 'di skad du/ thabs kyi phyogs dang / shes rab kyi

phyogs dang / zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa gsum mo/ dang po la rigs gsum/ tha ma tshogs tsam bsog pa/ 'bring las tshogs bsgrub pa/ rab bskyed rim bsgom pa'o/ /shes rab kyi phyogs
la gsum/ tha ma lta ba tsam la blo gnas pa/ 'bring bskyed rim la sems 'dzin par 'dod pa/ rab rlung gi rnal 'byor bsgom pa'o/ /gsum pa gang zag gi rnal 'byor pa la gsum/
dang po bzlas brjod dang sbyin sreg gis rgyud sbyangs/ 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag pa/ rab man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig gi lam khrid zhes bkod nas rnal 'byor pa grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyis sbyar ba'o zhes bris te/ sgo rum dpe khang nas brnyed do zhes zer ro/ /de ni ches shin tu mi 'thad de/ de 'dra ba'i yi ge khyed rang yan chad kyi
mkhas rmongs kyi gang zag su la yang ma grags pa'i phyir dang / grags na lam 'bras ji ltar dar ba ltar yi ge de yang dar te rnying pa mang du mthong dgos pa las re re tsam
yang ma mthong ba'i phyir dang / don la skyon cher gnas te/ thabs shes rab kyi phyogs su lhung ba'i rnal 'byor pas/ blang bya de dag nyams su blangs pa las/ rim gyis
zung 'jug la blo kha phyogs pa'i rgyur 'gyur ba gcig dgos pa las/ don de la phan pa'i lam ci yang mi snang ba'i phyir dang / yang na rang gang la mos pa'i lam de bsgom pa
ston dgos pa las de yang mi snang ba'i phyir dang / gal te sgo rum dpe khang nas brnyed pa bden srid na'ang / de la tshig don gang gi brgyud pa yang med pas ding sang lung
sogs 'chad pa ha cang bzhad gad chen po yin pa'i phyir

ro/ /'di dag gi dgag bsgrub zhib par kho bos logs su bris yod pas der blta bar bya'o/ /de kho na nyid gsum gyi man ngag dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis dkri ba'i gzhung
shing bkar bsgrub pa bshad zin to// //bzhi pa khrid kyi dkar chag sa paN gyi bkar bsgrub pa ni/ rjes 'brang kha cig sngon 'gro'i khrid bkag pa dang / pho brang drug tu
'dod pa ni gnyug ma dran gsal gyi lugs bsres pa yin no/ /zhes pho brang drug pa 'dod pa bkag pa dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis dkri ba'i gzhung shing gi yi ge rnying
pa dag bkag pas/ yi ge 'dir de dag gsal bar bshad pa'i phyir dang / rang gi grub pa'i mtha' la gnod par dogs pa'i bsam pas dgag pa brjod par byed mod/ de yang ches shin
tu mi 'thad de/ yi ge 'di nyid kyi gsal byed zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi zin bris yod pa'i phyir dang / bla ma dam pas kyang gzhung shing bzhi'i yi ger thun grangs
sogs yi ge 'di tshad mar byas nas bshad pa'i phyir dang / khyad par du brgyud pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang bar/ thun mong ma yin pa la khrid kyi dkar chag zhes mtshan
nas smos nas tshad mar bzhag pa'i phyir dang / tshogs bsgom rin po che'i slob ma nyan chen pa dang / gnyag snying po rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i gzhung ji lta ba bzhin
dkri ba'i khrid yig tu/ thog mar khrid kyi sngon 'gro dang thun gyi sngon 'gro rnams bstan nas/ de ma thag tu snang ba gsum gyi khrid bstan pas/ tshogs bsgom pa dpon
slob rnams kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar byas nas

gsungs pa grub pa'i phyir dang / chos rje gzungs pas bla ma klu pa la gnang ba'i dris lan du/ yi ge 'di tshad mar byas te lan mdzad pas gang zag dam pa de tsam zhig gis tshad
mar mdzad pas tshad mar mi 'grub na ha cang thal ba'i phyir dang / pho brang drug pa ni rje btsun gyi gdan sogs kyi yi ger/ pho brang lnga'am drug gi dbus ma de sangs
rgyas dang rig ma'i gdan/ zhes gsungs pa ma mthong bar zad pa'i phyir dang / de'i phyir gnyug ma dran gsal gyi lugs 'dres par smra ba ni rje btsun la dgag pa byed par snang
ba'i phyir dang / rje btsun bkag nas sa skya pa'i rjes 'brang du rlom pa ni gad mo'i gnas yin pa'i phyir dang / rje btsun gyi gsung de'i gsal byed du yi ge 'di med na
pho brang drug pa'i gnas tshul dang / bsgom tshul gang yang shes pa ma yin te/ yi ge gzhan du gsal bar ma bstan pas khyed cag gis mi shes pa'i phyir dang / de'i phyir yi
ge 'dir bstan pa'i zab pa'i gnas du ma dag las ring du gyur pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de ltar na khyed kyi smra ba 'di dag la ni/ dpal ldan sa skya paNDi tas/ 'di ni sangs rgyas
bstan pa la/ /bdud tshig yin pas rna ba dgag /zhes gsungs pa de dran par bya ba 'os pa'o/ /khrid kyi dkar chag bkar bsgrub pa bstan zin to/ /bsgrub pa rnam pa bzhi las
bka' bsgrub bstan pa'i le'u ste dang po'o/ /zhes pa de rnams kyi sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin rdzong lugs pa rnams kyi gtsug rgyan dam pa mtshungs med mus srad pa rdo rje
rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i bsgrub pa rnam bzhi'i nang tshan bka' bsgrub gsung rab las 'byung tshul bshad zin

nas// ! //gnyis pa de nyid kyi rtsod spong glo bo mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i bstan bcos las 'byung tshul bshad pa ni/ chos kyi rje mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i mdzad pa'i bka' bsgrub kyi rtsod spong gi yi ge tshig don mun sel zhes
bya ba las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ oM 'grub par gyur cig kun bzang gsung gi 'od zer gyis/ /cha shas shin tu phra mo yang / /phrag dog mig gi mi bzod pa'i/ /'khrul pa'i 'chal
gtam 'di skad lo/ /rjes 'brang kha cig rang gis bzhag pa'i kyai rdo rje'i zhabs kyi bzhugs lugs dang gzhung de nyid 'gal bar mthong ste/ ha shang gi dgongs pa nges 'grel
gyi mdo bltas pa ltar rnam par dag pa ma yin par smra 'o/ /zhes phyogs snga ma bkod pa'i lugs su byas nas/ de la dkar shAkya grags kyis mdzad pa'i dag ldan dang / 'phags
pa rin po ches/ zhabs mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs zhing g.yon bskum pa/ rgyab ma gnyis gar stabs kyi bzhugs pa zhes gsungs pa dang / ding sang yan chad kyi dpal ldan
sa skya pa rjes 'brang dang bcas pa'i kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi bris sku dang bzhengs sku sogs mthong ba kun 'dir bshad pa'i bzhugs tshul kho na ltar snang bas de dag
kun kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar byed par grub pa'i phyir dang / khyad par khyed rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i gur rigs bsdus kyi sgrub
thabs su bzhugs tshul 'di kho na ltar bshad

pa dang / grub chen buddha shrI'i thugs dam ras bris la yang bzhugs tshul 'di bzhin du yod par grags pas bla ma de dag kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar byed pa gsal ba'i phyir dang
/ gang zag de tsam gyis tshad mar byas pas tshad mar mi 'gyur na ha cang thal ba las kyang ches thal ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /zhes dang / rjes 'brang kha cig slob dpon rin
po ches mtsho skyes 'grel par de dag kyang mnyam par brtsegs pa'i snying khar zhabs g.yas pa gnyis kyi mnan pa'o/ /rol mo'i tshul ni skyil krung phyed pa'o zhes dang /
mtsho skyes dbang chog tu/ bdud bzhi brtsegs pa'i gdan la zhabs g.yas gnyis brkyangs/ g.yon gnyis bskum pa'i gar stabs kyis bzhugs pa zhes gsungs pas/ bzhugs tshul 'di dang
mi mthun pa'i phyir rnam par ma dag go zhes smra bar grag go zhes man ngag gi gsal byed las bshad pa de 'gog pa'i lugs su byas nas lugs so sor ma phyed pa yin no zhes
dang / rin chen 'bar bar lhag ma gar gyi tshul du bshad pa'i don yang / mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs pa'i brla la g.yon bskum gyis sor mo sbyar ba dang lhag ma rgyab ma gnyis
mdun ma 'di zla zer na med lta bu'i gar stabs so zhes 'bru gnon du rung na slob dpon thams cad dgongs pa gcig par 'gyur bas shin tu legs kyi/ gzhan du na slob dpon 'di
gnyis mi mkhas par thal ba'i skyon yod de rgyud dang mi mthun pa'i phyir ro zhe na/ shin tu mi 'thad de/ mdun rgyab gnyis bzhugs stabs mthun pa la dum bur byas nas mi
mthun pa'i tshig gis bstan pa la dgos pa ci zhig yod ces zer

zhing / tshig ngan gyi me rtse yang ston par byed do/ /'di dag la sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rnal por yod cing / dus ngan pa ma shar ba'i skabs su lan bya bar 'os pa ma yin yang
/ ding sang rtog dpyod che bar byas pa rnams kyis skyes bu dam pa 'gog pa kho na la rnam dpyod kyi shes rab che bar rlom zhing skal ba dman pa'i gang zag rnams kyang
lam zab mo nyams su len pa las phyir phyogs te 'gro ba dag snang bas/ gang zag mchog la smad pa'i nyes dmigs bstan pa'i sgo nas lan gyi spros pa cung zad brjod par bya'o//de
yang skyes bu dam pa rgyal bas lung bstan pa 'di lta bu la tshul gang gi sgo nas smad kyang nyes pa shin tu che ste/ rgyal ba'i yum las/ lung bstan ma thob byang chub
sems dpa' gang zhig gis/ /lung bstan thob la sems khro rtsod pa brtsom byed na/ /tha ba skyon ldan sems kyi skad cig ji snyed pa/ /de snyed bskal par bzhin nas go cha bgo
dgos so/ /zhes gsungs pa de go bar byos shig gnyis pa lan la/ gzhi med kyi skur ba btab par bstan pa dang / gdan dang bzhugs tshul ma spros pa dpyad pa'o/ /dang po ni/
rje btsun A nanda bha dra nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bla ma gong ma gsum gyi bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag rin po che'i lde mig las/ sa chen bka' 'bum gyi nang du kyai rdo rje'i gdan
gyi dag pa zhes dngos su smos shing kyai rdo rje'i rgyud kyi byung tshul 'chad pa'i rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rgya mtsho las kyang / bcom ldan 'das kyai rdo rje zhal brgyad
phyag bcu drug pa dang / drag po'i chung ma brgyad dang ming mthun pa'i gau rI la

sogs pa'i lha mo brgyad sprul nas dbang phyug rang dang / de bas che ba gsum dang bcas pa bcom ldan 'das nyid kyi gdan du mdzad de/ dregs pa can brgyad ni lha mo brgyad kyi
gdan du byas zhes rnam bshad dag ldan du 'byung la/ gdan gyi dag pa las/ drag po'i 'khor che shos ni gtso bos mnan/ drag po rang ni ghasma ris mnan ces cung zad mi 'dra
ba'i tshig gi khyad par dang bcas nas lung du drangs shing / rje btsun kun dga' bzang po nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gsung rab gang gi nang na yang 'di tshad ldan ma yin par ston
pa'i tshig gcig kyang med la/ 'di rang la 'dis mdzad kyi mdzad byang dngos su smos pa med kyang / bka' 'bum rnams kyi nang du sa chen gyi bka' 'bum nang du sgrigs pas/
rje btsun gyi bka' 'bum du sgrigs pa ni ci rigs pa 'byung ngo / /sa skya pa chen pos mdzad byang dngos su ma smos pa shas che ba yong gin 'dug ces rje btsun kun dga' dbang
phyug gsungs shing / de las rjes su dpag nas kyang sa chen bka' 'bum du 'jug pa nyid 'thad dam bsam mo/ /yang rje btsun kun dga' bzang po nyid kyi kyai rdo rje'i mngon
par rtogs pa bsdus par yang / zhabs mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskum/ rgyab ma gnyis skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs zhes dngos su bshad cing / rje nyid kyi thugs
dam bris sku la yang chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims dang / chos rje shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi sku'i steng du bcom ldan 'das kyai rdo rje'i sku bkram/ gdan gyi tshul
gyis bzhugs pa re re rje nyid kyi zhal bkod mdzod bris yod pa'i phyir/ bkram gdan du byas

pa thams cad ma dag go zhes su zhig gis smras/ de ltar smra ba ma dag ces gsungs so zer ba gang zag su zhig las khyed kyis thos legs par smros shig da ni gnyis pa gdan dang
bzhugs tshul la spros pa cung zad dpyad na/ gdan gyi bdud bzhi ni/ rgya gzhung rnams nas mi 'dra ba mang du 'byung yang / rang rang gi bla ma grub pa thob pa rnams kyi gsung
bgros yin pa'i phyir/ 'di dag cing 'di ma dag go zhes dgag bsgrub bya bar mi nus la/ 'khrul spong gi mchod brjod las/ gtso bo'i gdan gsum pa 'jug sel te khyab 'jug la
gsungs pa yang yod pas rnam grangs mi 'dra ba cung zad yod pa la skyon du bzung bar mi bya'o/ /rje btsun sa skya pa rnams la kyai rdo rje'i bka' babs bzhi byung ba'i mtsho
skyes lugs dang / man ngag lugs kyi bzhugs tshul ni/ zhabs g.yas g.yon du gnyis gnyis mdun rgyab tu sgrigs pa'i g.yas gnyis brkyangs ba'i brla la g.yon gnyis bskum pa'i
sor mo gtad pa'i skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs kyis bzhugs pa yin te/ rje btsun rtse mos mtsho skyes lugs kyi dkyil chog la tshig 'di dngos su gsungs shing / man ngag
lugs kyi gzhung rnams las kyang / skabs 'ga' zhig tu g.yas brkyangs zhes pa tsam dang / 'ga' zhig tu skyil krung phyed pa zhes pa tsam las ma gsungs kyang / mtsho skyes
kyi sgrub thabs dang / man ngag lugs kyi yan lag bzhi drug cig car du bdud bzhi brtsegs gdan 'ba' zhig gsungs pas bzhugs tshul 'di las ma 'das pa'i phyir ro/ /gal te rje
btsun rtse mos zhabs g.yas

brkyangs pa dang / g.yon bskum pa dang / skyil krung phyed pa'i dag pa gsum po so sor gsungs pas/ mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyang zhing g.yon bskum pa dang / rgyab ma gnyis skyil
krung phyed pa'i gar stabs bstan no snyam na/ de ni ma yin te/ skyil krung phyed pa de nyid la g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskum tshangs bas de'i dag pa ston pa yin pa'i phyir
te/ mtsho skyes kyi 'grel par/ de dag kyang mnyam par brtsegs pa'i snying khar zhabs g.yas pa gnyis kyis mnan pa'o/ /rol mo'i tshul ni skyil krung phyed pa'o/ /de'i g.yas
brkyangs pa ni thugs rjes sems can la khyab pa'o/ /g.yon bskums pa ni shes rab kyis chos gang yang mi 'dzin par btang ba'o/ /zhes gsal bar gsungs pa'o/ /gzhan du na 'khor
lo bde mchog la rdo rje dang dril bu 'dzin pa'i phyag gnyis las gzhan pa'i phyag gnyis kyi yum la 'khyud dgos par 'gyur te/ rje btsun gyis rdo rje 'dzin pa dang / dril
bu 'dzin pa dang / yum la 'khyud pa'i dag pa gsum so sor gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /'grel pa lugs kyi gzhung rnams las/ g.yas brkyangs zhes pa tsam dang / skyil krung phyed
pa zhes pa tsam las gsal kha mi snang yang / rin chen 'bar bar/ nyi mar zhabs g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskum/ /lhag ma gar gyi tshul gyis bzhengs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don ni/
mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskum/ rgyab ma gnyis skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs yin par mngon te/ rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i gdan gyi rnam dag las/ gtso bo'i
zhabs phyed krung du bzhugs pas tshangs pa'i snying kha

nas mnan pa dang / zhabs g.yas brkyangs bas dbang phyug chen po'i snying kha nas mnan pa dang / g.yon bskum pas gzhan 'phrul dbang byed bdud sdig can gyi snying kha nas mnan
pa dang / yum gyi zhabs g.yon pas brgya byin snying kha nas mnan par gsungs pa yang 'di la dgongs par snang bas/ bdud bzhi bkram gdan gyi tshe yab kyi zhabs brkyangs pa
gsum dang / yum gyi zhabs g.yon brkyangs pa gcig gis bdud bzhi so sor mnan nas/ bskums pa gnyis kyis mnan rgyu med pa la bya dgos par snang ngo / /mdor na gsungs tshul so
sor gsungs pa tsam ma gtogs sbyar tshul gang la sbyar yang dag pa re sbyar rgyu yod pas 'gal ba med pa 'dra'o zhes man ngag gi gsal byed las gsungs pa 'di kho nas log par
rtog pa sel bar nus la/ ku mu ti las/ khro bo'i phyag rgya 'chad pa'i skabs su phyag rgya yang bshad par bya ste/ g.yas kyi zhabs kyi brla sleb cing / g.yon pa'i zhabs
kyi rtses mnan pa/ mnan pa'am zhes pa yan khro mo'i phyag rgya yin la/ bzlog nas mnan pa ni khro bo'i phyag rgya gdan du brjod zhes pa'i tshig rkang phyed dang gnyis po
'dis khro bo'i phyag rgya dngos bstan cing / de ltar na/ bzlog nas mnan zhes pa'i don yin pas 'dir yang / g.yon pa'i zhabs kyi brla sleb cing / /g.yas pa'i zhabs kyi rtses
mnan pa/ /zhes sbyar dgos pas zhabs g.yas brkyangs ba'i brla la g.yon pa'i sor mo sleb cing / g.yas pa'i zhabs kyi rtses bdud bzhi'i snying khar mnan pa shin du gsal bar
gsungs pa dang / yang rje btsun kun

bzang gis/ kyai rdo rje bcu bdun ma'i mngon rtogs su/ lung 'di yab yum gnyis ka'i khro bo'i phyag rgya 'dam kha can du'ang zhes pa'i tshig la brten nas mdzad cing / yab la'ang
g.yon gnyis bskums pa'i skyil krung phyed pa mdzad do/ /rje btsun gyi 'khrul spong du yang / gang gi mtshungs med bde chen zhabs padmo/ /tshangs dbang 'jug sel drag po'i
gtsug gis mchod/ srid zhi'i dgrar gyur de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes gsungs pa 'dis kyang bzhugs tshul 'di kho na thon cing / mi thub zla ba nyid kyi yan lag drug par
yang / bdud bzhi'i snying kha nyams dga'i gnas su sems can don mdzad dgos/ zhes bdud bzhi kha'i snying kha zhabs kyis mnyam par mnan pa 'di legs par grub pa'i phyir ro/ /sgyi
chu ba'i dka' 'grel las kyang / gzhal yas khang de'i dbus su pad nyi'i steng du gtso bo bdud bzhi brtsegs pa'i gdan zhes gsal bar gsungs so/ /des na man ngag lugs kyi
yan lag bzhi drug dang / mtsho skyes lugs la brtsegs gdan bshad par ma zad/ 'grel pa lugs kyi ku mu ti dang / yan lag drug par yang brtsegs gdan du bshad pa yod par khas
len dgos shing / rin chen 'bar ba las/ nyi mar zhabs g.yas brkyangs g.yon bskum/ /lhag ma gar gyi tshul du bzhengs/ /zhes pa'i skabs su yang zhabs mdun ma g.yas brkyangs
g.yon bskum gyis bzhugs shing / lhag ma gar stabs kyis bzhengs pa gsal bar gsungs pas/ rin chen 'bar ba dang yan lag drug pa dang / ku mu tir bshad pa yang rnam grangs
mi 'dra ba'i khyad par

cung zad yod pa la 'gal ba ci yang med do snyam du kho bo cag sems te/ snying po don gsal las/ de slad khyod zhabs phyag dang phyag mtshan gzhan dbang kho nar bdag gis 'tshal/
/zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /'on kyang lugs gcig la brten pa'i rang rang gi bla ma brgyud pa tshad ldan gyi lung dang 'gal na/ de dang de'i skabs su dgag par nus pa yin
gyi/ dgongs pa so so'i bzhed tshul gcig gis gcig la gnod par nus pa ni gtan ma yin te/ mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgor/ gzhal bya gsum pa spyod pa na/ /rang rang lung dang 'gal
na gnod/ /dper na chags sogs sdig pa dang / /chags bral chos su 'chad bzhin du/ /khrus kyi sdig pa 'dag pa dang / /'tshe ba chos su smra ba bzhin/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/
/yang ras bris la sogs pa'i sku gzugs rnying pa rnams la brtsegs gdan du byas pa 'di lta bu ma mthong ngo zhes zer ba yang / rang nyid kyis ma mthong ba la zer na ni
shin tu mad pa yin kyang / spyir ma mthong ba ni khegs par nus pa ma yin te/ jo bo nA ro ta pa'i thugs dam rgya gar gyi ri mo ngo bo gur rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor paN chen
shAkya shrI'i bod du bsnams byon te thar pa lo tsA ba'i dgon par bzhugs 'dug pa bdag gis mngon sum du mthong ba la yang brtsegs gdan gyi bzhugs tshul 'di pa bzhed pa
ltar yod pa dang / 'phags pa'i yul gyi he badzra'i rdo sku rnying pa la yang / dus phyis rgya gar du phyin pa'i mis dngos su mthong ste ngor pa'i lugs kyi kyai rdo rje'i
zhabs kyi bzhugs tshul 'di rgya gar na yang 'dug go

zhes rjes su sgrog pa'i phyir dang / rje btsun ga ya dha ra'i rgya dpe'i thog mar yang 'di lta bu bris yod par sa lo tsA ba gnyis pa dag gis gzigs par grags pa'i yang phyir
ro/ /des na gong du bshad pa'i dgag yul gtan med pa'i dgag pa de dag dang / de dang rjes su 'brel ba'i skyon brjod spyi btol gyi tshig dang bcas te smras 'dug pa rnams kyang
legs par ma rtogs par yin pa bshad cing / dpal ldan sa skya paNDi tas/ rang nyid mun khung zhugs nas ni/ /nyi ma'i 'od la 'khang ba ltar/ /de bzhin sdig pa'i lugs zhugs
nas/ /phan mdzad khyod la 'khang bar zad/ /ces gsungs pa yang 'di 'dra ba la dgongs pa yin par go bar byos shig yang gzhal yas khang gi gsal byed ces bya ba'i yi ge bsdus
pa gcig yod 'di 'ba' zhig tu rje btsun rtse mos mdzad bya ba dang / la la rje btsun gyis mdzad zer ba yong gin 'dug kyang / rje btsun sku mched kyis mdzad par nges pa
dang / mdzad pa ma yin par nges pa'i shes byed khungs thub pa ci yang ma mthong zhing / khyed kyi chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rje btsun yab sras gsum gyi bka' 'bum
sgrigs pa'i srol thog mar phye ba de'i nang du ma chud kyang theg chen chos rje'i phyag dpe la 'di nyid kyi mjug tu/ 'di la phyi mo du ma snang na yang / bka' 'bum snga
ma rnams su ma bcug phyis sgo rum dpe khang nas kyang bla dpe rnying pa byung ba mthong bas yid ches par byas nas bka' 'bum phyi ma rnams su bzhugs su gsol ba yin no zhes
gsungs pas tshad ma yin par nges pa'i phyir yi ger bris so/ /'di yang sgrub byed tshad ldan ma yin

te/ sgo rum gyi dpe khang na bla dpe rnying pa yod pas kyang rje btsun sku mched gang rung gis mdzad par bsgrub par mi nus/ theg chen chos rjes bka' 'bum phyi ma rnams su bcug
pas rje btsun sku mched drung gis mdzad par bsgrub mi nus te/ rtags de dag la khyab pa ye mi 'dug pa'i phyir ro/ /'on kyang gzhung 'di rgyud 'grel mtha' dag gi lung gi
lugs dang bcas nas gzhal yas khang gi gnas lugs spros pa dang bcas te sgro 'dogs dpyod pa rnam bshad zla ba'i 'od zer du bshad pa lta bu mi snang yang / sgrub pa po'i blo
la bsgom bde zhing / gnad ma 'khrugs pa zhig ni yin nam snyam mo/ /rje btsun rdo rje kun dga' bzang po'i dngos kyi slob ma dag gi gsungs las kyang / rje btsun chen po
dang sa paN gyi slob ma zhang bya ru bas byas pa'i gzhas yas khang gi rnam dag kyang yod de zhes gsung gin 'dug pa thos kyi/ yi ge 'di nyid zhang phya ru bas byas pa yin
no zhes gsungs pa ni gtan ma thos so/ /zhang bya ru ba khrid kyi sngon 'gro mi byed pa la tshad mar byed la/ skabs 'di la tshad mar byar mi rung ba'i don mthun gyi rgyu mtshan
ci yang med pa'i phyir ro zhes bris 'dug pa 'di ni zhang bya ru bas khrid kyi sngon 'gro mi byed pa'i rgyu mtshan gsal po zhig khyed kyis gsungs shig de nas de'i lan
ldon par 'gyur ro// //yang gsum pa de kho na nyid gsum man ngag dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyi dkri ba'i gzhung shing rje btsun gyi bkar bsgrub bo zer nas/ sgrub byed
ltar snang du ma 'god pa ni shin tu mi rigs te/ da lta rje btsun gyis mdzad par

grags pa'i de kho na nyid gsum gyi man ngag tu grags pa 'di rje btsun gyi dngos slob dpyil bsgom tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis rje btsun gyi gsung bgros skyor ba la rje btsun
chen po'i zhal nas/ rdo rje dang dril bu de kho na nyid ston pa'i yi ge zhig byed 'dod pa yin pa la ma grub ces gsungs par dngos su bshad 'dug pas rje btsun gyi dngos
slob 'di nyid rje btsun gyi gsung rab la rgyus che bar byed dgos so/ /des na brgyud pa 'di pa rnams ni sambu Ti'i TIka chen gyi skabs su de gzhir byas nas/ rje btsun dang
sa paN gnyis ka'i dngos slob shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas kyi mdzad pa'i rdo rje dril bu'i de kho na nyid zhib tu bshad pa de gtso che bar mdzad do/ /yang dbang po rab
'bring gsum gyi dkri ba'i gzhung shing bkar bsgrub bo zer nas/ da lta 'ga' zhig gi tshad mar byed pa'i yi ge 'di rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i bsgrub byed ltar snang du ma zhig
'god pa la ni bla ma chos rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos dpyad pa cung zad tsam mdzad pa'i yi ge'i 'di la zhib tu gzigs la lan yod na drangs por gsungs shig de yang 'di ltar
gsungs te/ gang zag gi bye brag gsum du dkri ba'i gzhung shing zhes pa 'di glegs bam phal mo cher ma tshang la/ kha cig tu/ gang zag rigs kyi dbye bas lam gyi khrid/
/brjod pas dran pa gso phyir tho tsam bri/ /zhes pa tshig yod pa'i dpe chung mang ba gcig yod pa dang / glegs bam kha cig tu shog gcig ma chung ngu bris pa ste/ mi 'dra ba
gnyis snang ba las/ dang po dpe chung mang ba 'di ni rjes 'brang kha cig gis byas pa yin gyi/ rje btsun yab

sras kyis mdzad pa ma yin te nor ba'i tshogs mang du snang ba'i phyir ro/ /de'ang de nyid las/ dang por mi mthun dgos te/ zhes yig brgya maNDal 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs bsam pa
gsum sngon du song nas/ chos bcu gnyis nyams su len par bshad la/ chos bcu gnyis kyi sngon 'gro gsum ni gong gi yig brgya la sogs pa gsum po de yin pa'i phyir/ tshig bsgrig
lugs kyang ma shes pas nang 'gal lo/ /yang des sems sgyu mar bslab ste zhes bshad pa'ang ches nor ste/ 'khor 'das dbyer med du rmi lam snang ba sems su bsgrub pa'i rtsa
ba'i dpe dang / mig yor yan lag gi dper bshad kyi/ sems sgyu mar bsgrub pa'i dper ma bshad la/ yang der gzugs brnyan la/ ! ste ces pa'i me long yang sgyu ma de rten 'brel
du bsgrub pa'i dpe yin gyi/ sems sgyu mar bsgrub pa'i dpe ma yin pas ha cang nor ces thal lo/ /yang der btson pa tha ma la/ ! rung ces pa'ang shin tu mi 'thad de/ lus
dkyil bsgom pa la de'i dbang thob dgos shing / phyi dkyil du dbang rdzogs par ma thob na lus dkyil gyi dbang tsam yang bskur du mi rung bar bshad pas/ slob ma'i dbang thob
pa tsam gyi lus dkyil bsgom pa shin tu mi rung bas nor ba'o/ /yang der brtson pa 'bring gis lam gyi thun bzhi la dbang bzhi bsgom pa dang / brtson pa rab kyi bzlas bsgom
la rten nas las kyi tshogs rab 'byams bsgrub par bshad pa'ang nor te/ lam dus len pa'i gang zag de bas las tshogs bsgrub pa'i gang zag de khyad par 'phags par 'gyur la/
'dod

na ni mchog gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i gang zag de bas thun mong gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i gang zag de khyad par 'phags par 'gyur ro/ /yang shes rab kyi phyogs su lhung ba'i brtson
pa rab kyis man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig gis 'gro ba la bshad la/ ! gong mdor bstan kyi skabs su rab rlung / ! gsum mo zhes bshad pa dang nang 'gal lo/ /yang der gang
zag gis gsungs pa'o zhes dang / zung 'jug gi ! gsungs zhes zung 'jug la rab 'bring gsum du dbye mod kyang / zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa'i lam dkri lugs gcig yod par bshad
pa la/ 'og rgyas bshad du de'i bshad pa gtan mi snang ngo / zhes tho yig chung ngu 'dir dpyad pa mdzad par snang ba 'dis don la legs par soms shig yang khyed kyis nged kyi
phyogs la rang dgar bris pa yin no zhes zer ba'i yig phreng phyed gsum tsam byas pa'i tshig rnams ni nged rang gi lugs kyi glegs bam rnams kyi nang du bris pa med cing
/ de las cung zad tsam gyi mang ba'i shog gcig ma gcig yod pa la ni theg pa thun mong ba la bslab pa dang / 'khor 'das dbyer med la bslab pa dang / gang zag rigs so so'i
'jug pa ces gsum du phye nas/ theg pa thun mong ba la nyan thos dang thun mong ba/ theg pa chen po dang thun mong ba gnyis las/ dang po la 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs/ dal 'byor
rnyed dka'/ 'chi ba mi rtag pa gsum/ gnyis pa la byams pa/ snying rje/ byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa gsum/ 'khor 'das dbyer med la chos thams cad sems/ sems sgyu mar bsgrub/
de spros

bral du thag bcad/ de la dbu ma dang mthun par dpe brgyad dam bcu gnyis kyi dkri/ zhes 'di yan gyi pha rol du phyin pa'i lam gyi dkri tshul thams cad thabs shes rab kyi dkri
tshul rdzogs par bstan nas/ theg pa chen po thun mong ma yin pa ltar rnal 'byor chen po la gang zag rigs gsum so so'i 'jug pas dkri na/ thabs kyi phyogs dang / shes rab
kyi phyogs dang / byang chub kyi zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa gsum mo/ /dang po la rigs gsum/ tha ma tshogs tsam bsog pa/ 'bring las tshogs bsgrub pa/ rab bskyed rim bsgom
pa'o/ /gnyis pa shes rab kyi phyogs la gsum/ tha ma lta ba tsam la blo gnas pa/ 'bring bskyed rim la sems 'dzin par 'dod pa/ rab rlung gi rnal 'byor bsgom pa'o/ /gsum pa
zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor la gsum/ dang po bzlas brjod sbyin sreg gis rgyud sbyangs/ 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag rab man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig gi lam khrid/ de la tha
ma bzlas brjod sbyin sreg gis rgyud sbyang ba ni bsnyen pa ji tsam song ba'i bcu cha'i sbyin sreg byed/ 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag pa ni/ rgyu dus kyi lta ba'i
dpe sum cu so bdun gyi khrid byed/ rab man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig ni/ sbyang ba khyad par can nas brtsams te sems kyi rba rlabs phan chad 'jig rten pa'i lam la gnad dgu/
'das pa'i lam la gnad bcu gcig gi dkri ba'o/ /gang zag dbang po rab 'bring gsum du dkri ba'i gzhung shing 'di slob ma rnams kyi gsol ba btab pa'i ngor rnal 'byor pa grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyis sbyar ba'o/

/zhes bris pa 'di mnga' ris gung thang gi sgo mang chen po'i phyag dpe rnying pa zhig la bris pa yang mthong zhing / 'di la theg pa thun mong ba'i dkri lugs la gnyis su byas
pa'i nyan thos dang thun mong ba la yang gang zag gsum gyi rim pas 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs tsam bstan te 'khor ba thams cad sdug bsngal gyi rang bzhin du shes nas de spong
'dod kyi blo tsam bskyed pa dang / 'khor ba spong ba la chos bsgrub pa'i rten dal 'byor brnyed par dka' bar shes nas brten te/ de la chos byed 'dod kyi blo bcos ma ma yin
par bskyed pa dang / 'chi ba mi rtag pa bsgom pas myur du brtson 'grus bskyed de 'dus byas mi rtag pa'i gnas tshul bsgom pa ste/ 'di gsum yang gang zag tha ma'i khrid
tshul dang po'o/ /gnyis pas gnyis pa/ gsum pas gsum pa ste/ gsum po re re yang khrid tshul re re yin la/ de yang dang po gnyis ni thabs kyi phyogs kyi nyams len yin la/ gsum
pa ni nyan thos lugs kyi shes rab kyi phyogs te bsgom pa de mthar phyin pas 'dus byas mi rtag pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa zhi bar rtogs pa'i phyir ro/ ji skad du/
kye ma 'dus byas rnams mi rtag /skye zhing 'jigs pa'i chos can yin/ /skyes nas 'jig par 'gyur pas te/ /de bas nye bar zhi ba bde/ /zhes bshad pa ltar ro/ /'di lam 'bras dang
'brel pa can du bsgom pas yas bcal na zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa'o/ /yang theg pa chen po thun mong ba la byams pa tsam bsgom pas gzhan bde ba tsam 'dod pa'i blo skye/
snying rje bsgom pas sdug bsngal dang bral ba/ byang sems bsgom pa la

kun rdzob byang sems kyi sdug bsngal thams cad spong zhing bde ba dang ldan pa'i gnas sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob 'dod kyi blo bcos min skye zhing / 'di la yang gang zag
gsum gyi khrid tshul gsum ste/ gsum ka yang thabs kyi phyogs kyi khrid tshul gtso che'o/ /gnyis pa 'khor 'das dbyer med la bslab pa la yang / chos thams cad sems su bsgrub
pas rnal 'byor spyod pa'i dbu ma tsam/ de sgyu mar bsgrub pas sgyu ma lta bu'i dbu ma pa/ de spros bral du thag bcad pas rab tu mi gnas pa'i dbu ma pa'i lta ba'i khrid
tshul ste/ de la dbu ma dang mthun par dpe brgyad dam bcu gnyis kyis dkri ste gsum po re re yang lta ba'i khrid tshul re re yin no/ /'di yan theg pa thun mong ba'i khrid
tshul gnyis su byas pa'i gnyis po re re la yang lam yongs rdzogs kyi khrid tshul re re tshang bar yod do/ /'dir 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi khrid tshul ni dbang gi ye shes
dang sbyar nas ston pa ma yin gyi/ dbu ma dang mthun par thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs dpyod pa'i lta ba'i dkri tshul lo/ /gsum pa thun mong ma yin pa rnal 'byor chen po la gang
zag rigs gsum so so'i 'jug pa dkri na/ thabs kyi phyogs dang / shes rab kyi phyogs dang / zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa gsum mo/ /dang po la yang tha ma tshogs tsam bsog
pa/ 'bring las tshogs bsgrub pa/ rab bskyed rim bsgom pa'o/ /gnyis pa shes rab kyi phyogs la gsum/ tha ma lta ba tsam la blo gnas pa/ 'bring bskyed rim la sems 'dzin par
'dod pa/ rab rlung gi rnal 'byor bsgom pa'o/ /gsum pa

zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa la gsum/ dang po bzlas brjod dang sbyin sreg gi rgyud sbyangs/ 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag rab man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig gi lam khrid/ de
la tha ma bzlas brjod sbyin sreg gi rgyud sbyang ba ni bsnyen pa ji tsam song ba'i bcu cha'i sbyin sreg byed/ 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag pa ni/ rgyu dus kyi lta ba'i
dpe sum cu so bdun gyi khrid byed/ rab man ngag gi gnad bcu gcig ni/ sbyang ba khyad par can nas brtsams te sems kyi rba rlabs yan chad 'jig rten pa'i lam la gnad dgu/
'das pa'i lam la gnad bcu gcig gi dkri'o zhes gsungs pas/ thun mong ma yin pa'i rnal 'byor chen po'i lam gyi dkri tshul la/ gang zag gsum gyi dkri tshul dang po gnyis la
gsum gsum ste drug dang / gsum pa zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa la khrid tshul gsum yod pa'i/ dang po ni/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin dkri ba'i khrid yig las/ de yang bskyed pa'i
rim pa la brten nas bsnyen pa bzhi 'bum la sogs pa ci 'grub bzla zhes pa nas/ snang ba dkyil 'khor du gsal bar 'dod na gsal bar gyur ba'i bar du bskyangs so zhes pa'i
bar de khrid tshul gcig go /yang 'bring de kho na nyid la blo bzhag pa'i khrid tshul ni/ kha cig snang ba gsum gyi khrid bor te lta ba nas skyong ba yang yod do/ /zhes pa
nas lta ba rang byung gi ye shes skye bar 'gyur bas rgyu la nan tan du bya'o/ /zhes pa'i bar gyi zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa'i khrid tshul gnyis pa'o/ /gsum pa ni/ yang gang
zag gi rigs kha cig sngar bstan pa'i khrid thams cad lo gcig tsam gyi sbyangs nas/ zhes

pa nas/ 'di ni brtson 'grus mchog gi 'jug pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /zhes pa'i bar de zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa rab kyi khrid tshul lo/ /de ltar na gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du
dkri ba'i gzhung shing nyid kyi nang du zung 'jug gi rnal 'byor pa'i khrid tshul gsum ka bstan cing / nyan thos dang thun mong ba dang / theg pa chen po thun mong ba'i dkri
tshul drug ni yig chung 'di nyid du tho yig tsam bstan pa yin la/ gang zag mchog gi 'jug pa ma gtogs pa dkri tshul gyi lam gzhan rnams ni lam gyi phyogs re tsam gyi dkri
lugs yin gyi/ sa bcu gnyis pa'i bar gyi lam yongs rdzogs ni gnad bcu gcig gi dkri tshul la ma ltos par gzhan gyis dkri bar mi nus so/ /zhes pa ni dgongs pa mthar thug
pa'o/ /glegs bam phal che bar/ 'di la yig chung logs su mi 'byung ba yang gzhung shing dang po'i mjug tu/ gang zag gsum gyi khrid tshul gsum ka bstan pa 'di la yang dgongs
pa yin nam snyam mo/ /gang ltar yang dbang po rab 'bring tha gsum gyi khrid 'di ni gang zag gi bsam pa shes pa'i rdo rje slob dpon zhig gi slob ma so so la khrid tshul
gang gi sgo nas kyang lam gyi phyogs re la dkri ba dang / yongs rdzogs la khrid byas pas chog go zhes ston pa'o/ /yang sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i khrid kyi dkar chag gi yi ge
ni/ rje a nanda'i gsung rab gang gi nang na yang the tshom gyi dpyad gzhi mdzad pa cung zad tsam yang mi snang zhing / zin bris 'ga' zhig gi nang du gsung bgros yin zer
nas dpyad gzhi byas pa yang yod srid kyang / de dag la blo gtad thub pa ci

yang med cing / sgo rum dpe khang na bzhugs pa'i sa paN gyi bka' 'bum rgya shog la bris pa'i gser rkyang ma rnying pa gcig yod pa dang / 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam bla
brang bzhi thog na bzhugs pa'i gser ma la yang 'di nyid bzhugs la/ gdung brgyud rtse gdong pa rnams kyi bka' 'bum gser dngul ma rnying pa la yang 'di nyid bzhugs shing
/ rje btsun a nandas mdzad pa'i gsan yig thos pa rgya mtsho las kyang / khrid kyi dkar chag gi brgyud pa ni/ sa skya paNDi ta/ shab pa lung phu ba/ kras lung pa nam mkha'
bsod nams mkhas btsun/ gzhon nu grub/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ des rje btsun kun dga' bzang po
rnams la brgyud pa dngos su yang bshad do/ des na bdag ni 'grel pa mu tig gi phreng bar/ rgyal ba'i gsung la ma gsungs dang / /ma gsungs pa la de gsungs smra/ /'gro mchog
mi bslu sangs rgyas la/ /gnyis ka'ang gzhogs 'chas byed dang mtshungs/ /zhes bshad pa'i don yid la byed do/ /'dir smras pa/ gsung rab rgya mtsho'i 'jug ngogs la zhugs
pa'i/ /sngon gyi mkhas rnams bzhed pa'i tshul chen po/ /rdzogs ldan sprin bzhin 'dod dgu'i 'byung gnas la/ /ngan rtog rlung dmar g.yo ba ga la rigs/ /rtsod dus khengs ldan
chang gis myos pa yi/ /glang chen 'gram par chags pa'i rngul dag gis/ /nag por byas pa'i ngan rtog ri mo la'ang / /legs bshad sbrang rtsi'i ro mchog ga la yod/ /rnam dag
tshul khrims brtul zhugs mchog dag gis/

/mtshan dpe'i ri mo ci yang rab gsal zhing / /tshangs dbyangs sgrog pa 'chi med rnga sgra'i gsung / /zab yang thugs kyi shes bya kun mkhyen 'di/ /bla ma'i bla ma las kyang
ches mtho ba'i/ /yon tan kun gyi bang mdzod 'dzin byed cing / /rgyal ba'i bstan pa yun ring 'dzin byed na/ /'di la klan ka'i tshogs mang ci zhig bya/ /yongs rdzogs bstan
pa'i khur chen 'dzin byed cing / /nyes mang 'dam bu'i tshal brgya 'joms byed pa/ /blo ldan spos kyi glang chen bgrod pa'i shul/ /grong pa'i ma skyes gzhon nus ga la bsnyogs/
/gdong lnga ldan pa'i smra ba'i seng ge yi/ /lta ngan ri dwags mtha' dag skrag mdzad la/ /lung rigs gad rgyang sa gsum 'dar byed pa/ /'di la wa skyes gzhon nus brgal
thabs ci/ /de ltar bla ma dam pa'i yon tan la/ /gzhi med skur pa 'debs pa'i log rtog tshogs/ /mun par gyur rnams bdag gis bsal byas pas/ /'chi ba med pa'i lam kun snang bar
shog /ces pa'i rab tu byed pa cung zad tsam 'di 'ga' zhig gis rje btsun gong ma bkar bsgrub kyi ming btags nas rgyal ba gnyis pa kun dga' bzang po'i gsung rab la gzhi
med kyi skur pa 'debs pa du ma byas 'dug pa rnams la/ dug la rma bya'i phyogs bzhin cung zad tsam gsal bar byas pa 'di'ang / dge slong bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung
gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos shel dkar gtsug rgyan zhes bya ba'i ri bo'i rtse mor bris te/ phyogs su dri bzhon la springs pa'o/ /gzhan 'phags pa bkar bsgrub pa la sogs
pa mang du yod par grags

kyang rnam dpyod kyi nus pa dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen so so rnams kyi skabs su babs pa'i lan mdzad pa rnams las shes par 'gyur bas 'dir 'di tsam las ma bris so/ /zhes
pa de rnams kyi zhar las 'ong ba'i legs bshad kyi cha 'ga' zhig bshad pa bstan zin nas// ! //da ni 'phros don cung zad brjod par bya ste/ de yang gong du bshad pa'i
dogs dpyod de rnams gtso bor gyur pa la nye bar mkho ba'i dris lan/ gong du bshad ma thag pa'i rtsod spong gi yi ge ma rig mun sel zhes bya ba de nyid mdzad pa'i gong rol
tsam du mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub nyid kyis rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal la dri lan du gnang ba'i gsung rab ngo mtshar can las 'di ltar 'byung
ste/ ! /na mo gu ru/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma brgyud pa dang bcas pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gi mkhyen pa nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis/ /shes bya'i gnas kun gsal bar rab ston
la/ /phyi nang rten 'brel ma lus thugs chud pa'i/ /bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi mdzad pa dang / /mthun par chos kyi gnad rnams
dris pa'i lan/ /rang gi blo yis ji ltar rtogs pa tsam/ /nyung zhing go sla'i ngag gis cung zad 'bul/ /bshes gnyen dam pa khyed kyi dris pa'i lan dang po ni/ bden pa gnyis
ngo bo gcig la ldog pa tha dad yin pa thub pa dgongs gsal dang / ljon shing sogs las gsungs pa ni/ gtan nas yod pa ma yin te/ thub pa dgongs gsal las/ ngo bo gcig yin
na don dam pa la ngo bo grub par thal ba

dang / gcig pa bkag pa yin na don dam dngos med du thal ba'i skyon yod do zhes gsungs pa ni/ ngo bo grub par 'dod pa dang / don dam dngos med du 'dod na skyon de yod mod kyi/
'bum las/ mtshan nyid med par mtshan nyid gcig pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / sha ri'i bu sems med pa la yod pa'am/ med pa dmigs su yod dam zhes bya ba dang / sdud pa las/
yod dang med pa 'di gnyis med pa'i chos yin te/ zhes gsungs pa dang / rnam 'gres las/ dngos med ngo bo yod min pas/ /ngo bo med pa dpyad bya nyid/ /ma yin sgra ni de dag
nyid/ /rnam rtsod brjod par byed pa grub/ /zhes gsungs pa 'di gzhan sel gyi sgo nas legs par 'chad shes na skyon med mod/ ma shes na sngar gyi skyon de dag spang bar mi
nus so/ /des na rang gi lugs la/ don dam pa dang / tha snyad pa'i rnam gzhag gnyis las/ dang po ni/ gcig dang tha dad kyi spros pa dang bral ba yin te/ mdo dgongs pa nges
'grel las/ kun rdzob khams dang don dam de bzhin nyid/ /gcig dang tha dad bral ba'i mtshan nyid de/ /gcig dang tha dad nyid du gang rtog pa/ /de dag tshul min lta la zhugs
pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /gnyis pa tha snyad pa'i rnam gzhag ni/ gzhan sel gyi ngor/ ngo bo dbyer med ldog pa tha dad ces bya pa'am/ de nyid dang gzhan du brjod
du med pa zhes bya ba gsungs pa de kho na khas blangs so/ /zhes gsungs shing / ljon shing las/ gcig pa'i phyogs tha dad gtan med la'ang bzhi/ kun rdzob bzhin don dam
sgrib

pa'i dmigs par thal ba dang / kun rdzob ltar don dam mthong thos las btsal du yod par thal ba dang / kun rdzob mthong ba na don dam mthong bar thal ba dang / don dam ltar kun
rdzob la dbye ba med par thal ba'o/ /'og ma gnyis 'dir mi 'jug ste/ de yang rgyud las/ 'khor ba spangs nas gzhan du ni/ /mya ngan 'das pa rtogs mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs
te/ yul gcig nyid la blo'i 'jug pa tha dad do/ /de'i dpe dbu ma 'jug pa las/ rab rib mthu yis skra shad la sogs pa'i/ /ngo bo log pa gang zhig rnam rtogs pa/ /de nyid bdag
nyid gang gi mig dag pas/ /mthong ba de nyid de bzhin 'dir shes gyis/ /zhes so/ /zhes gsungs pa 'di tsam zhig yod la/ de'i don ni/ yul gcig gi thog tu snang ba'i cha nas
kun rdzob dang / de nyid rang bzhin med par shes pa'i cha nas don dam zhes tha snyad 'dogs kyi/ kun rdzob snang ba'i cha de las rang bzhin med pa logs su dbyer med pas/
de tsam la ngo bo dbyer med ces bya zhing / de tsam la gcig pa'i tha snyad btags pa ni 'gal ba yang med de/ gcig gi chos nyid gang yin pa/ /de ni kun gyi chos nyid yin/
/zhes dang / dngos gcig dngos po kun gyi ngo bo nyid/ /ces sogs dang / rgyud las/ gcig ni lhan cig med pa'o/ /zhes dang / gcig pu gnyis su med pa de/ /mtha' med rnam pas
yang dag gnas/ /zhes pa'i tshig sbyor bshad pa lta bu'o/ /cha dge sogs bden gnyis ngo bo gcig tu bzhed pa yin gsungs nas/ de la mkhas mchog smra seng gis skyon brjod mdzad
pa la/ dge ldan pa'i

lugs de la ni/ don gyi thog nas dgag pa legs par song ba yin/ slob dpon cha pa chen po de ltar bzhed pa'i nges pa med dam snyam pa/ gcig dang po rgyal sras 'jug ngogs mthong
ba'i dus su byung ba yin te/ da lta dpe ma brnyed pas gsal bar zhu rgyu ma mchis/ spyir ngo bo dang rang bzhin la sogs pa chos de dang de'i rang ldog tsam la bshad pa shin
tu mang po zhig 'byung bas/ dngos po dang yod pa'i sgra 'jug tshul ltar skabs thob kyis gang la gang 'jug shes pa gal che ste/ dper na/ gang phyir dngos kun rang bzhin
gyi/ /rang rang ngo bo la gnas phyir/ /mthun dngos gzhan gyi dngos dag las/ /ldog pa la ni rten pa can/ /zhes dang / dngos po kun la khyab pa po/ /zhes pa'i dngos po dang
/ rang bzhin rnams shes bya mtha' dag la bshad dgos pa bzhin no/ /bden gnyis kyi gnas lugs 'di dag rgyal sras lam bzang dang / rin po che'i ljon shing la da dung zhib
tu gzigs nas kun chub par zhig mdzad pa shin tu gal che lags/ dri ba gnyis pa ngo bo nyid la ngo bo nyid kyi rgya la sogs pa rigs 'chol ma yin par gzhung don rab gsal sogs
las gsal bar gsungs gda' lags pas/ de ltar na 'di la 'di'i rgyas btab na rigs 'chol du 'gyur zhes pa'i gsal kha cig ces gsungs ba'i lan ni/ ngo bo nyid la ngo bo nyid kyi
rgya la sogs pa ni rgyas btab ma 'chol ba yin la/ de dag las bzlog nas ngo bo nyid la ngo bo nyid kyi rgyas 'debs pa'i skabs su/ rgyu la 'bras bu'i rgyas 'debs lta bu
byas pa

dang / 'bras bu la rgyu'i rgyas 'debs kyi skabs su rgyu la 'bras bu'i rgyas 'debs tshul sogs byas na 'chol bar 'gro ste/ rgyas 'debs pa'i don ma 'khrul bar mtshon par nus pa
zhig yin la/ de dag gi don mtshon par mi nus pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i dper brjod ni/ gau rI dang pukka si la 'od dpag med kyi rgyas gdab byas pa lta bu'o/ /dri ba gsum pa sa
paN dkar chag tu byed pa dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum dkri ba'i khrid yig tu byed pa'i dpe sogs shes byed du byas nas/ dbang bskur gyi rjes la snang ba gsum ston par
byed pa la mi 'thad par sgrub byed mang du byed kyi gda' lags pa/ de ltar na gzhung dang po/ lung phu bas byas zer ba 'ga' zhig gda' lags pa/ de yin na lung phu ba de su
yin lags/ de min na gzhung gnyis po 'dis byas gsal ba gcig khrid rim de la chos kyi gnad bcos pa lta bu'i log rtog yin na gang zag sus byas/ de man brgyud pa chad pa lta
bur mi 'gyur lags sam/ gnad rnams min pa'i chos gzhan 'ga'/ /zhes pa ltar yin na/ gzhung gnyis gong ma'i min zer ba dang / shin tu mi rigs te zhes pa'i dgag pa rnams ji
ltar yin lags/ zhes gsungs pa'i lan la/ sa paN gyis mdzad zer ba'i dkar chag gi yi ge 'di/ sa skya'i bla brang bzhi thog na yod pa'i sa paN gyi bka' 'bum rgya shog la bris
pa'i gser ma/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa tsam gyi dus su byung ba gcig yod pa/ de'i nang du yang bris/ gzhan bka' 'bum rnying pa mang po'i nang du bcug yod cing / chos
rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pas kyang / sa

paN gyis mdzad par gsungs 'dug pa la/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang kun dga'i gsung nas/ sa paN gyis mdzad nges pa gcig yin na/ brda don gsal ba'i khrid kyi gsung tho dang / lho
pa'i zin bris sogs dang mthun par dgos rgyu yin pa la/ de dag dang mi mthun pa'i rim pa 'ga' re 'dug pas/ the tshom gyi gzhi yin gsung ba dang / de'i dpyad pa mdzad pa'i
yi ge cung zad cig kyang yod de dpe ma brnyed/ gsung bgros 'dzin pa phyi ma rnams kyang dpyad gzhir mdzad pa de ka shas che/ de la mus srad pa sogs kyi dkar chag bka' bsgrub
pa zer ba'i yi ge sogs byas nas/ sa paN gyi mdzad nges pa yin zer ba'i shes byed mang po bkod pa yod tshod 'dug kyang blta rtog byas nas ji ltar yin nges pa ma byung
zhing / 'di 'dra'i rigs can la yin min gyi shan 'byed pa shin tu dka' bar mchis/ dbang po rab 'bring gsum dkri ba'i khri yig glegs bam 'ga' zhig nang du 'byung ba'i cung
zad yi ge mang ba de'ang gong mas ma mdzad gsungs pa/ rdo rje 'chang gi mdzad pa'i dkar chag gsal byed kyi yi ger bshad yod la/ sa paN gyi khrid yig dang / khrid yig phyi
ma 'di gnyis la rten nas snang ba gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur byed pa rnams ni/ gdul bya la ltos pa'i lam dkri lugs kyi babs dang ye mi mthun pas/ rang re'i bla ma gong
ma rnams kyi dgag pa mang du mdzad pa dgongs pa'i yul du sngar nas gsal bar yod mchis bas/ da lan rgyas par ma zhus/ 'on kyang da lta snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur
byed pa yang dang po'i dus kyi lam

'bras pa rnams kyi sngar dbang gis smin pa zhig la lam 'bras kyi khrid ston pa'i tshe dbang bskur de khrid kyi sngon 'gro'i rgyu dus kyi dbang min kyang / slob dpon rang nyid
las kyai rdo rje'i dbang bskur re thob par byas nas de dang 'brel ba'i khrid ston pa la ma bu sgrigs pa'i lugs su byas nas/ de 'dra'i gang zag la rgyud gsum man chad kyis
dkris pas chog kyang / khrid kyi kha tshang ba'i phyir snang gsum nas ston pa mang po zhig byung zhing / de 'dra'i sgo nas khrid byed pa la 'gal ba yod pa ma yin yang
/ skal dman rim gyis pa'i dkri tshul la bsam nas tshogs pa shin tu mang ba la de ltar byed pa ni gang dang yang mi mthun nam snyam lags/ khrid yig gnyis po de sus mdzad
pa dang / lung phu pa de gang du byung sogs kyi zhib cha ni 'bul rgyu ma mchis/ dri ba bzhi pa lam skor phyi ma brgyad la khrid ston pa'i tshe/ sngon du dbang mi bskur ba
dang / lam 'bras la nges par dbang dgos pa'i khyad par ji ltar yin lags/ phyi ma brgyad kyi Dombhi ba/ mtsho skyes kyi nag po mtsho skyes kyi nas gling ma/ nag po pa'i nag
po dkyil chog ces bri dgos/ lam bslong rnams ma yin pa'i smin byed 'di yin zhes pa'i ngos 'dzin gsal ba cig gsal ba med na smin byed dgos tsa na gang gis byed lags/ rgyud
lta bu la gang yin pa'i dbang bskur gcig thob nas de'i rigs nyams su len du rung ba yin na/ bo dong bas rgyud sde bzhi po gang rung gi smin byed re thob nas de dang de'i
rigs nyams su len du rung bar 'dod pa la/ phag mo sngon 'byung sogs kyi lung drangs nas dgag pa mdzad pa tshur mi ldog lags

sam/ zhes pa'i lan ni/ lam bskor phyi ma brgyad po 'di yang rten sa'i rgyud gang dang gang yin pa de dang de'i dbang gi smin par byas pa dgos pas/ bsam mi khyab la sambu Ti'i
dbang ngam/ kyai rdo rje 'grel pa lugs kyi dbang gang rung dgos/ sa paN gyis 'grel pa lugs mdzad par bshad/ mtsho skyes la ni de nyid kyi dbang / lhan cig skyes grub la
'grel pa lugs/ gtum mo lam rdzogs dang yon po srong ba la 'khor lo bde mchog dang gsang ba 'dus pa gang rung / mchod rten drung thob la gsang ba 'dus pa/ yi ge med pa la
gsang ba 'dus pa dang rdo rje bdag med ma gang rung / dbang yon tan rim pa la gsang ba 'dus pa rnams dang po'i dus kyi lam bskor brgyad kyi smin byed yin no zhes rje btsun
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' dbang phyug gsung gin 'dug lags/ da lta'i dus kyi ston pa po rnams kyi ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni spobs par mi nus lags/ ding sang gi dus su
ni dbang de dag thob nas khrid de dag nyan pa po rnams la yang dbang de rnams smin byed du 'gro ba'i nges pa mi snang ste/ sngar nas dbang bskur gzhan gyis smin par byas
pa la khrid de dag ston pa shas che ba'i phyir ro/ /dri ba lnga pa bde gshegs snying po/ rang bzhin gnas rigs/ kun gzhi rgyu rgyud rnams ming gi rnam grangs lta bur mkhas
mchog smra seng gis gsungs gda' lags pa/ de ltar ma yin na/ lang gshegs stug po bkod pa dang / /rnal 'byor dbang phyug man ngag dang / dpal ldan zla ba'i zhabs sogs kyis/
/kun gzhi'i sgra yang 'di la bzhed/ /ces

pa'i gzhung gi don ji ltar yin lags/ de gsum ming gi rnam grangs yin na/ rgyu rgyud sbyang gzhi yin tsa na gnyis po'ang sbyang gzhir mi 'gyur lags sam zhes pa'i lan ni/ bde
gshegs snying po dang / kun gzhi rgyu rgyud sogs ngo bo'i sgo nas mi 'dra ba'i dbye ba med pas/ de la dgongs te rje btsun chen pos/ rang sems gdod nas spros bral rgyu rgyud
dang / /dbang gi ye shes lam gyi lta ba dang / /nyams myong sangs rgyas sa dang ngo bo gcig /ces gsungs pa dang / mkhas mchog smra seng gis gsungs pa de rnams khyad par
ci yang med cing / rang gi sems yod med kyi spros pa'i mtha' thams cad dang bral ba gcig nyid ma dag pa'i dri mas sgrib pa'i gnas skabs la rgyu rgyud dang / sems spros
bral de'i spyi'i mtshan nyid kyis thams cad la khyab pa'i cha nas bde gshegs snying po dang / chos sku'i rgyu byed pas rang bzhin gnas rigs sogs su gnas skabs la ltos nas
tha snyad so sor btags kyi/ rang gi ngo bo nas sbyang rgyu med pas sbyang gzhir ji ltar 'gyur te/ mi 'gyur la/ de'i rgyu mtshan gyis/ bdag med bstod 'grel las kyang / rang
bzhin la ltos nas gnas gyur med pa dang / yon tan la ltos nas gnas gyur yod pa sogs rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi rtsa ba'i grub mtha' yin la/ sbyang gzhi rgyu rgyud sbyong
byed thabs rgyud/ sbyang 'bras sangs rgyas zhes sogs dang / rgyu'i rgyud sngon du 'gro ba rten gyi gang zag zhes pa'i tshig tsam la brten nas/ sgyu ma mkhan gyi gang
zag gi tshig gis sprul pa sna tshogs su ston pa la thugs gtad par mi mdzad 'tshal

lo/ /mdor na rgyu rgyud kyi gnas skabs sbyang gzhir 'gyur ba mang du yod pas rgyu rgyud sbyang gzhi zhes dang / rgyu rgyud kyi gnas skabs la ma dag pa'i snang ba sna tshogs
pa yod pas ma dag pa'i snang ba la rgyu rgyud du bshad pa sogs mang du yod pa rnams kyi sgra ji bzhin pa la zhen pa dang / phung po lnga'i chos nyid sbyang gzhir bshad pa
yang / chos nyid rang ngos nas sbyang gzhir mi 'gyur yang blo snang gi chos nyid de tsam la bsam nas/ phung po lnga'i chos nyid mi dmigs te zhes sogs kyi tshig sbyor gsungs
pa yin la/ chos nyid bden grub du 'dod pa rnams la ni phung po lnga'i chos nyid mi dmigs te zhes zer du mi rung bas/ tshig gi sbyor tshur snga ma de nor pa yin par khas
len dgos so/ /rgyas par mkhas mchog smra ba'i seng ge'i gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i rnam bshad la zhib tu gzigs shing dpyod par zhu/ dri ba drug pa ljon shing
las rdo rje slob dpon la las dang po pa dang / brtan pa thob pa dang / brtan pa cher thob pa rnams/ drod ma skyes pa dang / drod chung 'bring thob pa dang / drod chen po
thob pa dang / rim bzhin du sbyar ba lta bu zhig gsungs 'dug pa dang / 'khrul spong du rgyud rgya gzhung nas gsungs pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid gsungs pa rnams
las dang po pa'i dbang du byas pa yin gsungs gda' lags pa/ mdor na gang zag gsum po de'i ngos 'dzin gsal ba gcig ces gsungs pa'i lan ni/ ljon shing las/ dbang bskur thob
cing dam tshig dang sdom par ldan pa'i gang zag spyi ldog nas/ las dang po pa

dang / brtan pa thob pa dang / brtan pa cher thob pa dang gsum du 'dus par gsungs shing / de rnams rim pa bzhin du drod ma skyes pa dang / drod chung 'bring thob pa dang /
drod chen po thob pa rnams dang rim pa bzhin du sbyar ba lta bu zhig yod kyang / rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang thob nas lam thams cad rdzogs par nyams su blang du btub ste/
zhes sogs brjod nas/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid gur le'u brgyad pa nas gsungs pa thams cad legs par bshad cing / mtshan nyid de rnams yongs su rdzogs pa rdo rje slob
dpon sa thob pa rnams la ldan pa shas che shing / bla ma lnga bcu pa nas gsungs pa'i mtshan nyid rnams kyang / ding sang gi rdo rje slob dpon las dang po pa rnams la
yongs rdzogs su yod pa ni shin tu dka' zhing / rtsa ltung 'khrul spong las rgyud rgya gzhung nas gsungs pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid rnams las dang po pa la dgongs
gsung ba/ 'khrul spong nyid las/ dbang bskur byed pa la rdo rje slob dpon sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor ston nus pa la sogs pa dgos zer ba la/ rgyud sde rnams las de lta bu'i
gang zag la dgongs nas dbang bskur gyi mngon par rtogs pa sa'i cho ga la sogs pa ma bshad par/ las dang po pa'i slob dpon gyis bya dgos pa'i cho ga'i rim pa rgyas pa rnams
gsungs pas na/ sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba sogs kyi cho ga ma gsungs/ zhes pa tsam ma gtogs/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid rnams las dang po pa kho na
la sbyar ba ni mi snang ngo / /gang zag gsum gyi ngos 'dzin ting nge 'dzin bsgom

pa'i stobs kyis mnyam gzhag tu yang / de kho na nyid kyi nyams myong mtshan nyid pa ma skyes pa'i bar las dang po pa/ de nas mnyam gzhag tu de lta bu'i nyams nges par skyes
shing / rjes thob du yang snang ba khra bor 'char ba'i bar brtan pa thob pa/ chu bo rgyun gyi rnal 'byor skyes nas brtan pa chen po thob par rje btsun sa skya pa gong ma
rnams bzhed par mngon lags/ dri ba bdun pa/ gnas gsum gsal byed las/ yul chen sum cu so bdun tshang bar 'byor ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa'i dga' ba'i me tog ces bya ba'i bstan
bcos las gsungs pa sogs gsungs gda' lags pa/ 'di dri med rgyan 'grel dang mi mthun tsa na/ yul chen sum cu so bdun dang / zhes sogs kyi gzhung gi dgongs par ji ltar 'gro
lags/ gling bzhi dang gling bzhi gcig tu sdom pa dang lnga/ phyi'i yul yin na gsung rab dgongs gsal las yin par gsungs gda' lags pa dang / sbas pa'i rtsa lnga'i ngos 'dzin
gsal ba gcig kyang zhu zhes pa'i lan la/ sdom gsum gyi dri ba'i nang du/ phyi rol yul chen so bdun zhes/ /bya ba rgyud gzhung gang nas bshad/ /ces dris pa'i lan la/
phyi rol du yul chen sum cu so bdun re re nas dkyus gcig la bgrang pa gcig gis khungs ston dgos byung ba la/ 'byor pa'i dbang po dang / bde mchog stod 'grel dang / 'grel
pa gru gzings sogs las gsal bar bshad pa'i khungs drangs nas gnas gsum gsal byed du bshad pa yin la/ stod 'grel gyi nang du yul sum cu rtsa gnyis phyi nang du sbyor tshul
dang / yul sum

cu rtsa bdun byang phyogs so bdun dang sbyor ba'i tshul tsam smos nas/ phyi'i yul chen sum cu so bdun re re nas 'di ltar yin bgrang pa med cing / phyi rol du re re nas 'dren
dgos pa'i tshe na/ indra bhu ti dang / rdo rje gsang ba dang / bde mchog stod 'grel dang / gru zings sogs las gsungs pa gang rung las/ mi 'da' zhes bsam pa yin pas 'gal
ba med par sems lags/ gling bzhi dang gling bzhi gcig tu sdom pa dang lnga/ phyi rol gyi yul chen du spos khang pa'i sdom gsum gyi TIkka dang / gsung rab dgongs gsal gnyis
las/ de lnga phyi rol yul chen du gsungs 'dug kyang / de rnams nged khas mi len pa rgyu mtshan dang bcas nas gnas gsum gsal byed rang du zhib par bshad yod lags/ sbas
pa'i rtsa lnga ni/ snying kha'i dbus su ro rkyang gnyis las mdun rgyab dang / g.yas g.yon du gyes pa'i rtsa bzhi dang / sambu Ti las/ dbu ma'i g.yon phyogs su chu shing gi
snye ma lta bu zhes dbu ma nyid las gyes pa'i rtsa gcig yod par bshad pas de dang lnga po la ngos 'dzin zhes rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gsung bgros 'dzin pa'i bla
ma bgres po rnams gsung gin mchis/ rtsa lnga po de'i rtse mo'i cha la yi ge lnga yod pa ni snying kha'i nang bskor gyi rtsa yin yang yi ge'i ldog pa nas sbas pa'i rtsa
lngar tha snyad mi 'dogs zhes pa 'di tsam gcig phul/ 'di la brjod par bya ba mang du yod kyang 'di rnams nang gi zab don yin pas yi ger mang du ma bris shing mtha' dpyod
byed pa la bla ma gong ma rnams mi dgyes 'dug lags/ dri ba brgyad pa/ nyi ma nub pa dang zhes pa la

brten nas/ dbang bskur nyi ma nub pa nas nyi ma ma shar gyi bar du mdzad par gsungs pa la/ ding sang nyin par mdzad pa dang / rdo rje slob dpon la dbang stegs grangs nges dang
bcas byed par gsungs pa la/ ding sang grangs nges mi mdzad pa rnams kyi lung rigs gnang ba zhu/ zhes pa'i lan ni/ rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i dngos bstan la ji ltar yod
pa'i phyag len de rnams da lta dus kyi stobs kyis ji lta ba bzhin du mdzad pa rgya bod kyi bla ma phyi ma phal che ba gcig la yang ma byung 'dug cing / de la lung rigs kyi
shes byed gzhan 'god rgyu med kyang / bstan pa dar nub kyi babs la sogs nas/ sdom pa gsum ka'i phyag len gyi rim pa ding sang gi dus su cha mtshungs pa tsam la gtso bor
byed dgos pa yin nam snyam pa byung lags/ 'di tsam du ma zad kyi dbang bskur bya ba'i yul dang / byed pa po slob dpon dang / ji ltar bya ba'i cho ga'i gnad che sa kun tu
yang legs par dpyad na ding sang gi dus su ji ltar yod dgongs par zhu zhing / dus skabs 'di 'dra ba la dgongs nas/ sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye bar/ des na nyan thos bstan
pa ni/ /nub kyang gzugs brnyan tsam zhig snang / /rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa ni/ /gzugs brnyan tsam yang mi snang ngo / /zhes gsungs pa yin par go lags/ rdo rje slob
dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges mi mdzad pa yang slob ma'i rigs so sor mi nges shing thams cad kyang slob dpon gyi rigs yin pa'i dbang du byas nas mdzad pa ka yin mchis/ dri
ba dgu pa rjes 'dzin byas pa'i slob ma gcig sta

gon gyi dus ma sleb na skyin pa 'jug par gsungs gda' ba/ de kha yar ba'i ched yin na'ang / gnyis ma tshang na lhag ma rnams la dbang bskur du rung lags sam/ yang kha 'cham
la dbang bskur na skye la nyes byas kyi dbang du byas na rung zer ba gda' lags pa ji ltar yin/ zhes pa'i lan ni/ rjes 'dzin byas pa'i slob ma ji tsam ma tshang yang lhag
ma rnams la dbang bskur ba'i tshe/ sta gon gyi skabs su grangs nges yod pa re byas nas de dag la dbang gi dngos gzhi bskur ba shin tu yang rung zhing / slob ma rjes 'dzin
gzhan 'os pa ci rigs pa la bskyar nas byed pa'am/ slob ma rjes 'dzin ma byas pa la yang sta gon gyi cho ga byas nas dbang bskur ba byar rung zhing / rjes 'dzin byas pa'i
slob ma sta gon gyi dus su med pa la yang / yod bzhin du ma 'dzoms pa dang / shi nas med pa sogs du ma 'byung bas/ lhag ma rnams la dbang ma bskur bar lam bstan du rung
ba ni ma yin no/ /kha 'cham la dbang bskur byas na skye la nyes byas yin zer ba ni/ skye la nyes byas dang nyes med kyi tha snyad rnams 'dul ba la grags kyi/ gsang sngags
la sbyar na lham dpe zhwa la bkab pa las ma 'das lags/ dri ba bcu pa mkhas mchog smra seng ge gsung ngag bstan pa rgyas pa'i nyi 'od kyi kha skong las/ bya rgyud nas 'khor
lo sdom pa'i snang ba gsum du bsdus nas nyams su len par gsungs shing / rgyud don man ngag gis nyams su len pa'i tshe/ don la'ang dgos par gda' lags pa/ snang ba gsum
po gang gi nang du/ ji ltar 'du rgyu mtshan zhib pa cig ces pa'i lan ni/ snang ba

gsum po 'di lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyor ba dang / lam yongs rdzogs la sbyor ba'i tshul gnyis las/ dang po la yang dbang po rtul po la rgyud las ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin gso sbyong
nas bde mchog sgyu ma'i bar ther chags su dkri ba dang / snang ba dang po dkri tshul tsam sngon du song nas/ bde mchog sgyu ma'i bar la ci rigs pa la dkri ba dang /
de lta bu'i dkri tshul rgyas shing mang ba mi dgos par snang ba dang po gnyis tsam gyi nang du so so thar pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i nyams len tshang ba la
bkod nas/ de rjes kyai rdo rje brtsams pas chog pa sogs du ma yod pa las/ lam gyi gzhi bca' ba'i skabs 'dir ni snang ba gsum gyi dkri ba tsam du bsdus nas nyams su blangs
pas chog ces pa'i don yin gyi/ gzhi bca'i skabs 'dir/ sgyu ma bde mchog gi bar gyi dkri tshul thams cad snang ba gsum du bsdus nas nyams su len pa ni ma yin te/ de'i tshe
pha rol tu phyin pa rang rkang nas bshad pa'i nyams len gyi rim pa yin pas/ rgyud sde bzhi'i nyams len gyi rim pa la ma zhugs pa'i phyir ro/ /yang snang gsum lam rdzogs
la sbyar ba'i tshe ni/ ma dag pa'i snang ba nas dbang gi bar rgyu rgyud/ nyams kyi snang ba thabs rgyud/ dag pa'i snang ba 'bras rgyud du 'gyur zhing / de'i tshe ma dag
pa'i snang ba'i skabs su skyes pa'i log lta spong ba'i nyams nas brtsams te/ bde mchog sgyu ma'i bar gyi ting nge 'dzin thams cad nyams snang dang / 'bras bu sangs rgyas
kyi sa'i yon tan la yid ches khyad par can skye ba yang / nyams snang

ngam/ 'bras bu rang gi khongs su bsdus kyang chog la/ thams cad kyang / 'khor ba'i nyams la rten nas log lta spong / /lam gyi nyams kyis theg pa gcig tu bsdu/ /'bras bu'i nyams
kyis spro ba mchog tu 'gyur/ /zhes bshad pa ltar/ gzhi lam 'bras gsum gyi nyams gsum gyi nang du bsdus shing sgro 'dogs chod par byas nas nyams su blang yang chog pas
na/ mkhas mchog smra seng gis bshad pa de rnams dang / 'khor 'das thun mong ba'i lam la gzhung tshom bu bdun du bshad pa re res kyang lam yongs rdzogs re bstan ces gsungs
pa ni/ kha nang du phyogs nas nyams su len pa rnams la man ngag gi dam pa lags/ dri ba bcu gcig pa/ ljon shing las/ de bas na theg chen thun mong ma yin pa'i lta ba dang
/ spyod pa rim pa can la bslab pa'i gang zag de la/ sngags kyi rim pa kun shes nas/ /zhes sbyar te zhes pa nas/ tshe 'di nyid la thob par byed/ /ces pa'i bar gyi gzhung
'dis/ bya rgyud nas bde mchog gi bar gyi sems bskyed/ tshul khrims/ de kho na nyid/ sa dang lam gyi rim pa/ 'bras bu 'grub tshul rnams myur bul ma gtogs/ theg pa thun mong
ba dang khyad par med pa lta bu gcig gsungs gda' lags pa/ de ltar yin nam min lags pa/ yin na 'di ltar yin gyi gsal cha dang / min na gzhung de'i don ji ltar lags/ zhes
gsungs pa'i lan ni/ rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag las/ don gcig na yang ma rmong pa dang / /thabs mang dka' ba med pa dang / /dbang po rnon po'i dbang byas pas/ /sngags
kyi theg pa khyad

par 'phags/ /zhes pa'i lung drangs nas/ phar phyin dang gsang sngags gnyis rtogs bya lta bar don gcig thabs byang chub kyi sems su don gcig 'bras bu sangs rgyas su don gcig
ces bshad pa dang / 'dir gsungs pa gnyis tshul mtshungs pa lags pas/ lam gyi spyi tshul mtshungs kyang / nang tshan la khyad par yod cing / spyi 'dra ba la don mtshungs
pa lta bur bshad pa yin pas na/ ljon shing gi gzhung don ni de ltar yin zhing / nang tshan gyi khyad par ni ma rmongs pa dang / thabs mang ba dang / dka' ba med pa dang /
dbang po rnon po'i dbang du byas pa sogs spyi rnam las ji ltar bshad pa bzhin dgongs par zhu/ dri ba bcu gnyis pa/ rab gnas bzang drug 'di don gsal dang mi 'dra ba'i khyad
par gcig yong dgos pa gda' lags pa/ khyad par 'di yin zer ba'i gsal kha cig ces gsungs pa'i lan ni/ rje btsun bsod nams rtse mos kyai rdo rje'i lam gyi cha lag yongs su
rdzogs pa gzhung gcig tu bkod pa rin chen 'bar ba lta bu gcig brtsom par bzhed nas/ mngon par rtogs pa rgyas pa'i bshad par dam bca' ba'i skabs su/ sgrub thabs dkyil 'khor
sbyin sreg rab gnas rnams/ /bla ma'i phyag len mdzad bzhin 'dir bri bya/ /zhes gsungs la/ de'i nang tshan gyi rab gnas ni bzang po drug pa 'di nyid yin zhing / tshogs
'khor gyi cho ga ni dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang 'brel bas de'i khongs su 'dus par dgongs nas logs su ma mdzad cing / 'on kyang de'i phyag len gyi rim pa ni/ rje btsun chen
pos mdzad pa'i tshogs

'khor 'bring po nyid yin no/ rab gnas bzang po drug pa 'di ni kyai rdo rje'i rgyud kyi dngos bstan gyi rab tu gnas pa yin la/ rab tu gnas pa'i rgyud/ gzhung bdun lo tsA ba
chen po rin chen bzang po'i sdom tshig dang bcas pa 'di ni rgyud sde bzhir phye ba'i tshe na/ rgyud rang gi ngo bo rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du bzhed cing / cho ga'i phyag len
gyi rim pa ni rgyud sde gong ma rnams la'ang sbyar du rung zhing / phyag len la yang mdzad pas na bzang po drug pa'i lugs ltar du kyai rdo rje la rten nas don gsal gyi lugs
dang mthun par cho ga mdzad pa 'di'i cho ga rang la ni/ bzang drug dang don gyi thog nas khyad par chen po mi 'dra ba 'di yin gyi gsal cha ni 'bul rgyu ma mchis/ dri
ba bcu gsum pa/ sras don ma sogs su bskyed rdzogs bsgom pa la rten nas ting 'dzin ma skyes na/ tshogs rang rkyang du shor ba yin pas pha rol tu phyin pa dang khyad par med
gsungs/ de gnyis bsgom pa la rten nas drod skyes na rnal 'byor pa'i lam sna 'di nas zin zhes pa dang / dri med rgyan 'grel las/ lung sgo bstun gyi dbang du byas na/ drod
gsum po de tshogs lam/ sbyor lam/ mthong lam gsum la rim pa bzhin du bzhog pa lta bur gsungs gda' lags pa/ des na rnal 'byor pa'i lam sna 'di nas zin zhes pa'i lam de lam
lnga'i dang po la 'jog pa yin nam bsam lags/ ji ltar lags gsal ba cig yang man ngag las/ drod gsum po de nyams bco lnga'i nang tshan gyi drod gsum la 'jog pa lta bur gsungs
gda' lags pa/ de ltar na nyams lhag ma rnams kyang drod gsum du 'dus pa lta bur mi

'gyur lags sam/ rgyud nas gsungs pa'i drod gsum dang / man ngag gi drod gsum rgyud don man ngag gi nyams su len pa'i tshe 'jig rten pa'i lam du 'jog pa 'di gong ma'i dgongs
pa yin gsungs pa 'dra gda' lags pa ji ltar lags gsal ba zhig thugs rje chen po'i bka' drin gyis bskyang du gsol/ zhes gsungs pa'i lan ni/ man ngag las gsungs pa'i drod gsum
gyi nang du drod thams cad 'dus par sras don ma las bshad de/ de nyid las khams 'dus pa gsum1 gyis drod gsum du bzhag pa dang / skye sla ba dang / skye dka' ba dang /
skye shin tu dka' ba gsum gyis drod gsum2 du bzhag pa dang / yul rkyen gyi gnod pa dang / phan gnod med pa dang / yul rkyen gyis rtogs pa ye shes kyi grogs byed pa'i sgo
nas drod che 'bring chung gsum3 du bzhag pa dang / chos brgyad kyi rtog pa rags rim 'gags pa dang / tshar bcad rjes bzung gang rung nus pa dang / tshar bcad rjes bzung gnyis
ka mnyam par grub pa'i sgo nas drod gsum4 du bzhag pa dang / phung po lnga dul zhing ye shes kyi 'gro ldog byed pa dang / rgyu dus kyi 'bras bu bzhi thob pa dang / grub
mtha' dang po la 'char ba'i 'bras bu bzhi mngon du gyur pa'i sgo nas drod gsum5 du bzhag pa ste 'jog tshul lnga gsungs shing / dmar ma'i mchan bu dkar gyis btab pa las
kyang / de ltar du 'byung bas 'di rnams kyi drod gsum gyi 'jog tshul phyi ma gnyis po de'i nang du rgyud nas gsungs pa'i drod che 'bring chung gsum yang 'du ba lags shing
/ 'on kyang man ngag gi

nang du drod gsum po de gtso che bar 'jig rten pa'i lam dang sbyar nas gsungs shing / che 'bring chung gsum yang rim pa yin min du skye bar gsungs la/ rgyud kyi skabs su spyod
pa dang mtshams sbyor ba'i skabs yin pas chung 'bring che gsum rim can du skye bar spyod pa'i go rim gyis gsal bar grub pa lags/ yang rgyud kyi nang du spyod pa'i skabs
kyi drod chung 'bring gnyis dngos su gsungs pa de'i shugs la man ngag tu gsungs pa'i drod rnams kyang thon pas na/ dngos shugs kyi sgo nas rgyud las bshad pa'i drod gsum
du yang man ngag gi drod gsum 'dus shing / de ltar ma yin na lung dang sbyor rgyu mi yong ngam snyam/ rnal 'byor pa'i lam sna gang nas zin pa ni/ gzhung bshad dmar ma
las/ mnyam gzhag la zhi gnas/ lhag mthong dang zung 'brel gyi nyams thun gcig la sogs pa dus 'da' 'am/ rjes spyod la phyi'i yul rkyen gyis mi gnod de/ shin tu brtan pa ni/
khams 'dus pa dang po'i lam sna zin pa yin te/ sbyor lam drod chung ngu'i ye shes so zhes gsungs pas/ tshogs drod 'byor ba'i ting nge 'dzin brtan pa gcig la gsungs shing
/ 'di pa'i lugs kyi tshogs sbyor spel mar skye bas/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i lugs kyi tshogs lam dang 'jog lugs mi 'dra zhing / rang lugs kyi tshogs lam 'dis kyang lam lnga'i
nang tshan gyi tshogs lam gyi go chod par ni khas blangs pas chog pa'i rigs su mchis/ zhes ji ltar dri ba mdzad pa rnams kyi lan rang gis go tshod tsam phul ba yin zhing
/ bla ma gong ma sangs rgyas dang 'dra ba rnams kyi gsung rab 'di

rnams kyang tshig brling zhing don rgya che la yun ring por dpyad cing / gsung rab gnad kyi go yul thams cad nas blang zhing / rang gi yid la shar tshod kyi go yul snga ma
rnams dang / grags tshod kyi chos skad ci rigs pa rnams dang yang ma 'dres par byas nas dpyad pa shin tu dag pa dang / rje btsun gong ma de rnams la dad pa chen po'i kun
nas blangs te dgongs pa len dgos par 'dug pa la/ lhag bsam rnam par dag pa 'di lta bu'i sgo nas dri ba mdzad pa ni shin tu rjes su yi rang lags shing / da dung yang rje btsun
gong ma'i gsung rab 'di rnams gting dpag par dka' ba yin pas gzhan la 'chad pa dang / rang gi nyams su len pa la sogs pa thabs tshul du ma'i sgo nas bstan pa'i 'khur
bzhes su gsol/ zhes bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung rab kyi don la blo gros kyi snang ba shin tu rgyas shing / nges don gyi nyams len mthar phyin par mdzad pa'i yongs kyi
dge ba'i bshes gnyen dam pa blo gros rab gsal gyis dri ba mdzad pa'i lan/ rang gi cung zad tsam go yul du shar ba 'di ltar yin nam bsam ste mdor bsdus pa tsam phul ba 'di
ni/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung rab la yid ches cung zad tsam brnyed pa'i dge slong bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang pos/ du ru ka'i dmag gi 'jigs pas nyen te/ bas mtha'i dgon pa zhig tu gnas pa'i tshe bris te phul ba'o/ /dus mthar chos min sna tshogs kyi/ /'jig pas nyen pa'i g.yang
sa dang / /lta ngan mun pa mi zad pa'i/

/lam gyi gegs las thar bar shog /mangga laM bha wantu/ zhes pa de rnams kyi 'phros don cung zad brjod pa bshad zin nas/ de dag gis ni bstan bcos chen po lugs gnyis gsal ba'i
nyin byed ma tshang ba med par bstan zin to// //'dir smras pa/ rgyud sde bye ba'i gsang mdzod kun gyi bdag /'khrul med sa skya'i rje btsun mchog rnams kyi/ /gsang sngags
zab mo'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzogs gnyis/ /zhes grags dam pa'i skyes chen rnams la 'dud/ /sngon tshe mang thos dpyod ldan blo gsal rnams/ /gong ma'i gsung rab 'chad nyan
sgrub pas brel/ /deng sang dpyod ldan skyes bur rlom rnams kyang / /don med 'dir snang bya bas mi tshe skyel/ /de phyir bdag blo brtson pa'i ded dpon gyis/ /yongs 'dzin mkhas
pa'i gru la rten byas te/ /gsung rab rgya mtsho chen por legs zhugs nas/ /legs bshad rin chen len la brtson par gyur/ /ding sang 'di na col chung blun po 'ga'/ /sangs
rgyas bstan pa 'dzin pa'i skyes bu las/ /gang dran lag len grol bar rlom pa dag /mtshar du 'dzin pa'i rmongs pa 'ga' med dam/ /de lta na yang rang nyid bstan 'gro'i don/
/rlabs chen bsgrub phyir 'di phyi'i don mtha' dag /yid la re ba ji bzhin kun 'grub par/ /bla mar gsol 'debs kho bo'i dge sbyor legs/ /tshad ldan sa skya'i rje btsun grub
mtha'i srol/ /cung zad 'dra min rjes 'jug mkhas pa yis/ /so sor bshad pa'i legs bshad 'di ltos dang / /lugs gnyis bzhed srol mtha' dag rtogs par 'gyur/ /'di sbyar dge bas
bdag cag dpon slob

rnams/ /dus 'dir tshe ring nad med bsam don 'grub/ /bstan pa cher rgyas don gnyis mthar phyin nas/ /phyi ma lhan cig bde ba can bgrod shog /ces dpal ldan sa skya pa'i sngags
phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin ngor rdzogs rnam gnyis kyi kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi phyag len gyi rim pa gtso bor gyur pa'i zab mo'i gnad 'ga' zhig la bzhed tshul mi 'dra
ba'i grub mtha'i rnam gzhag mdo tsam bshad pa lugs gnyis gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di yang / rigs ldan chos kyi rgyal po grub pa'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs
bsod nams dbang po dang / rgyal sras sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ rigs thams cad dang dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang
chen po nyid gzhan ngor ngur smr-ig gi bla gos 'chang ba rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan rnams gtso bor smos pa'i yongs 'dzin bslu med du ma'i zhabs
rdul spyi bos len pa shrI sa skya pa shAkya'i dge bsnyen paNDi ta mkhas pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ bod yul bstan
pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos kyai rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi phyag len gyi rim pa gtso bor gyur pa'i zab mo'i gnad 'ga' zhig la mkhas pa'i dbang po ngor
rdzong rnam gnyis kyi grub mtha'i bzhed srol mi 'dra ba du ma snang ba'i legs bshad rnams rang dang skal ba mnyam pa'i blo gsal rnams 'jug pa bde ba'i phyir phyogs gcig
tu sdebs te sa mo sbrul gyi lo zla ba gsum pa'i dmar cha'i tshes la dpal sa

skya'i bzhi thog bla brang gi 'od gsal snang bar grub par bgyis pa'i yi ge pa ni shab stod pa bkra shis don grub dang / sa skyar skyes pa'i bsam 'grub kyis bgyis so/ /'dis
kyang bstan pa spyi dang / bye brag tu gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas pa'i rgyur gyur cig/ //mangga laM// // ! mkhan chen a pad rin
po che'i dgongs bzhed ltar gu rus zhabs zhu bgyis pa'o/
